Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - State System of Higher Education
==================================================================

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 1 - Governance, Powers, Rights, and Responsibilities
**********************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5 Definitions.
----------------------------------------------
As used in this title:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(1)(a): "Academic education" means an educational program that is offered by a degree-granting institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(1)(b): "Academic education" does not include technical education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(2): 53B-1-402 "Board" means the Utah Board of Higher Education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(3): "Career and technical education" means an educational program that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(3)(a): is designed to meet industry needs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(3)(b): leads to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(3)(b)(i): a certificate; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(3)(b)(ii): a degree; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(3)(c): may qualify for funding under the Carl D. Perkins Career and Technical Education Improvement Act of 2006, 20 U.S.C. 2301 et seq.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(4): 53B-1-408 "Commissioner" means the commissioner of higher education appointed in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(5): 53B-1-102(1)(a) "Degree-granting institution of higher education" or "degree-granting institution" means an institution of higher education described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(6): 53B-2-103; 53B-2a-108 "Institution board of trustees" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(6)(a): 53B-2-103 an institution of higher education board of trustees described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(6)(b): 53B-2a-108 a technical college board of trustees described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(7): 53B-1-102(1)(b) "Technical college" means an institution of higher education described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(8): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(8)(a): "Technical education" means career and technical education that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(8)(a)(i): leads to a certificate; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(8)(a)(ii): is short-term training.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.5(8)(b): "Technical education" does not include general education.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-101.8 Health insurance mandates.
------------------------------------------------------------
An institution of higher education shall include in a health plan it offers to its employees insurance mandates in accordance with Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102 Utah system of higher education.
----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1): The Utah system of higher education consists of the following institutions:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a): degree-granting institutions, which are:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(i): the University of Utah;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(ii): Utah State University;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(iii): Weber State University;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(iv): Southern Utah University;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(v): Snow College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(vi): Utah Tech University;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(vii): Utah Valley University; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(a)(viii): Salt Lake Community College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b): technical colleges, which are:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(i): Bridgerland Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(ii): Davis Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(iii): Dixie Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(iv): Mountainland Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(v): Ogden-Weber Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(vi): Southwest Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(vii): Tooele Technical College; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(b)(viii): Uintah Basin Technical College;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(c): the Utah Board of Higher Education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(1)(d): other public post-high school educational institutions as the Legislature may designate.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(2): A change in the name of an institution within the Utah system of higher education is not a change in the role or mission of the institution, unless otherwise authorized by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(3): It is not the intent of the Legislature to increase the number of research universities in the state beyond the University of Utah and Utah State University.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-102(4): (1) An institution or board described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-108 Board succeeds to rights and duties of predecessor board and council.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The board is the successor to and is vested with all rights, duties, obligations, and liabilities to which its predecessor governing boards and the Coordinating Council of Higher Education were subject, except as otherwise provided by law.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109 Coordination of higher education and public education information technology systems -- Use of unique student identifier.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(1): 53B-33-201; 53B-1-102; 53E-4-308 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(1)(a): 53B-33-201 "Center" means the Utah Data Research Center created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(1)(b): 53B-1-102 "Institution of higher education" means an institution of higher education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(1)(c): 53E-4-308 "Unique student identifier" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(2): 53E-4-308 The board and State Board of Education, in collaboration with the center, shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(2)(a): 53E-4-308 coordinate public education and higher education information technology systems to allow individual student academic achievement to be tracked through both education systems in accordance with this section and Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(2)(b): coordinate access to the unique student identifier of a public education student who later attends an institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-109(3): Information technology systems used at an institution of higher education shall use the unique student identifier of all students who have previously been assigned a unique student identifier.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110 Criminal background checks of prospective and existing employees of higher education institutions -- Institutions to adopt policy.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(1): 53B-1-102 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(1)(a): 53B-1-102 "Institution" means an institution listed in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(1)(b): "Minor" means a person younger than 21 years old.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(2): An institution shall adopt a policy providing for criminal background checks of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(2)(a): prospective employees of institutions; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(2)(b): existing employees of institutions, where reasonable cause exists.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3)(a): The policy shall require that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3)(a)(i): an applicant for any position that involves significant contact with minors or any position considered to be security sensitive by an institution or its designee shall submit to a criminal background check as a condition of employment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3)(a)(ii): an existing employee submit to a criminal background check, where reasonable cause exists.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3)(b): Subsection (3)(a)(i) does not apply to adjunct faculty positions.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3)(c): The policy may allow or require applicants for positions other than those described in Subsection (3)(a)(i) to submit to a criminal background check as a condition of employment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(3)(d): The policy may allow criminal background checks for new employees to be phased in over a two-year period.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(4): The applicant or employee shall receive written notice that the background check has been requested.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(5): Each applicant or employee subject to a criminal background check under this section shall, if required by the institution:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(5)(a): be fingerprinted; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(5)(b): consent to a fingerprint background check by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(5)(b)(i): the Utah Bureau of Criminal Identification; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(5)(b)(ii): the Federal Bureau of Investigation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6)(a): Institutions may request the Utah Bureau of Criminal Identification to conduct criminal background checks of prospective employees and, where reasonable cause exists, existing employees pursuant to an institution's policy.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6)(b): At the request of an institution, the Utah Bureau of Criminal Identification shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6)(b)(i): release the individual's full record of criminal convictions to the administrator requesting the information; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6)(b)(ii): seek additional information from regional or national criminal data files in responding to inquiries under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6)(c): Information received by the Utah Bureau of Criminal Identification from entities other than agencies or political subdivisions of the state may not be released to a private entity unless the release is permissible under applicable laws or regulations of the entity providing the information.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(6)(d): Except as provided in Subsection (7), the institution shall pay the cost of background checks conducted by the Utah Bureau of Criminal Identification, and the money collected shall be credited to the Utah Bureau of Criminal Identification to offset its expenses.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(7): An institution may by policy require an applicant to pay the costs of a criminal background check as a condition of employment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(8): The applicant or employee shall have an opportunity to respond to any information received as a result of the criminal background check.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-110(9): If a person is denied employment or is dismissed from employment because of information obtained through a criminal background check, the person shall receive written notice of the reasons for denial or dismissal and have an opportunity to respond to the reasons under procedures established by an institution in policy.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-111 Organ donation notification.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-111(1): 26B-4-137; 26B-4-137; 53B-3-102 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-111(1)(a): 26B-4-137 "Donor" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-111(1)(b): 26B-4-137 "Donor registry" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-111(1)(c): 53B-3-102 "Institution of higher education" means an institution as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-111(2): (2)(a)(ii); (2)(a)(i); 26B-8-319
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-111(2)(a): (2)(a)(ii); (2)(a)(i); 26B-8-319 An institution of higher education shall distribute, twice each academic year to each enrolled student:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-111(2)(a)(i): (2)(a)(ii) an electronic message notifying each student of the option to register as a donor by selecting the Internet link described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-111(2)(a)(ii): (2)(a)(i); 26B-8-319 through the electronic message described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-111(2)(b): An institution of higher education may also provide to students information on donor registry by other electronic, printed, or in-person means.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112 Disclosure requirements for institution programs.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1): 53B-1-102 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(a): "Department" means the Department of Workforce Services.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(b): 53B-1-102 "Institution" means an institution of higher education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(c): "Job placement data" means information collected by the board, and based on information from the department, that reflects the job placement rate and industry employment information for a student who graduates from a program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(i): "Program" means a program of organized instruction or study at an institution that leads to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(i)(A): an academic degree;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(i)(B): a professional degree;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(i)(C): a vocational degree;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(i)(D): a certificate of one year or greater or the direct assessment equivalent; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(i)(E): another recognized educational credential.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(d)(ii): "Program" includes instruction or study that, in lieu of time as a measurement for student learning, utilizes direct assessment of student learning, or recognizes the direct assessment of student learning by others, if the assessment is consistent with the accreditation of the institution or program utilizing the results of the assessment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(e): "Student loan information" means the percentage of students at an institution who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(e)(i): received a Title IV loan authorized under:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(e)(i)(A): the Federal Perkins Loan Program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(e)(i)(B): the Federal Family Education Loan Program; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(e)(i)(C): the William D. Ford Direct Loan Program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(e)(ii): fail to pay a loan described in Subsection (1)(e)(i)(A), (B), or (C).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f): "Total costs" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f)(i): the estimated costs a student would incur while completing a program, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f)(i)(A): tuition and fees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f)(i)(B): books, supplies, and equipment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f)(ii): calculated based on a student's degree, the institution's average costs that would be incurred while a student completes a program and are subsidized by taxpayer contribution, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f)(ii)(A): tuition and fees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(f)(ii)(B): other applicable expenses subsidized by taxpayer contribution for program completion.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(1)(g): "Wage data" means information collected by the board, and based on information from the department, that reflects a student's wage the first year and fifth year after a student has successfully completed a program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(2)(a): Except as provided in Subsection (4), for each program listed in an institution's course catalog or each program otherwise offered by the institution, the institution shall provide a conspicuous and direct link on the institution's website, subject to Subsection (2)(b), to the following information maintained by the board in accordance with Subsection (3):
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(2)(a)(i): job placement data;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(2)(a)(ii): to the extent supporting data is available, student loan information;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(2)(a)(iii): total costs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(2)(a)(iv): wage data.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(2)(b): An institution shall include the information described in Subsection (2)(a) on each institutional website that includes academic, cost, financial aid, or admissions information for a program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(3): The commissioner, under the board's direction, shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(3)(a): collect the information described in Subsection (2)(a);
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(3)(b): develop through user testing a format for the display of information described in Subsection (2)(a) that is easily accessible and informative; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(3)(c): maintain the information described in Subsection (2)(a) so that it is current.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(4): An institution is not subject to Subsection (2) for a program that the institution is required to report on under 34 C.F.R. Sec. 668.412.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-112(5): The board shall, in accordance with Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act, make rules for the implementation and administration of this section.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113 Education loan notifications.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(a): "Borrower" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(a)(i): an individual enrolled in an eligible postsecondary institution who receives an education loan; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(a)(ii): an individual, including a parent or legal guardian, who receives an education loan to fund education expenses of an individual enrolled in an eligible postsecondary institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(b): "Education loan" means a loan made to a borrower that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(b)(i): made directly by a federal or state program; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(b)(ii): insured or guaranteed under a federal or state program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(c): "Eligible postsecondary institution" means a public or private postsecondary institution that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(c)(i): is located in Utah; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(1)(c)(ii): participates in federal student assistance programs under the Higher Education Act of 1965, Title IV, 20 U.S.C. Sec. 1070 et seq.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(2): Annually, on or before July 1, an eligible postsecondary institution that receives information about a borrower's education loan shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(2)(a): notify the borrower that the borrower has an education loan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(2)(b): direct the borrower to the National Student Loan Data System described in 20 U.S.C. Sec. 1092b to receive information about the borrower's education loan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(2)(c): provide the borrower information on how the borrower can access an online repayment calculator.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-113(3): An eligible postsecondary institution does not incur liability for information provided to a borrower in accordance with this section.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116 Prohibition on the use of certain submissions in higher education -- Exceptions.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(1): 67-27-107 As used in this section, "prohibited submission" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2): Except as provided in Subsections (4) and (6), an institution may not require, request, solicit, or compel a prohibited submission as a certification or condition before taking action with respect to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(a): employment, including decisions regarding:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(a)(i): hiring;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(a)(ii): terms of employment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(a)(iii): benefits;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(a)(iv): compensation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(a)(v): seniority status;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(a)(vi): tenure or continuing status;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(a)(vii): promotion;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(a)(viii): performance reviews;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(a)(ix): transfer;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(a)(x): termination; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(a)(xi): appointment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(b): admission to, advancement in, or graduation from an institution or an academic program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(c): participation in an institution-sponsored program; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(2)(d): qualification for or receipt of state financial aid or other state financial assistance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(3): An institution may not grant any form of preferential consideration to an individual who, with or without solicitation from the institution, provides a prohibited submission for consideration for any action described in Subsection (2).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(4): If federal law requires an institution to accept or require a prohibited submission, the institution:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(4)(a): may accept the prohibited submission only to the extent required under federal law; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(4)(b): shall limit consideration of the information contained in the prohibited submission to the extent necessary to satisfy the requirement under federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(5): For a required prohibited submission under Subsection (4), an institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(5)(a): prepare a report to the institution's governing board detailing the circumstances under which a prohibited submission is required; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(5)(b): publish the report described in Subsection (5)(a) on the institution's governing board website in a conspicuous location.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(6): Nothing in this section limits or prohibits an institution's authority to establish policies that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(6)(a): are necessary to comply with state or federal law, including laws relating to prohibited discrimination or harassment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(6)(b): require disclosure of an employee's academic research, classroom teaching, or coursework; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(6)(c): require an applicant for employment, tenure, or promotion to disclose or discuss the applicant's:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(6)(c)(i): research;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(6)(c)(ii): teaching agenda;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(6)(c)(iii): artistic creations; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(6)(c)(iv): pedagogical approaches or experiences with students of all learning abilities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(7): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(7)(a): Beginning on July 1, 2025, the board shall conduct a biennial review of an institution of higher education's compliance with this section as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(7)(a)(i): for 2025, on each institution of higher education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(7)(a)(ii): for 2026, and every year after, on one-half of the degree granting institutions of higher education and one-half of the technical colleges.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(7)(b): If the board identifies a violation of this section, the board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(7)(b)(i): on or before 30 days after the day on which the board identifies the violation, work with the institution to create a remediation plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(7)(b)(ii): provide the institution 180 days after the day of the creation of the remediation plan to cure the violation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(8): On or before November 1 of each year, the board shall prepare and submit a report to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee on:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(8)(a): the review process and each institution's compliance determination; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(8)(b): if a violation is identified, the remediation plan and progress under Subsection (7)(b).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(9): The Legislature may withhold future state appropriations to an institution that fails to cure a violation of this section within the time provided under Subsection (7)(b).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-116(10): The board shall make rules in accordance with Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act, to establish a procedure for accepting and processing an individual's complaint against an institution for an alleged violation of this section.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117 Prohibition on the use of certain training in higher education -- Exceptions.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(1): 53B-1-118 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(1)(a): 53B-1-118 "Prohibited training" means a mandatory instructional program and related materials that an institution requires the institution's employees, prospective employees, students, or prospective students, to attend that promote prohibited discriminatory practices as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(1)(b): "Prohibited training" includes an in-person or online seminar, discussion group, workshop, other program, or related materials.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(2): An institution may not require prohibited training.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(3): An institution shall annually train the institution's faculty and staff on academic freedom and freedom of speech in accordance with state or federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(4): Nothing in this section limits or prohibits an institution's authority to establish policies that are necessary to comply with state or federal law, including laws relating to prohibited discrimination or harassment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(5)(a): Beginning on July 1, 2025, the board shall conduct a biennial review of an institution of higher education's compliance with this section as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(5)(a)(i): for 2025, on each institution of higher education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(5)(a)(ii): for 2026, and every year after, on one-half of the institutions of higher education and one-half of the technical colleges.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(5)(b): If the board identifies a violation of this section, the board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(5)(b)(i): on or before 30 days after the day on which the board identifies the violation, work with the institution to create a remediation plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(5)(b)(ii): provide the institution 180 days after the day of the creation of the remediation plan to cure the violation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(6): On or before November 1 of each year, the board shall prepare and submit a report to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee on:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(6)(a): the review process and each institution's compliance determination; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(6)(b): if a violation is identified, the remediation plan and progress under Subsection (5)(b).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(7): The Legislature may withhold future state appropriations to an institution that fails to cure a violation of this section within the time provided under Subsection (5)(b).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-117(8): The board shall make rules in accordance with Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act, to establish a procedure for accepting and processing an individual's complaint against an institution for an alleged violation of this section.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118 Prohibited discriminatory practices -- Restrictions -- Campus climate survey -- Exceptions.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(a): "Important government interest" means a governmental purpose relating to athletic competition or athletic safety in public education or privacy.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(b): "Personal identity characteristics" means an individual's race, color, ethnicity, sex, sexual orientation, national origin, religion, or gender identity.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(i): "Prohibited discriminatory practice" means engaging in or maintaining a policy, procedure, practice, program, office, initiative, or required training that, based on an individual's personal identity characteristics:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(i)(A): promotes the differential treatment of an individual without an important government interest;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(i)(B): influences the employment decisions of an individual other than through the use of neutral hiring processes with regard to personal identity characteristics and in accordance with federal law;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(i)(C): influences an individual's admission to, advancement in, or graduation from an institution, the public education system, or an academic program; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(i)(D): influences an individual's participation in an institution-sponsored or public education system-sponsored program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(ii): "Prohibited discriminatory practice" also means engaging in or maintaining a policy, procedure, practice, program, office, initiative, or required training that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(ii)(A): asserts that one personal identity characteristic is inherently superior or inferior to another personal identity characteristic;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(ii)(B): asserts that an individual, by virtue of the individual's personal identity characteristics, is inherently privileged, oppressed, racist, sexist, oppressive, or a victim, whether consciously or unconsciously;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(ii)(C): asserts that an individual should be discriminated against in violation of Title VI, Title VII, and Title IX, receive adverse treatment, be advanced, or receive beneficial treatment because of the individual's personal identity characteristics;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(ii)(D): asserts that an individual's moral character is determined by the individual's personal identity characteristics;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(ii)(E): asserts that an individual, by virtue of the individual's personal identity characteristics, bears responsibility for actions committed in the past by other individuals with the same personal identity characteristics;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(ii)(F): asserts that an individual should feel discomfort, guilt, anguish, or other psychological distress solely because of the individual's personal identity characteristics;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(ii)(G): asserts that meritocracy is inherently racist or sexist;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(ii)(H): asserts that socio-political structures are inherently a series of power relationships and struggles among racial groups;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(ii)(I): promotes resentment between, or resentment of, individuals by virtue of their personal identity characteristics;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(ii)(J): ascribes values, morals, or ethical codes, privileges, or beliefs to an individual because of the individual's race, color, ethnicity, sex, sexual orientation, national origin, or gender identity;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(ii)(K): considers an individual's personal identity characteristics in determining receipt of state financial aid or other state financial assistance, including a scholarship award or tuition waiver; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(ii)(L): is referred to or named diversity, equity, and inclusion.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(c)(iii): "Prohibited discriminatory practice" does not include policies or procedures required by state or federal law, including laws relating to prohibited discrimination or harassment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(d): "Student success and support" means an office, division, employment position, or other unit of an institution established or maintained to provide support, guidance, and resources that equip all students, including all students at higher risk of not completing a certificate or degree, with experiences and opportunities for success in each student's academic and career goals, and without excluding individuals on the basis of an individual's personal identity characteristics.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(e): "Title VI" means Title VI of the Civil Rights Act of 1964, 42 U.S.C. Sec. 2000d et seq.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(f): "Title VII" means Title VII of the Civil Rights Act of 1964, 42 U.S.C. Sec. 2000e et seq.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(1)(g): "Title IX" means Title IX of the Education Amendments of 1972, 20 U.S.C. Sec. 1681 et seq.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(2): 67-27-107(1)(b)(ii) An institution may not:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(2)(a): engage in prohibited discriminatory practices;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(2)(b): 67-27-107(1)(b)(ii) take, express, or assert a position or opinion on subjects described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(2)(c): establish or maintain an office, division, employment position, or other unit of an institution established to implement, develop, plan, or promote campus policies, procedures, practices, programs, or initiatives, regarding prohibited discriminatory practices; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(2)(d): employ or assign an employee or a third-party whose duties for an institution include coordinating, creating, developing, designing, implementing, organizing, planning, or promoting policies, programming, training, practices, activities, and procedures relating to prohibited discriminatory practices.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(3): An institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(3)(a): ensure that all students have access to programs providing student success and support;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(3)(b): publish the titles and syllabi of all mandatory courses, seminars, classes, workshops, and training sessions on the institution's website in an online database readily searchable by the public;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(3)(c): annually train employees on the separation of personal political advocacy from an institution's business and employment activities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(3)(d): develop strategies, including inviting speakers, to promote viewpoint diversity; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(3)(e): establish policies and procedures to include opportunities for education and research on free speech and civic education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(4): Beginning on or before July 1, 2025, the board shall report to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee on the status and allocation of appropriated funds for student success and support.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(5): The Legislature shall, in a line item appropriation, appropriate ongoing funding to support an institution's student success and support program in accordance with this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(6)(a): On or before January 1, 2025, the board shall contract with a third-party contractor, in accordance with Title 63G, Chapter 6a, Utah Procurement Code, to conduct a campus expression climate survey of each institution:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(6)(a)(i): to assess student, faculty, and staff perceptions of and experiences with an institution's campus environment that measures the student's, faculty member's, and staff member's perception of and experience with an institution's campus environment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(6)(a)(ii): that measures the student's, faculty member's, and staff member's perception of and experience with campus policy and practice regarding freedom of speech and academic freedom at the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(6)(b): The board shall collect the results of each campus expression climate survey under Subsection (6) and submit the results to the Office of Legislative Research and General Counsel beginning on or before July 1.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(7): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(7)(a): The Office of Legislative Research and General Counsel shall provide a summary report on the data collected from the campus expression climate surveys to the Education Interim Committee on or before:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(7)(a)(i): November 1, 2027, for reports received in years 2025, 2026, and 2027;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(7)(a)(ii): November 1, 2030, for reports received in years 2028, 2029, and 2030; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(7)(a)(iii): November 1, 2033, for reports received in years 2031, 2032, and 2033.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(7)(b): On or before November 1, 2035, the Office of Legislative Research and General Counsel shall provide a comprehensive report of the campus expression climate surveys to the Education Interim Committee.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(8): Nothing in this section requires an individual to respond to a campus expression climate survey.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(9): Nothing in this section limits or prohibits an institution's authority to establish policies that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(9)(a): are necessary to comply with state or federal law, including laws relating to prohibited discrimination or harassment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(9)(b): require disclosure of an employee's academic research, classroom teaching, or coursework; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(9)(c): require for employment, tenure, or promotion to disclose or discuss the applicant's:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(9)(c)(i): research;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(9)(c)(ii): teaching agenda;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(9)(c)(iii): artistic creations; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(9)(c)(iv): pedagogical approaches or experiences with students of all learning abilities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(10): This section does not apply to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(10)(a): requirements necessary for athletic and accreditation compliance;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(10)(b): academic research;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(10)(c): academic course teaching in the classroom;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(10)(d): a grant that would otherwise require:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(10)(d)(i): a department, office, division, or other unit of an institution to engage in a prohibited discriminatory practice if the grant has been reviewed and approved by the institution's board of trustees; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(10)(d)(ii): an institution to engage in a prohibited discriminatory practice if the grant has been reviewed and approved by the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(10)(e): requirements necessary for an institution to establish or maintain eligibility for any federal program; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(10)(f): private scholarships administered by an institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(11): Notwithstanding any other provision of this part, the University of Utah may take any action required for the University of Utah to comply with the terms of an agreement entered into between the University of Utah and the Ute Indian Tribe before July 1, 2024.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(12): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(12)(a): Beginning on July 1, 2025, the board shall conduct a biennial review of an institution of higher education's compliance with this section as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(12)(a)(i): for 2025, on each institution of higher education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(12)(a)(ii): for 2026, and every year after, on one-half of the degree granting institutions of higher education and one-half of the technical colleges.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(12)(b): If the board identifies a violation of this section, the board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(12)(b)(i): on or before 30 days after the day on which the board identifies the violation, work with the institution to create a remediation plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(12)(b)(ii): provide the institution 180 days after the day of the creation of the remediation plan to cure the violation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(13): On or before November 1 of each year, the board shall prepare and submit a report to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee on:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(13)(a): the review process and each institution's compliance determination; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(13)(b): if a violation is identified, the remediation plan and progress under Subsection (12)(b).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(14): On or before December 1 of each year, the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(14)(a): report the findings under Subsections (4) and (13) to the Legislature; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(14)(b): make appropriation recommendations about an institution's compliance with this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(15): The Legislature may withhold future state appropriations to an institution that fails to cure a violation of this section within the time provided under Subsection (12)(b).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-118(16): The board shall make rules in accordance with Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act, to establish a procedure for accepting and processing an individual's complaint against an institution for an alleged violation of this section.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-119 Bereavement leave for miscarriage and stillbirth.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-119(1): As used in this section "miscarriage" means the spontaneous or accidental loss of a fetus, regardless of gestational age or the duration of the pregnancy.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-119(2): 78B-6-103 An institution shall adopt policies providing at least three work days of paid bereavement leave for an employee following the end of the employee's pregnancy by way of miscarriage or stillbirth or following the end of another individual's pregnancy by way of a miscarriage or stillbirth, if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-119(2)(a): the employee is the individual's spouse or partner;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-119(2)(b): the employee is the individual's former spouse or partner and the employee would have been a biological parent of a child born as a result of the pregnancy;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-119(2)(c): 78B-6-103 the employee provides documentation to show that the individual intended for the employee to be an adoptive parent, as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-119(2)(d): under a valid gestational agreement in accordance with Title 78B, Chapter 15, Part 8, Gestational Agreement, the employee would have been a parent of a child born as a result of the pregnancy.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402 Establishment of board -- Powers, duties, and authority -- Reports.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1)(a): There is established the Utah Board of Higher Education, which:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1)(a)(i): is the governing board for the institutions of higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1)(a)(ii): controls, oversees, and regulates the Utah System of Higher Education in a manner consistent with the purpose of this title and the specific powers and responsibilities granted to the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1)(b): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1)(b)(i): The University of Utah shall provide administrative support for the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(1)(b)(ii): Notwithstanding Subsection (1)(b)(i), the board shall maintain the board's independence, including in relation to the powers and responsibilities granted to the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2): 53B-16-101; 53B-16-102; 53B-2-102; 53B-2a-117; 53B-2a-118; 53B-16-110; 53B-16-105; 64-13-6 The board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(a): establish and promote a state-level vision and goals for higher education that emphasize data-driven retrospective and prospective system priorities, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(a)(i): quality;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-402(2)(a)(ii): affordability;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-403 Committees.
-------------------------------------------
The board may form committees to support the board in fulfilling the board's duties.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405 Qualifications for board members.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(1): The board shall develop qualifications for the composition of the board to ensure that combined, the board members have:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(1)(a): a range of experience, including experience in industry;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(1)(b): varied areas of expertise; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(1)(c): varied geographic representation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2): In developing the qualifications, the board shall consider:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(a): expertise in:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(a)(i): business or industry;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(a)(ii): technical education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(a)(iii): general education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(a)(iv): advanced education and research;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(b): geographic representation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c): knowledge or experience in a field including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(i): finance;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(ii): accounting or auditing;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(iii): law;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(iv): facilities or real estate;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(v): educational delivery models;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(vi): workforce development;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(vii): economic development;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(viii): kindergarten through grade 12 education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(2)(c)(ix): educational quality assessment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-405(3): The board shall consult with the governor to develop the qualifications described in this section.

----------------------------------------------------------------

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-410(1): The board is the successor to the Utah System of Technical Colleges Board of Trustees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-410(2): For the Utah System of Technical Colleges Board of Trustees, the board:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-410(2)(a): is vested with all rights, titles, privileges, powers, obligations, liabilities, immunities, franchises, endowments, assets, property, and claims;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-410(2)(b): shall fulfill and perform all obligations, including obligations relating to outstanding bonds and notes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-1-410(2)(c): may continue an administrative rule.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-101(1): The following institutions of higher education are bodies politic and corporate with perpetual succession and with all rights, immunities, and franchises necessary to function as such:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-101(1)(a): the University of Utah;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-101(1)(i): Bridgerland Technical College;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-101(2)(b): An institution of higher education is vested with all the property, franchises, and endowments of, and is subject to, all the contracts, obligations, and liabilities of the institution's respective predecessor.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-102 Appointment of institution of higher education presidents.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-102(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-102(1)(a): "Institution of higher education" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-102(1)(a)(i): a degree-granting institution; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-102(1)(a)(ii): a technical college.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-102(1)(b): "President" means the president of an institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-102(1)(c): "Search committee" means a committee that selects finalists for a position as an institution of higher education president.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-102(2): The board shall appoint a president for each institution of higher education.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103 Degree-granting institution board of trustees -- Powers and duties.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(1): A degree-granting institution has a board of trustees that may act on behalf of the institution in performing duties, responsibilities, and functions as may be specifically authorized to the board of trustees by the board or by statute.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(2): 53B-16-102 A board of trustees of a degree-granting institution has the following powers and duties:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(2)(a): to facilitate communication between the institution and the community;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(2)(b): to assist in planning, implementing, and executing fund raising and development projects aimed at supplementing institutional appropriations;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(2)(c): to perpetuate and strengthen alumni and community identification with the degree-granting institution's tradition and goals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(2)(d): to select recipients of honorary degrees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(2)(e): 53B-16-102 to approve changes to the degree-granting institution's programs, in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3): 53B-1-402 A board of trustees of a degree-granting institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3)(a): 53B-1-402 approve a strategic plan for the institution of higher education that is aligned with:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3)(a)(i): state attainment goals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3)(a)(ii): workforce needs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3)(a)(iii): 53B-1-402 board goals and metrics described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3)(a)(iv): the institution of higher education's role, mission, and distinctiveness; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-103(3)(b): monitor the institution of higher education's progress toward achieving the strategic plan.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104 Degree-granting institution board of trustees -- Membership --  Terms -- Vacancies -- Oath -- Officers -- Bylaws -- Quorum -- Committees -- Compensation.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(1): As used in this section, "board of trustees" means the board of trustees for a degree-granting institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(2)(a): The board of trustees of a degree-granting institution consists of the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(2)(a)(i): except as provided in Subsection (2)(c), eight individuals appointed by the governor with the advice and consent of the Senate in accordance with Title 63G, Chapter 24, Part 2, Vacancies; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(2)(a)(ii): two ex officio members who are the president of the institution's alumni association, and the president of the associated students of the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(2)(b): In making the appointments described in Subsections (2)(a)(i) and (2)(c)(i), the governor:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(2)(b)(i): shall ensure that the membership of a board of trustees includes representation of interests of business, industry, and labor; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(2)(b)(ii): may not appoint an individual to more than two consecutive full terms.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(2)(c): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(2)(c)(i): The board of trustees of Utah State University has nine individuals appointed by the governor with the advice and consent of the Senate in accordance with Title 63G, Chapter 24, Part 2, Vacancies.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(2)(c)(ii): One of the nine individuals described in Subsection (2)(c)(i) shall reside in the Utah State University Eastern service region or the Utah State University Blanding service region.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(3)(a): The governor shall appoint four members of each board of trustees during each odd-numbered year to four-year terms commencing on July 1 of the year of appointment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(3)(b): Except as provided in Subsection (3)(d), a member appointed under Subsection (2)(a)(i) or (2)(c)(i) holds office until a successor is appointed and qualified.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(3)(c): The ex officio members serve for the same period as they serve as presidents and until their successors have qualified.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(3)(d): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(3)(d)(i): The governor may remove a member appointed under Subsection (2)(a)(i) or (2)(c)(i) for cause.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(3)(d)(ii): The governor shall consult with the president of the Senate before removing a member in accordance with Subsection (3)(d)(i).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(4): When a vacancy occurs in the membership of a board of trustees for any reason, the governor shall, with the advice and consent of the Senate in accordance with Title 63G, Chapter 24, Part 2, Vacancies, appoint a replacement for the unexpired term.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(5)(a): Each member of a board of trustees shall take the official oath of office prior to assuming the office.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(5)(b): The oath shall be filed with the Division of Archives and Records Services.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(6): A board of trustees shall elect a chair and vice chair, who serve for two years and until their successors are elected and qualified.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(7): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(7)(a): A board of trustees may enact bylaws for the board of trustees' own government, including provisions for regular meetings.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(7)(b): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(7)(b)(i): A board of trustees may provide for an executive committee in the board of trustees' bylaws.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(7)(b)(ii): If established, an executive committee shall have full authority of the board of trustees to act upon routine matters during the interim between board of trustees meetings.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(7)(b)(iii): An executive committee may act on nonroutine matters only under extraordinary and emergency circumstances.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(7)(b)(iv): An executive committee shall report the executive committee's activities to the board of trustees at the board of trustees' next regular meeting following the action.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(7)(c): Copies of a board of trustees' bylaws shall be filed with the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(8): A quorum is required to conduct business and consists of six members.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(9): A board of trustees may establish advisory committees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(10): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107; 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 A member may not receive compensation or benefits for the member's service, but may receive per diem and travel expenses in accordance with:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(10)(a): 63A-3-106 Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(10)(b): 63A-3-107 Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(10)(c): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 rules made by the Division of Finance pursuant to Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-104(11): A board of trustees member shall comply with the conflict of interest provisions described in Title 63G, Chapter 24, Part 3, Conflicts of Interest.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106 Duties and responsibilities of the president of an institution of higher education -- Approval by board of trustees.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(1)(a): "Institution" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(1)(a)(i): a degree-granting institution; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(1)(a)(ii): a technical college.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(1)(b): "President" means the president of an institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(2): The president of each institution may exercise grants of power and authority as the board delegates, as well as the necessary and proper exercise of powers and authority not denied to the institution or the institution's administration, faculty, or students by the board or by law, to ensure the effective and efficient administration and operation of the institution consistent with the statewide strategic plan for higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3): A president may:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(a): appoint or employ administrative officers, deans, faculty members, professional personnel, and support personnel;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(b): prescribe duties for a position described in Subsection (3)(a); and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(3)(c): determine the salary for an employed position described in Subsection (3)(a), in accordance with the institution's human resources policies.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(4)(a): A president may, after consultation with the institution's board of trustees, exercise powers related to the institution's employees, including faculty and persons under contract with the institution, by implementing:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(4)(a)(i): policies governing personnel;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(4)(a)(ii): furloughs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(4)(a)(iii): reductions in force;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(4)(a)(iv): program reductions or discontinuance;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(4)(a)(v): early retirement incentives that provide cost savings to the institution; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(4)(a)(vi): other measures that provide cost savings, facilitate efficiencies, or otherwise enable the institution to meet the institution's mission and role.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5): 53B-7-101; 53B-1-402 A president shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(a): control and manage the budget and finances of the institution, including by, as determined by the president:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(a)(i): establishing the institution's budget; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(a)(ii): establishing or adjusting administrative or academic unit budgets; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(b): 53B-7-101; 53B-1-402 subject to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(b)(i): 53B-1-402 tuition for the institution, including both resident and nonresident tuition if the institution is a degree-granting institution, subject to the approval of the board as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(b)(ii): fees and other charges for the institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(5)(c): establish the organization and structure of the institution, including by, as determined by the president, creating, merging, or eliminating a college, department, or other administrative or academic unit of the institution;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6): 53B-2-106.1 Subject to the approval of the institution's board of trustees, a president:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6)(a): shall establish a budgetary policy, such as policy regarding benefits and endowment investments;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6)(b): 53B-2-106.1 subject to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6)(b)(i): enacting and implementing rules;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6)(b)(ii): ensuring that the faculty may only have jurisdiction over:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6)(b)(ii)(A): academic requirements for admission, degrees, and certificates; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6)(b)(ii)(B): course curriculum and instruction;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6)(b)(iii): permitting faculty to have jurisdiction over a matter other than a matter described in Subsection (6)(b)(ii) only if the following entities expressly authorize or delegate such power:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6)(b)(iii)(A): the Legislature;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6)(b)(iii)(B): the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6)(b)(iii)(C): institution's board of trustees; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6)(b)(iii)(D): the institution's president; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6)(b)(iv): if the institution is a degree-granting institution, the establishment of a prescribed system of tenure; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(6)(c): may authorize the faculty to determine the general initiation and direction of instruction and of the examination, admission, and classification of students.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(7): A president may establish policies for the administration and operation of the institution that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(7)(a): are consistent with the institution's role that the board establishes, rules which the board enacts, and the laws of the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(7)(b): may provide for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(7)(b)(i): administrative, faculty, student, and joint committees with jurisdiction over specified institutional matters;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(7)(b)(ii): student government and student affairs organizations;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(7)(b)(iii): the establishment of institutional standards in furtherance of the ideals of higher education to which the institution and the institution's administration, faculty, and students subscribe and foster; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(7)(b)(iv): the holding of classes on legal holidays, other than Sunday.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(8): A president shall manage the president's institution as a part of the Utah System of Higher Education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(9): In performing any of the acts described in this section, a president may, in the president's sole discretion, seek input from the institution's faculty, staff, or students.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(10): The board shall establish guidelines relating to the roles and relationships between presidents and boards of trustees, including those matters for which law requires the approval of a board of trustees before implementation by the president.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(11): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(11)(a): A president is subject to regular review and evaluation that the board administers, in consultation with the institution's board of trustees, through a process the board approves.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106(11)(b): Only the board may formally assess a president's performance, formally declare a president's standing, or take other formal action to evaluate a president.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1 Tenure -- Reporting.
------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(1): A president of a degree-granting institution, in consultation with the degree-granting institution's board of trustees, shall make policies:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(1)(a): related to tenure and post-tenure review; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(1)(b): ensuring that the terms and conditions of tenured employment are stated in writing and provided to a faculty member.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(2): Tenure and post-tenure policies shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(2)(a): protect academic freedom in teaching, research, and in an individual's personal life;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(2)(b): require that a final award of tenure be approved by the president of the degree-granting institution offering the award of tenure, in consultation with the board of trustees of the degree-granting institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(2)(c): comply with this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(3): Beginning July 1, 2024, a tenured faculty member may be dismissed from employment at a degree-granting institution:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(3)(a): for cause, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(3)(a)(i): professional incompetence;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(3)(a)(ii): serious misconduct or unethical behavior;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(3)(a)(iii): legal misconduct substantially related to the performance of duties;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(3)(a)(iv): serious violations of board or institution rules;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(3)(a)(v): the conviction of a crime affecting the fitness of the tenured faculty member to engage in teaching, research, service, outreach, administration, or other assigned duties;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(3)(a)(vi): falsified credentials or plagiarism; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(3)(a)(vii): inability or unwillingness to meet institutional expectations, including failure to address deficiencies outlined in a remediation plan following post-tenure review;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(3)(b): if the program in which the tenured faculty member works is discontinued by the degree-granting institution or modified to such a degree that the tenured faculty member's position is no longer needed; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(3)(c): in the event of financial exigency of the degree-granting institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(4): Policies governing dismissal of a tenured faculty member for cause shall include, at a minimum:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(4)(a): notice to the tenured faculty member of the alleged cause, including any evidence supporting the allegation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(4)(b): providing reasonable time and opportunity for the tenured faculty member to respond;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(4)(c): a hearing before an independent board of tenured faculty peers;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(4)(d): a written determination on the issue, including a determination of termination or continued employment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(4)(e): an appeals process ending with the final decision of the president of the degree-granting institution in consultation with the board of trustees of the degree-granting institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(5): A tenured faculty member who is being dismissed because the program in which the tenured faculty member works is discontinued or modified, as described in Subsection (3)(b), or in the event of financial exigency of the degree-granting institution, as described in Subsection (3)(c), shall receive severance in accordance with the terms of the tenured faculty member's employment contract.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(6): Nothing in this section prohibits a president of a degree-granting institution from creating additional policies and processes regarding discipline of a tenured faculty member.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(7): Beginning July 1, 2024, a degree-granting institution shall conduct, and a tenured faculty member shall receive:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(7)(a): an annual performance review of the tenured faculty member's performance; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(7)(b): a post-tenure review, as described in Subsection (9).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(8): A president of a degree-granting institution shall ensure that each program or department at the degree-granting institution has policies describing the minimum performance of a tenured faculty member for use in a post-tenure review.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(9): A post-tenure review shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(9)(a): be conducted by a committee of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(9)(a)(i): tenured faculty member peers, appointed by the appropriate vice president at the degree-granting institution in consultation with the faculty member's department chair, including at least two individuals appointed from either a different department than the tenured faculty member going through post-tenure review, a different degree-granting institution than the tenured faculty member going through post-tenure review, or both; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(9)(a)(ii): the provost or the provost's designee; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(9)(b): consist of a comprehensive review of the tenured faculty member's performance over the previous five years, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(9)(b)(i): teaching assessment, including student evaluations, for all courses taught;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(9)(b)(ii): the quality of the tenured faculty member's scholarly research;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(9)(b)(iii): service to the profession, school, or community;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(9)(b)(iv): annual performance reviews;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(9)(b)(v): intellectual property owned wholly or partly by, or commercialization efforts attributed to, the tenured faculty member;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(9)(b)(vi): the tenured faculty member's compliance with the degree-granting institution's policies regarding the responsibilities and ethical obligations of faculty members; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(9)(b)(vii): any improvement plans for underperformance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(10): (10)(a); (10)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(10)(a): If, following a post-tenure review, a tenured faculty member is found to not meet the standards established by the degree-granting institution, the degree-granting institution shall create a remediation plan to address deficiencies and a timeline by which the tenured faculty member is expected to address the deficiencies.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(10)(b): (10)(a) A tenured faculty member who fails to address deficiencies as described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(10)(c): (10)(a) In consultation with the board of trustees, a president of a degree-granting institution who does not dismiss a tenured faculty member who fails to address deficiencies as described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(11): A president of a degree-granting institution shall provide an annual report to the board, no later than October 1 of each year, with the following information:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(11)(a): the number of post-tenure reviews that took place at the degree-granting institution in the previous year;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(11)(b): an analysis of scores from post-tenure reviews that took place in the previous year with personal information redacted;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(11)(c): the number of post-tenure reviews from the previous year that resulted in a remediation plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(11)(d): a qualitative summary of the types of remediation plans created in the previous year, including an average timeline by which tenured faculty members are expected to address deficiencies; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-106.1(11)(e): a summary of written justifications described in Subsection (10)(c), if any, with personal information redacted.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-110 Utah Valley University -- Institutional name change.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-110(1): Beginning July 1, 2008, Utah Valley State College shall be known as Utah Valley University.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-110(2): The university is a continuation of Utah Valley State College and shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-110(2)(a): possess all rights, title, privileges, powers, immunities, franchises, endowments, property, and claims of the college; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-110(2)(b): fulfill and perform all obligations of the college, including obligations relating to outstanding bonds and notes.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111 Utah Tech University -- Institutional name change.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(1)(a): "Board of trustees" means the board of trustees of Utah Tech University.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(1)(b): "Institution" means Utah Tech University.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(2)(a): Dixie State University shall be known as Utah Tech University.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(2)(b): Utah Tech University is a continuation of Dixie State College of Utah and Dixie State University and shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(2)(b)(i): possess all rights, titles, privileges, powers, immunities, franchises, endowments, property, and claims of Dixie State University and Dixie State College of Utah; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(2)(b)(ii): fulfill and perform all obligations of Dixie State University and Dixie State College of Utah, including obligations relating to outstanding bonds and notes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(3): The board of trustees in consultation with the Utah Board of Higher Education shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(3)(a): create a committee to recommend a name for the institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(3)(b): ensure that the committee:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(3)(b)(i): represents students, university personnel, community members, and industry leaders in the committee's membership;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(3)(b)(ii): provides opportunity for input from and collaboration with the public, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(3)(b)(ii)(A): residents of southwestern Utah;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(3)(b)(ii)(B): institutional partners; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(3)(b)(ii)(C): university faculty, staff, students, and alumni;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(3)(b)(iii): reviews options for the institution's name; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(3)(b)(iv): makes recommendations regarding the institution's name to the board of trustees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(4): (3)(b); (4)(a); (4)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(4)(a): (3)(b) The board of trustees shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(4)(a)(i): (3)(b) review the committee's recommendation described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-111(4)(a)(ii): choose whether to forward a name for the institution to the Utah Board of Higher Education.
