Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-113 Vaccination requirements -- Exemptions -- Face covering requirements.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-113(1): 53B-2-101 An institution of higher education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-113(1)(a): a medical exemption if the student provides to the institution a statement that the claimed exemption is for a medical reason; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-113(1)(b): a personal exemption if the student provides to the institution a statement that the claimed exemption is for a personal or religious belief.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-113(2): An institution that offers both remote and in-person learning options may not deny a student who is exempt from a requirement to receive a vaccine under Subsection (1) to participate in an in-person learning option based upon the student's vaccination status.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-113(3): 53G-9-210; 53B-2-101
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-113(3)(a): 53G-9-210 For purposes of this Subsection (3), "face covering" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-113(3)(b): 53B-2-101 An institution of higher education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-113(4): Subsections (1), (2), and (3) do not apply to a student studying in a medical setting at an institution of higher education if the institution of higher education provides the student the same rights under Title VII of the Civil Rights Act to seek an exemption from a vaccination mandate or face covering mandate as the institution of higher education provides to a health care professional employed by the institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-113(5): Nothing in this section restricts a state or local health department from acting under applicable law to contain the spread of an infectious disease.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-114 Degree-granting institution attorneys -- Appointment -- Duties.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-114(1): Recognizing the status of institutions within the Utah System of Higher Education as bodies politic and corporate, the president of a degree-granting institution may appoint attorneys to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-114(1)(a): provide legal advice to the degree-granting institution's administration; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-114(1)(b): coordinate legal affairs within the degree-granting institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-114(2): An institution shall fund compensation costs and related office expenses for an attorney described in Subsection (1) within existing budgets.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-114(3): The board shall coordinate the activities of attorneys described in Subsection (1).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-114(4): An attorney described in Subsection (1):
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-114(4)(a): may not:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-114(4)(a)(i): conduct litigation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-114(4)(a)(ii): settle a claim covered by the State Risk Management Fund; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-114(4)(a)(iii): issue a formal legal opinion; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-114(4)(b): shall cooperate with the Office of the Attorney General in providing legal representation to a degree-granting institution.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115 Institution of higher education required to provide leave to a legislator on an authorized legislative day.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(a): "Authorized legislative day" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(a)(i): the day on which the Legislature convenes in annual general session, and each day after that day, until midnight of the 45th day of the annual general session;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(a)(ii): a special session day;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(a)(iii): a veto override session day;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(a)(iv): an interim day designated by the Legislative Management Committee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(a)(v): an authorized legislative training day; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(a)(vi): any other day on which a meeting of a committee, subcommittee, commission, task force, or other entity is held, if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(a)(vi)(A): the committee, subcommittee, commission, task force, or other entity is created by statute or joint resolution;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(a)(vi)(B): the legislator's attendance at the meeting is approved by the Legislative Management Committee; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(a)(vi)(C): service and payment for service by the legislator is not in violation of the Utah Constitution, including Article V and Article VI, Sections 6 and 7.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(b): "Authorized legislative training day" means a day that a Legislative Expenses Oversight Committee designates as an authorized legislative day for training or informational purposes, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(b)(i): chair training;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(b)(ii): an issue briefing;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(b)(iii): legislative leadership instruction;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(b)(iv): legislative process training;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(b)(v): legislative rules training;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(b)(vi): new legislator orientation; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(b)(vii): another meeting to brief, instruct, orient, or train a legislator in relation to the legislator's official duties.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(c): "Legislator" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(c)(i): a member of the Utah Senate;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(c)(ii): a member of the Utah House of Representatives; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(c)(iii): an individual who has been elected as a member described in Subsection (1)(c)(i) or (ii), but has not yet been sworn in or begun the individual's term of office.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(d): "Retaliatory action" means to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(d)(i): dismiss the employee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(d)(ii): reduce the employee's compensation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(d)(iii): fail to increase the employee's compensation by an amount that the employee is otherwise entitled to or was promised;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(d)(iv): fail to promote the employee if the employee would have otherwise been promoted; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(1)(d)(v): threaten to take an action described in Subsections (1)(d)(i) through (iv).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(2): Except as provided in Subsection (4), an institution of higher education that employs an individual who is a legislator:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(2)(a): shall grant leave to the individual on an authorized legislative day for the number of hours requested by the individual;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(2)(b): may not interfere with, or otherwise restrain the individual from, using the leave described in Subsection (2)(a); and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(2)(c): may not take retaliatory action against the individual for using the leave described in Subsection (2)(a).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(3): The leave described in Subsection (2) is leave without pay unless the institution of higher education and the individual described in Subsection (2) agree to terms that are more favorable to the individual.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2-115(4): An institution of higher education is not required to comply with Subsection (2) if the institution board of trustees of the institution of higher education determines that complying with the requirement would cause the institution of higher education significant difficulty or expense when considered in relation to the size, financial resources, nature, or structure of the institution of higher education's operations.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 2a - Technical Education
******************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-100.5 Title.
-----------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "Technical Education."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-101 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-101(1): 63A-5b-401 "Capital development" means the same as capital development project, as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-101(2): "Competency-based" means mastery of subject matter or skill level, as demonstrated through business and industry approved standards and assessments, achieved through participation in a hands-on learning environment, and which is tied to observable, measurable performance objectives.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-101(3): 53B-2a-118 "Dedicated project" means a capital development project for which state funds from the Technical Colleges Capital Projects Fund created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-101(4): 53B-2a-118 "Nondedicated project" means a capital development project for which state funds from a source other than the Technical Colleges Capital Projects Fund created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-101(5): 63A-5b-401 "State funds" means the same as that term is defined in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106 Technical colleges -- Duties.
--------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1): (1)(a) Each technical college shall, within the geographic area served by the technical college:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(a): offer technical education programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(b): (1)(a) offer a program described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(b)(i): low cost to adult students, as approved by the board; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(b)(ii): no tuition to secondary students;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(c): develop cooperative agreements with school districts, charter schools, other higher education institutions, businesses, industries, and community and private agencies to maximize the availability of instructional facilities within the geographic area served by the technical college; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d): after consulting with school districts and charter schools within the geographic area served by the technical college:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d)(i): ensure that secondary students in the public education system have access to technical education at the technical college; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d)(ii): prepare and submit an annual report to the board detailing:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d)(ii)(A): how the technical education needs of secondary students within the region are being met;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d)(ii)(B): what access secondary students within the region have to programs offered at the technical college;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d)(ii)(C): how the technical college emphasizes high demand, high wage, high skill jobs in business and industry; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(1)(d)(ii)(D): student tuition and fees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(2): 53E-3-501; 53F-4-504 A technical college may offer:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(2)(a): 53E-3-501 a competency-based high school diploma approved by the State Board of Education in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(2)(b): basic instruction in areas such as reading, language arts, and mathematics that are necessary for student success in a chosen technical education or job-related program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(2)(c): courses of interest when similar offerings to the community are limited and courses are financially self-supporting; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(2)(d): 53F-4-504 secondary school level courses through the Statewide Online Education Program in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(3): (2)(d); (2)(b); (c); (5) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(3)(a): (2)(b); (c) offer courses other than technical education or the basic instruction described in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(3)(b): offer a degree;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(3)(c): (5) offer technical education or basic instruction outside the geographic area served by the technical college without a cooperative agreement between an affected institution of higher education, except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(3)(d): provide tenure or academic rank for its instructors; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(3)(e): participate in intercollegiate athletics.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(4): The mission of a technical college is limited to technical education and may not expand to include academic programs that lead to a degree.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5): (3)(c); (5)(a)(ii); (5)(a)(iii)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(a): (3)(c); (5)(a)(ii) A technical college may offer technical education or basic instruction outside the geographic area served by the technical college without a cooperative agreement, as required in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(a)(i): the technical education or basic instruction is specifically requested by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(a)(i)(A): an employer; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(a)(i)(B): a craft, trade, or apprenticeship program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(a)(ii): the technical college notifies the affected institution about the request; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(a)(iii): (5)(a)(ii) the affected institution is given an opportunity to make a proposal, prior to any contract being finalized or training being initiated by the technical college, to the employer, craft, trade, or apprenticeship program about offering the requested technical education or basic instruction, provided that the proposal shall be presented no later than one business week from the delivery of the notice described under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-106(5)(b): (5)(a)(iii) The requirements under Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107 Technical college presidents.
--------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(1): 53B-2-102 The board shall appoint a president for each technical college in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(2): A technical college president is the chief executive officer of the technical college.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3): A technical college president:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3)(a): does not need to have a doctorate degree; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(3)(b): shall have extensive experience in career and technical education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(4): 53B-2-106 In addition to the duties described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(4)(a): after consulting with the board, other institutions of higher education, school districts, and charter schools within the technical college's region, prepare a comprehensive strategic plan for delivering technical education within the region;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(4)(b): consult with business, industry, the Department of Workforce Services, the Governor's Office of Economic Opportunity, and the Governor's Office of Planning and Budget on an ongoing basis to determine what workers and skills are needed for employment in Utah businesses and industries;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(4)(c): coordinate with local school boards, school districts, and charter schools to meet the technical education needs of secondary students; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-107(4)(d): develop policies and procedures for the admission, classification, instruction, and examination of students in accordance with the policies and accreditation guidelines of the board and the State Board of Education.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-109(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-109(6)(a): A technical college board of trustees may enact bylaws for the technical college board of trustees' own government, including provisions for regular meetings, that are in accordance with the policies of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-109(6)(b): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-109(6)(b)(i): A technical college board of trustees may provide for an executive committee in the technical college board of trustees' bylaws.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-109(6)(b)(ii): If established, an executive committee shall have the full authority of the technical college board of trustees to act upon routine matters during the interim between board of trustees' meetings.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-109(6)(b)(iii): An executive committee may act on nonroutine matters only under extraordinary and emergency circumstances.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-109(6)(b)(iv): An executive committee shall report the executive committee's activities to the technical college board of trustees at the technical college board of trustees' next regular meeting following the activities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-109(7): A technical college board of trustees may establish advisory committees.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110 Technical college board of trustees' powers and duties.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1): 53B-16-102; 53B-1-402 A technical college board of trustees shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(a): assist the technical college president in preparing a budget request for the technical college's annual operations to the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(b): after consulting with the board, other higher education institutions, school districts, and charter schools within the technical college's region, assist the technical college president in preparing a comprehensive strategic plan for delivering technical education within the region;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(c): 53B-16-102 in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(d): adopt an annual budget and fund balances;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(e): conduct annual program evaluations;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f): 53B-1-402
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f)(i): 53B-1-402 approve a strategic plan for the technical college that is aligned with:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f)(i)(A): state attainment goals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f)(i)(B): workforce needs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f)(i)(C): the technical college's role, mission, and distinctiveness; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f)(i)(D): 53B-1-402 board goals and metrics described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(f)(ii): monitor the technical college's progress toward achieving the strategic plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(1)(g): act on behalf of the technical college in performing other duties as authorized by the board or by statute.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-110(2): A technical college board of trustees may not exercise jurisdiction over career and technical education provided by a school district or charter school or provided by a higher education institution independently of the technical college.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1): As used in this section, "higher education institution" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(a): Utah State University for:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(a)(ii): Tooele Technical College; and

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(b)(ii): Davis Technical College;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(d): Southern Utah University for Southwest Technical College; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(1)(e): Utah Tech University for Dixie Technical College.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(2): A technical college may enter into agreements:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(2)(a): with other higher education institutions to cultivate cooperative relationships; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(2)(b): with other public and higher education institutions to enhance career and technical education within the technical college's region.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(3): Before a technical college develops new instructional facilities, the technical college shall give priority to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(3)(a): maintaining the technical college's existing instructional facilities for both secondary and adult students;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(3)(b): coordinating with the president of the technical college's degree-granting partner and entering into any necessary agreements to provide career and technical education to secondary and adult students that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(3)(b)(i): maintain and support existing higher education career and technical education programs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(3)(b)(ii): maximize the use of existing higher education facilities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(3)(c): developing cooperative agreements with school districts, charter schools, other higher education institutions, businesses, industries, and community and private agencies to maximize the availability of career and technical education instructional facilities for both secondary and adult students.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(4): (3)(a); (c)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(4)(a): (3)(a); (c) Before submitting a funding request pertaining to new capital facilities and land purchases to the board, a technical college shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(4)(a)(i): (3)(a); (c) ensure that all available instructional facilities are maximized in accordance with Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(4)(a)(ii): coordinate the request with the president of the technical college's degree-granting partner, if applicable.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(4)(b): The Division of Facilities Construction and Management shall make a finding that the requirements of this section are met before the Division of Facilities Construction and Management may consider a funding request from the board pertaining to new capital facilities and land purchases for a technical college.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(4)(c): A technical college may not construct, approve the construction of, plan for the design or construction of, or consent to the construction of a career and technical education facility without approval of the Legislature.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(5): Before acquiring new fiscal and administrative support structures, a technical college shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(5)(a): review the use of existing public or higher education administrative and accounting systems, financial record systems, and student and financial aid systems for the delivery of education in the region;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(5)(b): determine the feasibility of using existing systems; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-112(5)(c): with the approval of the technical college board of trustees and the board, use the existing systems.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113 Technical colleges -- Leasing authority -- Lease-purchase agreements -- Report.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(1): A technical college may enter into a lease with other higher education institutions, school districts, charter schools, state agencies, or business and industry for a term of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(1)(a): one year or less with the approval of the technical college board of trustees; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(1)(b): more than one year with the approval of the board if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(1)(b)(i): the Legislature approves funding for the lease prior to a technical college entering into the lease; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(1)(b)(ii): the lease agreement includes language that allows termination of the lease without penalty.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2): (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a): A technical college may enter into a lease-purchase agreement if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(i): there is a long-term benefit to the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(ii): the project is included in the technical college master plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(iii): the lease-purchase agreement includes language that allows termination of the lease;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(iv): the lease-purchase agreement is approved by the technical college board of trustees and the board; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(v): the lease-purchase agreement is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(v)(A): reviewed by the Division of Facilities Construction and Management; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(a)(v)(B): approved by the Legislature.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(b): (2)(a) An approval under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(b)(i): all parties, dates, and elements of the agreement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(b)(ii): the equity or collateral component that creates the benefit; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(2)(b)(iii): the options dealing with the sale and division of equity.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(3)(a): Each technical college shall provide an annual lease report to the board that details each of the technical college's leases, annual costs, location, square footage, and recommendations for lease continuation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(3)(b): The board shall compile and distribute an annual combined lease report for all technical colleges to the Division of Facilities Construction and Management and to others upon request.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-113(4): The board shall use the annual combined lease report in determining planning, utilization, and budget requests.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119 Technical college required to provide leave to a legislator on an authorized legislative day.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(a): "Authorized legislative day" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(a)(i): the day on which the Legislature convenes in annual general session, and each day after that day, until midnight of the 45th day of the annual general session;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(a)(ii): a special session day;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(a)(iii): a veto override session day;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(a)(iv): an interim day designated by the Legislative Management Committee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(a)(v): an authorized legislative training day; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(a)(vi): any other day on which a meeting of a committee, subcommittee, commission, task force, or other entity is held, if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(a)(vi)(A): the committee, subcommittee, commission, task force, or other entity is created by statute or joint resolution;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(a)(vi)(B): the legislator's attendance at the meeting is approved by the Legislative Management Committee; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(a)(vi)(C): service and payment for service by the legislator is not in violation of the Utah Constitution, including Article V and Article VI, Sections 6 and 7.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(b): "Authorized legislative training day" means a day that a Legislative Expenses Oversight Committee designates as an authorized legislative day for training or informational purposes, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(b)(i): chair training;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(b)(ii): an issue briefing;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(b)(iii): legislative leadership instruction;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(b)(iv): legislative process training;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(b)(v): legislative rules training;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(b)(vi): new legislator orientation; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(b)(vii): another meeting to brief, instruct, orient, or train a legislator in relation to the legislator's official duties.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(c): "Legislator" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(c)(i): a member of the Utah Senate;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(c)(ii): a member of the Utah House of Representatives; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(c)(iii): an individual who has been elected as a member described in Subsection (1)(c)(i) or (ii), but has not yet been sworn in or begun the individual's term of office.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(d): "Retaliatory action" means to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(d)(i): dismiss the employee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(d)(ii): reduce the employee's compensation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(d)(iii): fail to increase the employee's compensation by an amount that the employee is otherwise entitled to or was promised;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(d)(iv): fail to promote the employee if the employee would have otherwise been promoted; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(1)(d)(v): threaten to take an action described in Subsections (1)(d)(i) through (iv).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(2): Except as provided in Subsection (4), a technical college that employs an individual who is a legislator:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(2)(a): shall grant leave to the individual on an authorized legislative day for the number of hours requested by the individual;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(2)(b): may not interfere with, or otherwise restrain the individual from, using the leave described in Subsection (2)(a); and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(2)(c): may not take retaliatory action against the individual for using the leave described in Subsection (2)(a).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(3): The leave described in Subsection (2) is leave without pay unless the technical college and the individual described in Subsection (2) agree to terms that are more favorable to the individual.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-2a-119(4): A technical college is not required to comply with Subsection (2) if the institution board of trustees of the technical college determines that complying with the requirement would cause the technical college significant difficulty or expense when considered in relation to the size, financial resources, nature, or structure of the technical college's operations.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 3 - Enforcement of Regulations at Institutions
****************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-101 Purpose of chapter.
---------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-101(1): It is the purpose of this chapter to confirm and clarify the power vested in the board to pass rules and regulations governing parking and traffic on campuses and related facilities and to enforce the rules and regulations by all appropriate methods.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-101(2): The board may delegate this authority and other authority granted under this chapter to the president of each institution so long as the rules and regulations are approved by the institution's board of trustees.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-102 State institution of higher education defined.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-102(1): 53B-2-101 As used in this chapter, "state institution of higher education" means an institution described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-102(2): A state institution of higher education includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-102(2)(a): a branch or affiliated institution; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-102(2)(b): a campus or facilities owned, operated, or controlled by the governing board of the state institution of higher education.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103 Power of board and institutions to adopt rules and enact regulations.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(1): 53B-1-102 As used in this section, "institution" means an institution listed in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(2)(a): The board may enact regulations governing the conduct of university and college students, faculty, and employees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(2)(b): A president in consultation with the board of trustees, may enact policies governing the conduct of university and college students, faculty, and employees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(3): 53G-9-210
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(3)(a): An institution may enact traffic, parking, and related policies governing all individuals on campus and facilities owned or controlled by the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(3)(b): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(3)(b)(i): The board and an institution may not require proof of vaccination as a condition for enrollment or attendance within the system of higher education unless the board or an institution allows for the following exemptions:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(3)(b)(i)(A): a medical exemption if the student provides to the institution a statement that the claimed exemption is for a medical reason; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(3)(b)(i)(B): a personal exemption if the student provides to the institution a statement that the claimed exemption is for a personal or religious belief.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(3)(b)(ii): An institution that offers both remote and in-person learning options may not deny a student who is exempt from a requirement to receive a vaccine under Subsection (2)(b)(i) to participate in an in-person learning option based upon the student's vaccination status.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(3)(b)(iii): Subsections (2)(b)(i) and (ii) do not apply to a student studying in a medical setting at an institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(3)(b)(iv): Nothing in this section restricts a state or local health department from acting under applicable law to contain the spread of an infectious disease.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(3)(c): 53G-9-210
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(3)(c)(i): 53G-9-210 For purposes of this Subsection (2)(c), "face covering" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(3)(c)(ii): The board or an institution may not require an individual to wear a face covering as a condition of attendance for in-person instruction, institution-sponsored athletics, institution-sponsored extracurricular activities, in dormitories, or in any other place on a campus of an institution within the system of higher education at any time after the end of the spring semester in 2021.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(3)(c)(iii): Subsection (2)(c)(ii) does not apply to an individual in a medical setting at an institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(4): The board shall enact regulations that require all testimony be given under oath during an employee grievance hearing for a non-faculty employee of an institution of higher education if the grievance hearing relates to the non-faculty employee's:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(4)(a): demotion; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(4)(b): termination.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(5): 76-8-311.1; 53-5-704; 53-5-705 Acknowledging that the Legislature has the authority to regulate, by law, firearms at higher education institutions, the board may:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(5)(a): 76-8-311.1 authorize higher education institutions to establish no more than one secure area at each institution as a hearing room in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(5)(b): 53-5-704; 53-5-705 authorize a higher education institution to make a policy that allows a resident of a dormitory located at the institution to request only roommates who are not licensed to carry a concealed firearm under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(6): 76-8-311.1; 76-8-311.2; 76-8-311.1 In addition to the requirements and penalty prescribed in Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(6)(a): the use of reasonable means such as mechanical, electronic, x-ray, or similar devices, to detect firearms, ammunition, or dangerous weapons contained in the personal property of or on the person of any individual attempting to enter a secure area hearing room;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(6)(b): 76-8-311.1 that an individual required or requested to attend a hearing in a secure area hearing room is notified in writing of the requirements related to entering a secure area hearing room under this Subsection (6)(b) and Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(6)(c): that the restriction of firearms, ammunition, or dangerous weapons in the secure area hearing room is in effect only during the time the secure area hearing room is in use for hearings and for a reasonable time before and after the hearing; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(6)(d): the application of reasonable space limitations to the secure area hearing room as the number of individuals involved in a typical hearing warrants.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(7): The board and institutions may enforce the rules, regulations, and policies described in this section in any reasonable manner, including the assessment of fees, fines, and forfeitures, through:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(7)(a): withholding from money owed the violator;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(7)(b): the imposition of probation, suspension, or expulsion from the institution;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(7)(c): the revocation of privileges;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(7)(d): the refusal to issue certificates, degrees, and diplomas;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(7)(e): judicial process; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-103(7)(f): any reasonable combination of the alternatives described in this Subsection (7).


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-104 Establishment of police or security departments.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-104(1): 53B-1-102 As used in this section, "institution" means an institution listed in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-104(2): An institution's president may establish and maintain police or security departments for the purpose of enforcing the regulations of each institution of higher education and the laws of the state.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-105 Appointment of police or security personnel -- Powers.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-105(1): 53B-1-102 As used in this section, "institution" means an institution listed in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-105(2): An institution shall appoint members of the police or security department of the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-105(3): Upon appointment, members described in Subsection (2) are peace officers and have all the powers of police in cities and of sheriffs, including the power to make arrests on view or on warrant of violation of state statutes and city or county ordinances.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-105(4): Members of the police or security department of any institution also have the power to enforce all rules and regulations that the institution or the board promulgates as related to the institution.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-106 Criminal and traffic laws in full force and effect.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-106(1): All of the criminal laws of this state, including the traffic laws, are in full force and effect on the campuses of state institutions of higher education and upon all other property or facilities owned by the institutions or operated or controlled by the governing board of the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-106(2): Title 41, Chapter 6a, Traffic Code
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-106(2)(a): State institutions of higher education are "political subdivisions" and the board of the institutions is a "local authority."
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-106(2)(b): Title 41, Chapter 6a, Traffic Code All streets, roadways, alleys, and parking lots on property owned or controlled by state institutions of higher education are "streets or highways" as these terms are used in


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-107 Traffic violations -- Notice of rule or regulation.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-107(1): It is a violation of this section for any person to operate or park a vehicle upon any property owned or controlled by a state institution of higher education contrary to posted signs authorized by the published rules and regulations of the institution or to block or impede traffic through or on any of these properties.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-107(2): (1) A violation of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-107(3): Notice of a rule or regulation to all persons is sufficient if the rule or regulation is published in one issue of a newspaper of general circulation in the county or counties in which the institution and the campus or facility is located.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-108 Violation of chapter a misdemeanor.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
A violation of this chapter is a class B misdemeanor.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-109 Jurisdiction of district and justice courts.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Any district court or any justice court of any city or county in which property owned or controlled by a state institution of higher education is located has jurisdiction to hear and determine cases involving an alleged violation of this chapter.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-3-110 Fines and forfeitures -- Disposition.
---------------------------------------------------------------------
All fines and forfeitures collected by any justice court judge and one-half of all the fines and forfeitures collected by the clerk of any district court for a violation of any of this chapter are remitted to the state treasurer to be credited to the general operating fund of the state institution of higher education complaining of the violation.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 4 - Compact for Western Regional Cooperation - Interstate Commission for Higher Education
***********************************************************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-101 WICHE compact.
----------------------------------------------
As empowered by law, the governor of Utah has duly entered into a compact the text of which is as follows:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103 Commissioners -- Duties -- Records of academic progress -- Cancellation of student registration.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(1): The commissioners are the three resident members from the state of Utah, required by Article IV of the compact, and are authorized to function as representatives of the state on the Western Interstate Commission for Higher Education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(2): The commissioners' duties are as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(2)(a): to study the need for professional and graduate educational facilities not available within this state;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(2)(b): to recommend appropriations to meet the needs of this act;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(2)(c): to provide for screening of all applicants for professional, graduate, or higher educational study not available within the state in accordance with established rules; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(2)(d): to certify to out of state institutions under the compact all acceptable candidates.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(3): An applicant may not be certified unless the applicant has been a bona fide resident of the state for at least the five years prior to the date of application.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(4)(a): Students must maintain continuous Utah residency during their attendance at an out of state institution in order to receive financial support under the compact.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(4)(b): If Utah residency is terminated by a student during any academic year in which the student has received financial support under the compact, the support shall be relinquished and terminated at the end of that academic year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(5)(a): The Commissioner of Higher Education shall maintain records of the academic progress of Utah students receiving financial support under the compact while attending out of state institutions.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-4-103(5)(b): If the records reveal a student is not progressing satisfactorily, upon recommendation of the out of state institution, the commissioner shall cancel the student's registration and withhold future payments otherwise due.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 6 - Master Planning
*************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-102 Standardized systems prescribed by the board.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
The board shall prescribe for all institutions under its jurisdiction standardized systems of accounts, records, and reports covering in sufficient detail the operations of the educational institutions under its control.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-104 Multi-University Consortium for Teacher Training in Sensory Impairments -- Purposes -- Appropriation.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-104(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-104(1)(a): In conjunction with the board's master plan for higher education, there is established a Multi-University Consortium for Teacher Training in Sensory Impairments which is an outgrowth of a consortium established by the federal government.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-104(1)(b): The consortium shall include within its membership the University of Utah, Utah State University, Brigham Young University, the Utah Schools for the Deaf and the Blind, the Services for At-Risk Students section under the State Board of Education, and local school districts.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-104(2): The consortium, in collaboration with the board and the State Board of Education, shall develop and implement teacher preparation programs that qualify and certify instructors to work with students who are visually impaired, deaf, or hard of hearing, or both visually impaired and deaf or hard of hearing.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-6-104(3): The board shall consider including within the board's annual budget recommendations a line item appropriation to provide ongoing funding for the programs provided pursuant to this section.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101 Combined requests for appropriations -- Board review of operating budgets -- Submission of budgets -- Recommendations -- Hearing request -- Appropriation formulas -- Allocations -- Dedicated credits -- Financial affairs.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(1): 53B-1-102 As used in this section:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(2)(a): Subject to Subsection (3), the board shall recommend a combined appropriation for the operating budgets of higher education institutions for inclusion in a state appropriations act.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(2)(b): The board's combined budget recommendation shall include:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(2)(b)(iv): statewide and institutional priorities, including scholarships, financial aid, and technology infrastructure; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(2)(b)(v): enrollment growth.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(2)(c): The board's recommendations shall be available for presentation to the governor and to the Legislature at least 30 days before the convening of the Legislature, and shall include schedules showing the recommended amounts for each institution, including separately funded programs or divisions.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(2)(d): The recommended appropriations shall be determined by the board only after the board has reviewed the proposed institutional operating budgets, and has consulted with the various institutions and board staff in order to make appropriate adjustments.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(5)(a): The budget recommendations of the board shall be accompanied by full explanations and supporting data.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(5)(b): The appropriations recommended by the board shall be made with the dual objective of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(5)(b)(i): justifying for higher education institutions appropriations consistent with their needs, and consistent with the financial ability of the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(5)(b)(ii): determining an equitable distribution of funds among the respective institutions in accordance with the aims and objectives of the statewide master plan for higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(6)(a): The board shall request a hearing with the governor on the recommended appropriations.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(6)(b): After the governor delivers his budget message to the Legislature, the board shall request hearings on the recommended appropriations with the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(6)(c): If either the total amount of the state appropriations or its allocation among the institutions as proposed by the Legislature or the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee is substantially different from the recommendations of the board, the board may request further hearings with the Legislature or the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee to reconsider both the total amount and the allocation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(7): The board may devise, establish, periodically review, and revise formulas for the board's use and for the use of the governor and the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee in making appropriation recommendations.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(8):

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(8)(b): Subject to Subsection (13), the board may fix the tuition, fees, and charges for each institution at levels the board finds necessary to meet budget requirements.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(9): Money allocated to each institution by legislative appropriation may be budgeted in accordance with institutional work programs approved by the board, provided that the expenditures funded by appropriations for each institution are kept within the appropriations for the applicable period.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(10): The dedicated credits, including revenues derived from tuitions, fees, federal grants, and proceeds from sales received by the institutions are appropriated to the respective institutions to be used in accordance with institutional work programs.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(11): An institution may do the institution's own purchasing, issue the institution's own payrolls, and handle the institution's own financial affairs under the general supervision of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-101(12): If the Legislature appropriates money in accordance with this section, the money shall be distributed to the board and higher education institutions to fund the items described in Subsection (2)(b).

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-102 Fiscal year.
--------------------------------------------
The fiscal year for each institution and for the board begins on July 1 and ends on June 30 in each year.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103 Board designated state educational agent for federal contracts and aid -- Individual research grants -- Powers of institutions or foundations under authorized programs.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103(1)(a): The board is the designated state educational agency authorized to negotiate and contract with the federal government and to accept financial or other assistance from the federal government or any of its agencies in the name of and in behalf of the state of Utah, under terms and conditions as may be prescribed by congressional enactment designed to further higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103(1)(b): Nothing in this chapter alters or limits the authority of the Division of Facilities Construction and Management to act as the designated state agency to administer programs on behalf of and accept funds from federal, state, and other sources, for capital facilities for the benefit of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103(2): (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103(2)(a): Subject to policies and procedures established by the board, an institution of higher education and the institution of higher education's employees may apply for and receive grants or research and development contracts within the educational role of the recipient institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103(2)(b): (2)(a) A program described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103(3): (3)(c); (3)(c) An institution or the institution's foundation or organization engaged in a program authorized by the board may do the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103(3)(a): enter into contracts with federal, state, or local governments or their subsidiary agencies or departments, with private organizations, companies, firms, or industries, or with individuals for conducting the authorized programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103(3)(b): subject to the approval of the controlling state agency, conduct authorized programs within any of the penal, corrective, or custodial institutions of this state and engage the voluntary participation of inmates in those programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103(3)(c): accept contributions, grants, or gifts from, and enter into contracts and cooperative agreements with, any private organization, company, firm, industry, or individual, or any governmental agency or department, for support of authorized programs within the educational role of the recipient institution, and may agree to provide matching funds with respect to those programs from resources available to the institution; and

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103.5 Uses of revenue for athletic gender equity.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Beginning on July 1, 1998, a state institution of higher education shall annually use for the purposes described in Title IX of the Education Amendments of 1972, 20 U.S.C. Sec. 1681 et seq., an amount of revenue equal to the total amount of sales and use tax revenue collected underUtah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103.5(1): during the one-year period beginning on July 1, 1997, and ending on June 30, 1998; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-103.5(2): on amounts paid for admission to athletic events at the institution of higher education.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-104 Retention of net reimbursed overhead revenues.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-104(1): For fiscal year 1990-91 and for each succeeding year, all budget documents for the system of higher education shall reflect retention by the institutions within the system of their net reimbursed overhead revenues for support of research and related programs under policies established by the board. These overhead revenues may not be considered a dedicated credit.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-104(2): The board, in conjunction with institutions within the system, shall provide the Legislature, through the Office of Legislative Fiscal Analyst, with a complete accounting of the net reimbursed overhead revenues on an annual basis.  This accounting shall include actual expenditures for the prior fiscal year, budgeted expenditures for the current fiscal year, and planned expenditures for the following fiscal year.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-105 Higher education cost disclosure.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-105(1): (1)(a); (b) Each institution within the Utah system of higher education shall, at the time of registration, plainly disclose to all of the institution's undergraduate resident students the following amounts, in dollar figures for a full-time equivalent student:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-105(1)(a): the full cost of instruction;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-105(1)(b): the amount collected from student tuition and fees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-105(1)(c): (1)(a); (b) the difference between the amounts described under Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-105(2): (1)(c) The disclosure under Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106 Personal use expenditures for officers and employees of institutions of higher education.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1): 53B-1-102; 51-7-3 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(a): "Employee" means a person who is not an elected or appointed officer and who is employed on a full- or part-time basis by an institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(b): 53B-1-102 "Institution of higher education" means an institution that is part of the state system of higher education as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(c): "Officer" means a person who is elected or appointed to an office or position within an institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(i): "Personal use expenditure" means an expenditure made without the authority of law that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(i)(A): is not directly related to the performance of an activity as an officer or employee of an institution of higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(i)(B): primarily furthers a personal interest of an officer or employee of an institution of higher education or the family, a friend, or an associate of an officer or employee of an institution of higher education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(i)(C): would constitute taxable income under federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(ii): "Personal use expenditure" does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(ii)(A): a de minimis or incidental expenditure; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(d)(ii)(B): a state vehicle or a monthly stipend for a vehicle that an officer or employee uses to travel to and from the officer or employee's official duties, including a minimal allowance for a detour as provided by the institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(1)(e): 51-7-3 "Public funds" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(2): An officer or employee of an institution of higher education may not:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(2)(a): use public funds for a personal use expenditure; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(2)(b): incur indebtedness or liability on behalf of, or payable by, an institution of higher education for a personal use expenditure.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(3): (2); (3)(b) If the institution of higher education determines that an officer or employee of an institution of higher education has intentionally made a personal use expenditure in violation of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(3)(a): require the officer or employee to deposit the amount of the personal use expenditure into the fund or account from which:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(3)(a)(i): the personal use expenditure was disbursed; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(3)(a)(ii): payment for the indebtedness or liability for a personal use expenditure was disbursed;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(3)(b): require the officer or employee to remit an administrative penalty in an amount equal to 50% of the personal use expenditure to the institution of higher education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(3)(c): (3)(b) deposit the money received under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(4): (2); (4)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(4)(a): (2) Any officer or employee of an institution of higher education who has been found by the institution of higher education to have made a personal use expenditure in violation of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(4)(b): (4)(a) The institution of higher education shall establish an appeal process for an appeal made under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(5): (5)(b); (2); (3); (4); (2)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(5)(a): (5)(b); (2); (3) Subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-106(5)(b): (4); (2) If the officer or employee has requested an appeal under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-501 Purpose.
----------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-501(1): The Legislature recognizes that community colleges and established branch campuses and centers throughout the state have a special mission to provide comprehensive higher education opportunities for financially needy students, at geographically disbursed locations and at favorable tuition rates.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-501(2): The Legislature further recognizes that tuition and general fee costs to students at Utah community colleges and established branch campuses and centers represent significant challenges for many of the students they serve, and that additional scholarship money for financially needy students attending those institutions is needed to ensure financial access to higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-501(3): It is the purpose of this part to establish a program of matching grants as an incentive for institutions to raise money for scholarships at community colleges, branch campuses, and centers.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-601(2)(b): terms of a grant, gift, or contract require the funds to be deposited in the foreign country.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-601(3): 51-7-18 The foreign depository institution in which funds are deposited under this section shall meet the requirements of rules made by the State Money Management Council under Section

--------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704 Reporting of estimated revenue growth from targeted jobs.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(1): On or before October 1, 2030 and each subsequent fifth year, the Department of Workforce Services shall report to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee on:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(1)(a): the total wages in Utah according to the Quarterly Census of Employment and Wages program over the previous five years;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(1)(b): total wages in Utah attributable to four- and five-star jobs that require postsecondary training according to the Occupational Employment and Wage Statistics program over the previous five years;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(1)(c): total wages in Utah for all occupations according to the Occupational Employment and Wage Statistics program over the previous five years;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(1)(d): the quotient of total wages in Subsection (1)(a) and total wages in Subsection (1)(b); and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(1)(e): the quotient of total wages in Subsection (1)(c) and total wages in Subsection (1)(b).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2): On or before October 1, 2030 and each subsequent fifth year, the commissioner shall report to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee on:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(a): all institutions' high yield awards over the previous five years;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(b): the estimated revenue growth from targeted jobs associated with high yield awards over the previous five years;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(c): the connection between the data described in Subsections (2)(a) and (2)(b); and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-704(2)(d): the estimated median effective income tax rate.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705 Determination of full new performance funding amount -- Role of appropriations subcommittee -- Program review.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(1): In accordance with this section, and based on money deposited into the account, the Legislature shall, as part of the higher education appropriations budget process, annually determine the full new performance funding amount for each:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(1)(a): degree-granting institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(1)(b): technical college.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(2): The Legislature shall annually allocate:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(2)(a): 80% of the money in the account to degree-granting institutions; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(2)(b): 20% of the money in the account to technical colleges.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(3)(a): The Legislature shall determine a degree-granting institution's full new performance funding amount based on the degree-granting institution's prior year share of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(3)(a)(i): full-time equivalent enrollment in all degree-granting institutions; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(3)(a)(ii): the total state-funded appropriated budget for all degree-granting institutions.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(3)(b): In determining a degree-granting institution's full new performance funding amount, the Legislature shall give equal weight to the factors described in Subsections (3)(a)(i) and (ii).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(4)(a): The Legislature shall determine a technical college's full new performance funding amount based on the technical college's prior year share of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(4)(a)(i): full-time equivalent enrollment for all technical colleges; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(4)(a)(ii): the total state-funded appropriated budget for all technical colleges.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(4)(b): In determining a technical college's full new performance funding amount, the Legislature shall give equal weight to the factors described in Subsections (4)(a)(i) and (ii).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(5): Annually, at least 30 days before the first day of the legislative general session the board shall submit a report to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee on each degree-granting institution's and each technical college's performance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(6): 53B-7-706; 53B-7-706; 53B-7-706; 53B-7-706
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(6)(a): In accordance with this Subsection (6), and based on the report described in Subsection (5), the Legislature shall determine for each degree-granting institution and each technical college:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(6)(a)(ii): the amount of new performance funding to recommend that the Legislature appropriate, from the account, to the degree-granting institution or technical college.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(6)(b): 53B-7-706 A degree-granting institution or technical college earns the full new performance funding amount if the degree-granting institution or technical college meets the annual performance goals the board sets under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-705(6)(c): 53B-7-706; 53B-7-706 A degree-granting institution or technical college that does not meet the goals the board sets under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709 Five-year performance goals.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1): 53B-7-706(2)(a)(ii)(A); 53B-7-706(2)(c); 53B-7-706(2)(a)(ii)(C); 53B-1-102; 53B-7-706(2)(a)(ii)(B) As used in this section:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(c): "Cohort" means a group of students, defined by the year in which the group enrolls in an institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(d): "Five-year performance period" means the five-year period beginning on July 1, 2022, and ending on June 30, 2027.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(e): 53B-7-706(2)(c) "High-yield award" means the same as that term is defined in board policy under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(f): 53B-7-706(2)(a)(ii)(C) "High-yield awards metric" means the metric described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(g): 53B-1-102 "Institution" means an institution of higher education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(h): "Standard completion time" means the time in which a student typically completes an award program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(i): "System" means the Utah System of Higher Education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(1)(j): 53B-7-706(2)(a)(ii)(B) "Timely completion metric" means the metric described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(2): 53B-7-706(1)(a)(ii) The goals established by the board in accordance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(2)(a): for the access metric, to increase the percent of Utah high school graduates participating in the system by 3.0%;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(2)(b): for the timely completion metric, to increase the system percentage of a cohort that completes an award in up to and including 1.5 times the standard completion time by 3.0%; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(2)(c): for the high-yield awards metric, to increase the system percentage of high-yield awards by 3.0%.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(3): (2) In order to meet the system goals described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(3)(a): for the access metric, to increase the institution's share of Utah high school graduates participating in the system by a percentage that the board determines;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(3)(b): for the timely completion metric, to increase the percent of a cohort enrolled at the institution that completes an award in up to and including 1.5 times the standard completion time or sooner by a percentage that the board determines; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-709(3)(c): for the high-yield awards metric, to increase the percent of high-yield awards the institution grants by a percentage that the board determines.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-801 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part, "endowment"  means the Higher Education Student Success Endowment created in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802 Higher Education Student Success Endowment.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(1): There is created the Higher Education Student Success Endowment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(2): The endowment consists of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(2)(a): the proceeds from divestment of the dissolved Utah Higher Education Assistance Authority's loan portfolio;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(2)(b): appropriations made to the endowment by the Legislature, if any;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(2)(c): income from the investment of the endowment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(2)(d): other revenues received from other sources.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(3): The board shall account for the receipt and expenditures of endowment money in accordance with the policies and guidance of the Division of Finance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(a): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(a)(i): The state treasurer shall invest the endowment money with the primary goal of providing for stability, income, and growth of the principal.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(a)(ii): The state treasurer may deduct any administrative costs incurred in managing endowment assets from earnings before distributing the earnings.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(b): Nothing in this section requires a specific outcome in investing.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(c): The state treasurer may employ professional asset managers to assist in the investment of assets of the endowment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(d): The state treasurer may only provide compensation to asset managers from earnings generated by the endowment's investments.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(e): The state treasurer shall invest and manage the endowment assets as a prudent investor would, by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(e)(i): considering the purposes, terms, distribution requirements, and other circumstances of the endowment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(e)(ii): exercising reasonable care, skill, and caution in order to meet the standard of care of a prudent investor.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(f): In determining whether or not the state treasurer has met the standard of care of a prudent investor, the judge or finder of fact shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(f)(i): consider the state treasurer's actions in light of the facts and circumstances existing at the time of the investment decision or action, and not by hindsight; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(4)(f)(ii): evaluate the state treasurer's investment and management decisions respecting individual assets not in isolation, but in context of an endowment portfolio as a whole as a part of an overall investment strategy that has risk and return objectives reasonably suited to the endowment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(5)(a): The endowment shall earn interest.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(5)(b): The state treasurer shall deposit the interest or other revenue earned from investment of the endowment into the endowment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(6): 53B-1-402(2)(a); 53B-2-101 The board:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(6)(a): 53B-1-402(2)(a); 53B-2-101 may expend money from the endowment for programs that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(6)(a)(i): 53B-1-402(2)(a) advance the system priorities as established in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(6)(a)(ii): 53B-2-101 support prospective students or current students enrolled at an institution, as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(6)(b): may not expend money from the endowment for a capital expenditure, including the construction or lease of a capital facility or operation and maintenance of a capital facility.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(7): 53B-1-402(2)(a) The board shall ensure that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(7)(a): 53B-1-402(2)(a) money deposited into the endowment is irrevocable and is expended only for programs that advance the system priorities as established in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-802(7)(b): creditors of the board of directors may not seize, attach, or otherwise obtain assets of the endowment.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803 Board duties.
---------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1): 53B-7-802 The board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1)(a): act as trustee of the endowment and exercise the state's fiduciary responsibilities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1)(b): meet at least twice a year to conduct business on behalf of the endowment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1)(c): review and approve all endowment policies, projections, rules, criteria, procedures, forms, standards, and performance goals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1)(d): 53B-7-802 review and approve the budget and expenditures for the endowment in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1)(e): review financial records for the endowment, including endowment receipts, expenditures, and investments; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(1)(f): take any other action necessary to perform the board's fiduciary obligations.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-803(2): The board shall annually submit a budget and expenditures to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee no later than November 1.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-804 State grants to the authority.
--------------------------------------------------------------
To the extent otherwise allowed, a state entity may grant money or property to the endowment.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-7-805 Gifts to the endowment.
-------------------------------------------------------
A person may make a contribution, gift, grant, bequest, or devise, or loans to the endowment.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-8-102 Definitions -- Resident student status -- Exceptions.
