Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 13 - Higher Education Loan Act
************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-101 Short title of chapter.
--------------------------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Higher Education Loan Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-102 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-102(1): "Bonds" means the bonds authorized to be issued by the board under this chapter, and may consist of bonds, notes, or debt obligations evidencing an obligation to repay borrowed money and payable solely from revenues and other money of the board pledged for repayment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-102(2): "Eligible borrower" means a person, or the parent of a person, who is eligible to borrow under regulations applicable to the student loan program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-102(3): "Eligible institution" means an institution which is approved by the board and the United States Secretary of Education for purposes of the guaranteed loan program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-102(4): "Obligations" means student loan notes and other debt obligations reflecting loans to students which the board may take, acquire, buy, sell, or endorse under this chapter, and may include a direct or indirect interest in the whole or any part of the notes or obligations.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-102(5): "Resolution," when used in relation to the issuance of bonds, means the resolution or trust agreement securing the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-102(6): "Student" means a person who, under rules promulgated by the board, is enrolled or accepted for enrollment at an eligible institution and who is making suitable progress in his education toward obtaining a degree or other appropriate certification in accordance with standards acceptable to the board.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103 Powers of Utah Board of Higher Education.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
The Utah Board of Higher Education has the powers necessary to carry out the purposes of this chapter, including the following:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(1): to accept gifts, grants, loans, and other aids or amounts from a person, corporation, or governmental agency;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(2): to loan money to eligible borrowers to assist them in obtaining a post-high school education by attending an eligible institution, including refinancing or consolidating obligations previously incurred by eligible borrowers with other lending sources for this purpose and participating in loans to eligible borrowers for this purpose with other lending sources;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(3): to acquire, purchase, or make commitments to purchase, and take assignments from lenders of obligations.  No obligation is eligible for acquisition, purchase, or commitment to purchase by the board unless at or before the time of transfer to the board the lender certifies either: (a) that, under and to the extent required by rules and regulations of the board, the proceeds of sale or its equivalent shall be reinvested in other obligations under the student loan program; or (b) that the obligation was made in anticipation of its sale to the board under rules and regulations of the board promulgated under this chapter;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(4): to enforce its rights under a contract or agreement including the commencement of court action;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(5): to acquire, hold, and dispose of real and personal property necessary for the accomplishment of the purposes of this chapter;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(6): to obtain insurance against losses which may be incurred in connection with its property, assets, activities, or the exercise of the powers granted under this chapter;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(7): to borrow money and to issue its bonds and provide for the rights of bondholders and to secure the bonds by assignment, pledge, or granting a security interest in its property including all or a part of an obligation.  The state is not liable for the repayment of bonds issued by the board.  The bonds issued by the board are not a debt of the state, and each bond shall contain on its face a statement to this effect;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(8): to invest funds not required for immediate use or disbursement as provided in the State Money Management Act;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(9): subject to a contract with the holders of its bonds, an applicable bond resolution, or a contract with the recipient of a loan, to consent to the modification, with respect to security, rate of interest, time of payment of interest or principal, or other term of a bond contract or agreement between the board and a recipient of a loan, bondholder, or agency or institution guaranteeing the repayment of an obligation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(10): to engage and employ officers, agents, employees, and other private consultants to render and perform professional and technical duties, assistance, and advice in carrying out the purposes of this chapter, to describe their duties, and to fix the amount and source of their compensation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(11): to make rules and regulations governing the activities authorized under this chapter;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(12): to solicit grants and contributions from the public or from any government or governmental agency and to arrange for the guaranteeing of the repayment of obligations by other agencies of this state or the United States;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(13): to collect fees and charges in connection with its loans, commitments, and servicing, including reimbursement of the costs of financing, service charges, and insurance premiums which are determined as reasonable and are approved by the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(14): to sell obligations held by the board at such prices and at such times as it may determine, when that sale would not impair the rights or interests of holders of bonds issued by the board; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-103(15): to participate in federal programs supporting loans to eligible borrowers and to agree to, and comply with, the conditions of those programs.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104 Issuance of bonds -- Disposition of funds -- Refunding bonds -- Resolution to authorize bonds -- Contents -- Sale of bonds -- Bond debt service reserve funds -- Restoration of fund assets -- Establishment of other subfunds.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(1): The board may issue its bonds in the principal amounts necessary to provide funds for achieving its purposes under this chapter, including the payment of interest, the establishment of reserves to secure the bonds, and other expenditures of the board necessary to carry out its purposes and powers.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(2): The board may issue refunding bonds when it considers refunding expedient, whether the bonds to be refunded have or have not matured.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(3): The proceeds of the refunding bonds shall be applied to the purchase, redemption, or payment of the bonds refunded.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(4): Except as otherwise expressly provided in a resolution authorizing bonds, an issue of bonds is a special obligation of the board to be satisfied only out of revenue or money of the board, subject to an agreement with the holders of particular receipts or revenues of the board which have been pledged.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(5): The board shall authorize its bonds by resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(6): The bonds are fully negotiable for all purposes, shall bear a date, shall be serial bonds or term bonds or both and, if serial bonds, shall be payable either semiannually or annually, and shall mature at a time or times, not exceeding 40 years after the date of issue, as provided in the resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(7): The resolution shall specify the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(7)(a): either the interest rate or rates or a formula by means of which the interest rate or rates are determined during the time the bonds are outstanding;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(7)(b): denomination and form, either coupon or registered;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(7)(c): registration privileges;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(7)(d): manner of execution;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(7)(e): medium of payment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(7)(f): place and terms for the redemption of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(8): If the resolution sets forth a formula by means of which the interest rate or rates on the bonds are determined, it shall also state the maximum rate which the bonds may bear under the formula.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(9): Pursuant to the resolution or another instrument, the board may delegate to the chair, vice-chair, or chair of the Budget and Finance Subcommittee the authority:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(9)(a): to approve any changes with respect to interest rate, price, amount, redemption features, and other terms of the bonds as are within reasonable parameters set forth in the resolution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(9)(b): to approve and execute all documents relating to the issuance of the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(10): The bonds are sold by the board in such manner and at such a price as the board determines.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(11): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(11)(a): The board may create and establish one or more bond debt service reserve funds in order to secure its bonds from the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(11)(a)(i): any proceeds of the sale of bonds, to the extent provided in the resolution authorizing the issuance of the bonds;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(11)(a)(ii): any money appropriated and made available by the state for the purpose of the funds; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(11)(a)(iii): any other money available to the board for the purpose of the funds.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(11)(b): All money held in any bond debt service reserve fund shall be used, as provided in the resolution establishing the fund, to pay principal of, premium, and interest on bonds of the board issued under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(11)(c): If the assets in any bond debt service reserve fund are less than the amount currently required in the authorizing resolution to be on deposit, the chairman of the board shall, annually before the second day of December, certify to the governor and to the director of finance the amount necessary to restore the assets of the funds to the required amount.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(11)(d): The governor may request from the Legislature an appropriation of the certified amount in order to restore the required amount to the funds.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-104(12): The board may create and establish any other subfunds and accounts as may be necessary for its corporate purposes.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-105 Agreements with bondholders unalterable.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-105(1): Neither limitations or alterations of the rights vested in the board to fulfill the terms of an agreement made with bondholders nor impairment of the rights and remedies of those bondholders may occur until:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-105(1)(a): the bonds, together with interest on the bonds and interest on unpaid installments of interest are met and discharged; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-105(1)(b): all costs and expenses in connection with an action or proceeding by or on behalf of those bondholders are met and discharged.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-105(2): The board may include provisions to this effect in an agreement with the holders of the bonds.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-106 Investments in bonds of the board.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
The bonds of the board are securities, in which public officers and bodies of this state, municipalities and municipal subdivisions, insurance companies and associations, persons carrying on an insurance business, banks, trust companies, savings banks and savings associations, saving and loan associations, investment companies, administrators, guardians, executors, trustees, other fiduciaries, and all other persons who are authorized to invest in bonds or other obligations of the state, may properly and legally invest funds, including capital, in their control or belonging to them.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-107 Payment of funds -- Payment on warrants -- Contracts with bondholders -- Security.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-107(1): The funds of the board, except as otherwise authorized or provided in this section, are paid to the state treasurer.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-107(2): The money in the accounts is paid out on warrants signed by the State Division of Finance on requisition of the chairman of the board or of a board authorized officer or employee.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-107(3): The board, subject to the approval of the state treasurer, may contract with the holders of its bonds as to the custody, collection, securing, investment, and payment of money of the board or of money held in trust or otherwise for the payment of bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-107(4): Money held in trust or otherwise for the payment of bonds or to secure bonds and deposits of the money may be secured in the same manner as money of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-107(5): Banks and trust companies are authorized to give such security for the deposits.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-108 Bonds and interest exempt from taxation except corporate franchise tax.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The bonds issued under this chapter and the interest on the bonds are exempt from all taxation in this state, except for the corporate franchise tax.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-109 Board pledges -- Attachment of lien -- Recording unnecessary.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-109(1): A pledge made by the board is valid and binding from the time the pledge is made.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-109(2): The money or property pledged and subsequently received by the board is immediately subject to the lien of the pledge without physical delivery or further act.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-109(3): The lien of the pledge is valid and binding against all parties having a claim in tort, contract, or otherwise against the board, irrespective of whether the parties have notice of the claim.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-109(4): Neither the resolution nor another instrument by which a pledge is created need be recorded.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-110 Default by board -- Appointment of a trustee -- Powers of the trustee and bondholders.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-110(1): If the board defaults in the payment of principal of or interest on an issue of bonds after the issue becomes due, whether at maturity or upon call for redemption, and the default continues for 30 days, or if the board fails or refuses to comply with this chapter, or defaults in an agreement made with the holders of an issue of bonds, the holders of 25% of the aggregate principal amount of the bonds of the issue then outstanding, may appoint a trustee to represent all holders of that issue of bonds for the purposes provided in this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-110(2): The trustee may, and upon written request of the holders of 25% of the aggregate principal amount of the bonds of the issue then outstanding shall, in his own name by action or proceeding enforce all rights of the bondholders including the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-110(2)(a): bringing an action to require the board to collect fees, charges, interest, and amortization payments of loans made by it adequate to carry out the agreement as to, or pledge of, the fees, charges, interest, and amortization payment on the loans and other properties;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-110(2)(b): bringing an action to require the board to carry out other agreements with the holders of the bonds and to perform its duties under this chapter;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-110(2)(c): bringing an action upon the bonds; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-110(2)(d): bringing an action to require the board to account as if it were the trustee of an express trust for the holders of the bonds due and payable, and if all defaults are made good, then, with the consent of the holders of 25% of the principal amount of the issue of bonds then outstanding, to annul the declaration and its consequences.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-110(3): The holders of bonds and the trustee authorized by this section shall have all of the rights to which they are entitled by virtue of provisions included in the bonds or otherwise available to them under law.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-111 Loans or purchase of obligations -- Rules -- Options -- Repayment of federally insured loans.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-111(1): The board may purchase obligations from lenders or make loans to eligible borrowers, out of money available to the board for loans.  The board shall promulgate rules for determining the needs of the respective borrowers for loans and for the purpose of making loans or purchasing obligations.  The amount of an obligation purchased by the board or of a loan made by the board to an eligible borrower, whether enrolled or to be enrolled in a private institution or a tax-supported public institution, is determined by the board upon the basis of substantially similar standards and guides set forth in the board's rules.  The board, in determining the needs of eligible borrowers for guaranteed loans, may consider the amount of assistance available to the students.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-111(2): When the board purchases an obligation or makes a loan, and again immediately before a repayment schedule on the loan or obligation is signed by the borrower, the board shall cause a written statement to be delivered to the borrower describing in detail whether an option exists and, if so, who may exercise the option, under what conditions the option may be exercised, and what options are available relating to the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-111(2)(a): the term of the loan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-111(2)(b): the repayment period on the loan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-111(2)(c): an extension of the term or repayment period on the loan and the conditions of repayment under the extension;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-111(2)(d): a deferment or forbearance on the repayment of the loan or on interest accruing on the loan, whether interest is to be paid during the deferment or forbearance, and the terms of repayment after the deferment or forbearance;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-111(2)(e): the period of time between installment payments on the loan and whether graduated or unequal installment payments may be made;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-111(2)(f): the minimum annual payment on the loan, and if more than one loan is taken from the board or if the borrower takes or has taken an educational loan from another source, the availability of consolidation, transfer, or assignment of the loans and the minimum annual payment on the aggregate of the loans;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-111(2)(g): the granting of an interview before or at the time the borrower signs a repayment schedule; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-111(2)(h): the revision or renegotiation of the repayment schedule on the loan after repayment has commenced, or if other educational loans from the board or another source are taken after the repayment has commenced.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-111(3): On obligations purchased or loans made by the board which are federally insured loans, the board may establish variable repayment schedules conforming to the need and documented income levels of borrowers, if the schedules are not inconsistent with federal laws, rules, or regulations governing the insured loans.  A borrower making payments on a loan may request and be granted a revised repayment term or schedule based upon the established variable repayment schedules.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-112 Separation of duties, responsibilities, funds, liabilities, and expenses -- Immunity from personal liability.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-112(1): The duties, responsibilities, funds, liabilities, and expenses of the board under this chapter shall be maintained wholly separate and apart from their other duties, responsibilities, funds, liabilities, and expenses.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-112(2): A member of the board or a person executing the notes, bonds, or other obligations of the board is not personally liable for the repayment of the note, bond, or other obligation or subject to personal liability or accountability by reason of its issuance or nonissuance.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-113 Bond approval by attorney general incontestable after 30 days -- Recital of certification.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-113(1): The attorney general shall examine the resolutions and proceedings authorizing the issuance and confirming the sale of bonds under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-113(2): Once examined and certified as legal obligations by the attorney general, the bonds become incontestable in any court in the state unless suit is brought in a court having jurisdiction within 30 days from the date of certification.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-113(3): The bonds certified under this section shall contain a recital on their face as follows: "This bond is one of a series of bonds which were certified as legal obligations by the Attorney General of the state of Utah on _______________."
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-113(4): Bonds authorized, issued, and sold under resolutions and proceedings certified by the attorney general are valid and binding obligations according to their terms.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-114 Mandamus in Supreme Court -- Precedence.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-114(1): If an official required by the proceeding authorizing bonds under this chapter to sign the bonds refuses to affix his signature to them, or if the attorney general refuses to certify the bonds as legal obligations, alleging illegality of the bonds, the board may bring an original action in mandamus in the Supreme Court of Utah.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13-114(2): The importance to the state and its inhabitants of the program of loans to eligible borrowers is such that this action brought in the Supreme Court should be given precedence over the other matters pending before the court, and the court is requested to give this action precedence and to render its decision concerning it at the earliest possible time.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 13a - Utah Promise Program Act
************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102 Definitions.
----------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(1)(a): "Cost of attendance" means the estimated costs associated with attending an institution, as established by the institution in accordance with board policies.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(1)(b): "Cost of attendance" includes costs payable to the institution, other direct educational expenses, transportation, and living expenses while attending the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(2): 53B-8-102; 53B-8-106
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(2)(a): 53B-8-102; 53B-8-106 "Eligible student" means a financially needy student who is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(2)(a)(i): unconditionally admitted to and enrolled at a Utah postsecondary institution on at least a half-time basis, as defined by the board, in an eligible postsecondary program leading to a defined education or training objective, as defined by the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(2)(a)(ii): making satisfactory academic progress, as defined by the institution in published policies or rules, toward an education or training objective; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(2)(a)(iii): 53B-8-102; 53B-8-106
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(2)(a)(iii)(A): 53B-8-102 a resident student under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(2)(a)(iii)(B): 53B-8-106 exempt from paying the nonresident portion of total tuition under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(2)(b): "Eligible student" does not include a graduate student.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(3): "Financially needy student" means a student who demonstrates the financial inability to meet all or a portion of the cost of attendance at an institution for any period of attendance as defined by the board, after considering the student's expected family contribution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(4): "Fiscal year" means the fiscal year of the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(5): 53B-13a-106 "Partner award" means a financial award described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(6): "Program" means the Utah Promise Program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(7): 53B-13a-106 "Promise partner" means an employer that participates in the program described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(8): 53B-1-102 "Utah postsecondary institution" or "institution" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(8)(a): 53B-1-102 an institution of higher education listed in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-102(8)(b): a Utah private, nonprofit postsecondary institution that is accredited by an accrediting organization that the United States Department of Education recognizes.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-103 Utah Promise Program -- Annual report.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-103(1): The Legislature finds that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-103(1)(a): the prosperity, economic success, and general welfare of the people of Utah and of the state are directly related to the educational levels and skills of the citizens of the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-103(1)(b): financial assistance, to bridge the gap between a financially needy student's resources and the cost of attendance at a Utah postsecondary institution, is a necessary component for ensuring access to postsecondary education and training.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-103(2): There is created the Utah Promise Program to provide financial assistance to students.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-103(3): The board shall annually submit an electronic report to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee regarding the Utah Promise Program.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104 Promise grants.
-------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(1)(a): As part of the Utah Promise Program and in accordance with this section, the board shall allocate available money to each institution to use to award promise grants to eligible students to pay the eligible student's cost of attendance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(1)(b): An eligible student may apply for a promise grant in accordance with procedures established by board rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(1)(c): The amount of a promise grant to an eligible student may not exceed the amount equal to the difference between:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(1)(c)(i): the eligible student's cost of attendance; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(1)(c)(ii): the total value of other financial aid that the eligible student receives toward the eligible student's cost of attendance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(1)(d): An eligible student may transfer a promise grant to one or more other institutions.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(2): In administering this section, the board shall use a packaging approach that ensures that institutions combine loans, grants, employment, and family and individual contributions toward financing the cost of attendance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(3): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; (1) In accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(3)(a): an application process;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(3)(b): eligibility criteria, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(3)(b)(i): criteria related to academic achievement and enrollment status; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(3)(b)(ii): a requirement that an applicant demonstrate completion of the Free Application for Federal Student Aid, unless the student or the student's parent opts out in accordance with board rule;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(3)(c): how a student demonstrates financial need;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(3)(d): (1) a formula to determine the allocation of money to institutions in accordance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(3)(d)(i): the cost of attendance for programs offered by institutions; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(3)(d)(ii): the number of eligible students who attend each institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(3)(e): a methodology for prioritizing award of promise grants based primarily on financial need.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(4): A student is eligible for a promise grant until the student:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(4)(a): earns a first bachelor's degree; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(4)(b): completes 120 credit hours.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(5): The board or an institution may not represent to a recipient or a potential recipient of a promise grant that promise grants will remain available in perpetuity.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(6)(a): The board may require an institution to enter into a participation agreement before the institution may award promise grants.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(6)(b): In a participation agreement, the board shall include a requirement that the institution:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(6)(b)(i): provide to the board information necessary to administer the promise grants;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(6)(b)(ii): comply with this section and board rules related to the promise grants;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(6)(b)(iii): submit reports related to the promise grants as required by board rule; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(6)(b)(iv): cooperate in any review or financial audit related to the promise grants that the board determines necessary.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(7): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(7)(a): The board may use up to 2% of the money appropriated for promise grants for costs related to administering the promise grants.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(7)(b): An institution may use up to 3% of the money the institution receives for promise grants for costs related to administering the promise grants.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-104(8): The board may supplement state appropriations for the program with private contributions.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106 Utah promise partners.
--------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(1): As part of the Utah Promise Program, the board may select employers to be promise partners.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(2): (6) The board may select an employer as a promise partner if the employer:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(2)(a): applies to the board to be a promise partner; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(2)(b): (6) meets other requirements established by the board in the rules described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(3): (3) An individual employed by, or who is a dependent of an employee of, a promise partner is eligible to receive a partner award if the individual:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(3)(a): applies for a partner award;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(3)(b): is admitted to and enrolled in an institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(3)(c): (3) maintains the eligibility requirements described in this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(4): (4)(b); (3); (6)(a); (3); (3)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(4)(a): (4)(b); (3) Subject to legislative appropriations and Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(4)(b): (6)(a); (3) The board may:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(4)(b)(i): (6)(a) award a partner award for up to the portion of tuition and fees for a program at an institution that is not covered by a promise partnership described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(4)(b)(ii): (3) prioritize awarding partner awards if an appropriation for partner awards is not sufficient to provide a partner award to each individual who is eligible under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(4)(c): (3) The board may continue to award a partner award to a recipient who meets the requirements described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(4)(c)(i): four years after the day on which the individual initially receives a partner award;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(4)(c)(ii): when the recipient uses a partner award to attend an institution for eight semesters; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(4)(c)(iii): when the recipient completes an approved program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(5): The board may name a specific promise grant after the donating business.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(6): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act In accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(6)(a): a process for a business to seek and receive approval from the board to become a promise partner, including providing funds for tuition and fees to be distributed under the Utah Promise Program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(6)(b): a process for an individual to apply for a partner award; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(6)(c): criteria for the board to prioritize awarding partner awards to individuals.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13a-106(7): The board may allow an individual to apply directly to the board for a partner award.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 13b - Veterans Tuition Gap Program Act
********************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-101 Title.
----------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Veterans Tuition Gap Program Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102 Definitions.
----------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(1): "Federal program" means a veterans educational assistance program established in:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(1)(a): United States Code,
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(1)(b): United States Code,
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(1)(c): United States Code,
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(1)(d): United States Code,
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(1)(e): United States Code,
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(2): 53B-2-101(1) "Institution of higher education" or "institution" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(2)(a): 53B-2-101(1) an institution of higher education listed in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(2)(b): a private, nonprofit, postsecondary institution located in Utah that is accredited by an accrediting organization that the United States Department of Education recognizes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(3): "Program" means the Veterans Tuition Gap Program created in this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(4): 68-3-12.5; 53B-8-102
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(4)(a): 68-3-12.5; 53B-8-102 "Qualifying military veteran" means a veteran, as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(4)(a)(i): 53B-8-102 is a resident student under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(4)(a)(ii): is accepted into an institution and enrolled in a program leading to a bachelor's degree;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(4)(a)(iii): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(4)(a)(iii)(A): has exhausted the federal benefit under a federal program; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(4)(a)(iii)(B): demonstrates that the veteran no longer qualifies to receive federal benefits under any federal program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(4)(a)(iv): has not completed a bachelor's degree.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-102(4)(b): "Qualifying military veteran" does not include a family member.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-103 Establishment of the Veterans Tuition Gap Program.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
There is established a Veterans Tuition Gap Program to serve qualifying military veterans with tuition assistance at institutions of higher education when:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-103(1): federal benefits under the federal program have been exhausted or are not available; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-103(2): a qualifying military veteran has not finished a bachelor's degree and is in the final year of a bachelor's degree program.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104 Guidelines for administration of the program.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(1): The board shall use the guidelines in this section to develop policies to implement and administer the program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(2): (3)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(2)(a): The board shall allocate money appropriated for the program to institutions to provide grants for qualifying military veterans.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(2)(b): The board may not use program money for administrative costs or overhead.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(2)(c): An institution may not use more than 3% of its program money for administrative costs or overhead.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(2)(d): (3)(b) Money returned to the board under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(3): (3)(c)(ii); Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; (3)(c)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(3)(a): An institution shall award a program grant to a qualifying military veteran on an annual basis but distribute the money one quarter or semester at a time, with continuing awards contingent upon the qualifying military veteran maintaining satisfactory academic progress as defined by the institution in published policies or rules.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(3)(b): At the conclusion of the academic year, money distributed to an institution that was not awarded to a qualifying military veteran or used for allowed administrative purposes shall be returned to the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(3)(c): (3)(c)(ii); Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; (3)(c)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(3)(c)(i): (3)(c)(ii) To qualify for a program grant under this section, a military veteran shall demonstrate, in accordance with rules described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(3)(c)(ii): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; (3)(c)(i) In accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(3)(c)(ii)(A): provisions for students or parents to opt out of the requirement due to financial ineligibility for any potential grant or other financial aid, personal privacy concerns, or other reasons the board specifies; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(3)(c)(ii)(B): direction for applicants to financial aid advisors.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(4): A qualifying military veteran may receive a program grant until:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(4)(a): the qualifying military veteran completes the requirements for a bachelor's degree; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(4)(b): the qualifying military veteran receives the maximum award that the board sets.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(5): A qualifying military veteran who receives a program grant may use the grant toward tuition, fees, books, education-related supplies, and a housing allowance at an institution of higher education in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-13b-104(6): The board may accept grants, gifts, bequests, and devises of real and personal property from any source for the purpose of awarding grants to qualifying military veterans in addition to those funded by the state.

----------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 14 - Collection of Student Loans
**************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-101 Student loan delinquent or in default -- Authority to collect.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
If a National Direct Student Loan or a student loan made under

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-102 Mailing of notice of default -- Contents of notice.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-102(1): Upon default in payment of a student loan or an installment payment on a student loan, the entity responsible for collecting the loan may send a notice, by certified mail, to the borrower at the borrower's last known address.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-102(2): The notice shall state the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-102(2)(a): the date and amount of the loan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-102(2)(b): the balance of the loan;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-102(2)(c): the amount of delinquent installments and the dates they were due;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-102(2)(d): a demand for immediate payment of delinquent installments;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-102(2)(e): the right of the borrower to file a written response to the notice, to have a hearing, to be represented at the hearing, and to appeal any decision of the hearing examiner;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-102(2)(f): the time within which a written response must be filed; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-102(2)(g): the power of the college, university, or board upon the failure of the borrower to respond or upon a decision of the hearing examiner adverse to the borrower, to obtain an order under this chapter and to execute upon income tax overpayments or refunds of the borrower.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-103 Failure to receive response or payment after notice -- Authority to collect balance.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
If a written response or payment of delinquent installments is not received by the college, university, or board within 15 days from the date of receipt of the notice by the borrower, the college, university, or board may determine the balance due and proceed to collect the balance as provided in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-104 Hearing set after receipt of written notice -- Notice of hearing.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
If a written response to the notice sent under Section

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-105(3): The borrower and college, university, or board may be represented at the hearing by an attorney or other person, and may present evidence, exhibits, testimony, witnesses, and other material regarding the student loan, payments, and default as are relevant.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-105(4): The hearing examiner shall make specific written findings on the student loan, payments, default, and the balance due and shall enter a written order.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-105(5): If the hearing examiner finds the borrower has defaulted, the order shall state the fact of default and the balance due on the loan including interest.  If the examiner finds no default, the order shall dismiss the claim.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-105(6): The findings and order of the hearing examiner are filed with the college, university, or board and copies mailed to the borrower within 10 days after conclusion of the hearing.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-14-105(7): The hearing may be continued by agreement of the parties and approval of the hearing examiner or upon order of the hearing examiner.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 15 - Collection of Student Loans from Public Employees
************************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-101 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-101(1): "Disposable earnings" means the part of an employee's earnings remaining after the deduction of all amounts required by law to be withheld.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-101(2): "Earnings" or "earnings from personal services" means compensation paid or payable for personal services, whether designated as wages, salary, commission, bonus, or otherwise, and includes periodic payments under a pension or retirement program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-101(3): "Public employee" means any employee, officer, or servant of the state of Utah, or any office, department, agency, authority, commission, board, institution, hospital, college, university, or other instrumentality of the state, or of any county, city, town, school district, special improvement or taxing district, or any other political subdivision or public corporation of or within the state.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-102 Collection of defaulted student loan from public employee.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
If a National Direct Student Loan or a student loan made to a public employee under

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-103 Proceedings -- Notice -- Inspection of records -- Repayment -- Hearing.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
When a state college, university, or board determines that a public employee is indebted to the state for debts arising from a defaulted student loan, it may initiate proceedings to collect the debt through deductions from earnings by providing the public employee with the following:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-103(1): 53B-14-102 a minimum of 30 days' written notice as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-103(2): an opportunity to inspect and copy college, university, or board records relating to the debt;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-103(3): an opportunity to enter into a written agreement with the college, university, or board, under terms agreeable to the college, university, or board, to establish a schedule for the repayment of the debt; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-103(4): 53B-14-104; 53B-14-105; 53B-14-107; 53B-14-108 an opportunity for a hearing on the determination of the college, university, or board concerning the existence or the amount of the debt in accordance with Sections


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-104 Lack of response.
--------------------------------------------------
If a written response or payment of delinquent installments is not received by the college, university, or board within 15 days from the date of receipt of the notice by the public employee, the college, university, or board may determine the balance due and proceed to collect the balance as provided in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-105 Filing of abstract of order of default -- Lien -- Deduction from wages.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
An abstract of an order of a hearing examiner stating a default may be filed with the financial officer responsible for payment of the public employee's wages.  When filed, the abstract constitutes a lien against 15% of the disposable earnings due, or to become due, to the public employee to the extent of the balance due plus interest.  The financial officer shall deduct the amount subject to this lien from the public employee's disposable earnings, and remit the deducted amount to the college, university, or board, but no such amount shall be remitted to the college, university, or board until 20 days after the date of the hearing examiner's order.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-106 Personnel information.
-------------------------------------------------------
Upon written request of the state college, university, or board, persons with access to personnel information regarding public employees shall disclose the mailing address of individuals who have defaulted under Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-15-107 Reimbursed costs.
--------------------------------------------------
The public employer may obtain reimbursement for costs incurred in providing the information requested under Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102 Changes in curriculum -- Substantial alterations in institutional operations -- Program approval -- Periodic review of programs -- Career and technical education curriculum changes.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(1): 53B-1-102 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(1)(a): 53B-1-102 "Institution of higher education" means an institution described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(1)(b): "Program of instruction" means a program of curriculum that leads to the completion of a degree, diploma, certificate, or other credential.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(2)(a): Under procedures and policies approved by the board and developed in consultation with each institution of higher education, each institution of higher education may make such changes in the institution of higher education's curriculum as necessary to better effectuate the institution of higher education's primary role; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(2)(b): subject to Subsection (2)(a), an institution of higher education's faculty shall establish and have primary responsibility for the curriculum of a course within a program of instruction at the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(3): The board shall establish criteria for whether an institution of higher education may approve a new program of instruction, including criteria related to whether:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(3)(a): the program of instruction meets identified workforce needs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(3)(b): the institution of higher education is maximizing collaboration with other institutions of higher education to provide for efficiency in offering the program of instruction;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(3)(c): the new program of instruction is within the institution of higher education's mission and role; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(3)(d): the new program of instruction meets other criteria determined by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(4)(a): Except as board policy permits, an institution of higher education may not establish a branch, extension center, college, or professional school.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(4)(b): The president of an institution of higher education may, with the approval of the institution of higher education's board of trustees, establish a new program of instruction that meets the criteria described in Subsection (3), subject to board review for pathway articulation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(5)(a): An institution of higher education shall notify the board of a proposed new program of instruction, including how the proposed new program of instruction meets the criteria described in Subsection (3).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(5)(b): The board shall establish procedures and guidelines for institutional boards of trustees to consider an institutional proposal for a new program of instruction described in Subsection (4)(b).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(6): The president of an institution of higher education may discontinue a program of instruction in accordance with criteria that the president and the institution of higher education's board of trustees establish.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(7): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(7)(a): The board shall conduct a periodic review of all new programs of instruction, including those funded by gifts, grants, and contracts, no later than two years after the first cohort to begin the program of instruction completes the program of instruction.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(7)(b): The board may conduct a periodic review of any program of instruction at an institution of higher education, including a program of instruction funded by a gift, grant, or contract.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(7)(c): The board shall conduct:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(7)(c)(i): at least once every seven years, at least one review described in Subsection (7)(b) of each program of instruction at each institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(7)(c)(ii): annually, a qualitative and quantitative review of academic disciplines across the system, including enrollment, graduation rates, and workforce placement, ensuring that the board conducts a review of all disciplines within the system at least once every seven years.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(7)(d): Following a review described in this Subsection (7) and after providing the relevant institution of higher education an opportunity to respond to the board's review of a given program of instruction, the board may modify, consolidate, or terminate the program of instruction.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(8): In making decisions related to career and technical education curriculum changes, the board shall coordinate on behalf of the boards of trustees of higher education institutions a review of the proposed changes by the State Board of Education to ensure an orderly and systematic career and technical education curriculum that eliminates overlap and duplication of course work with high schools and technical colleges.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(9): The board shall demonstrate compliance with Subsection (7) by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(9)(a): creating a list of programs and corresponding review schedules;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(9)(b): upon request of the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee, providing the list described in Subsection (9)(a); and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(9)(c): providing a written report on or before October 1 to the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee of each year regarding relevant findings from the reviews conducted under Subsection (7).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(10): 53B-7-703; 53B-7-703 On or before October 1, 2026, if the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee finds the board to be out of compliance with Subsection (9), the Legislature shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(10)(a): 53B-7-703 deduct 10% of the appropriation described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-102(10)(b): 53B-7-703 deduct an additional 10% of the appropriation described in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-104(2)(a): a higher education entity, or any part of one, may not submit a proposal in response to the government entity's competitive procurement process; and

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-105 Common course numbering -- Transferability of credits -- Agreement with competency-based general education provider -- Policies.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-105(1): 53B-16-110; 53B-1-102 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-105(1)(a): "Accredited institution" means an institution that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-105(1)(a)(i): offers a competency-based postsecondary general education course online or in person; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-105(1)(a)(ii): is accredited by an organization that the United States Department of Education recognizes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-105(1)(b): "Articulation agreement" means an agreement between the board and a provider that allows a student to transfer credit awarded by the provider for a general education course to any institution of higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-105(1)(c): "Competency-based" means a system where a student advances to higher levels of learning when the student demonstrates competency of concepts and skills regardless of time, place, or pace.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-105(1)(d): "Competency-based general education provider" or "provider" means a private institution that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-105(1)(d)(i): offers a postsecondary competency-based general education course online or in person;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-105(1)(d)(ii): awards academic credit; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-105(1)(d)(iii): does not award degrees, including associates degrees or baccalaureate degrees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-105(1)(e): 53B-16-110 "Credit for prior learning" means the same as that term is defined in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-105(2)(c): avoid the unnecessary duplication of courses;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-202 Curricula at the community colleges.
---------------------------------------------------------------------
The curricula at the colleges shall include career and technical education, courses of a general nature which can be transferred to other higher education institutions, adult and continuing education, and developmental education.  The colleges also provide needed community service. Career and technical education continues as the highest priority role of the colleges; and to ensure continued emphasis of career and technical education, the board shall develop specific funding mechanisms which will maintain the high priority treatment of these programs and address the fact that many vocational programs are more costly than general education/transfer programs.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-203 Qualifications for entrance to community colleges -- Preference to veterans.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-203(1): The colleges shall give enrollment preference to veterans who furnish proof of other than a dishonorable discharge from the armed forces of the United States.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-203(2): Admission at the colleges is based upon an individual's interest, ability, and potential for the desired occupational area and payment of the required tuition or fee.  The colleges may not deny admission on the basis of an individual's previous schooling or training.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205 Establishment of Snow College Richfield campus.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205(1): There is established a branch campus of Snow College in Richfield, Utah, known as the Snow College Richfield campus.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205(2): Snow College shall administer the branch campus under the general control and supervision of the board as an integrated part of Snow College's mission, programs, and curriculum.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205(3): Snow College shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205(3)(a): maintain a strong curriculum in career and technical education courses at the Snow College Richfield campus and within the region served by Snow College which can be transferred to other institutions within the higher education system, together with lower division courses and courses required for associate degrees in science, arts, applied science, and career and technical education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205(3)(b): work with school districts and charter schools in developing an aggressive concurrent enrollment program in cooperation with Snow College Richfield campus.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205.5 Snow College Concurrent Education Program.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205.5(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205.5(1)(a): "Interactive video conferencing" means two-way, real-time transmission of audio and video signals between devices or computers at two or more locations.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205.5(1)(b): "Program" means the Snow College Concurrent Education Program.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205.5(2): Consistent with policies established by the board, Snow College shall establish and administer, subject to legislative appropriations, the Snow College Concurrent Education Program to provide:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205.5(2)(a): a consistent two-year schedule of concurrent enrollment courses delivered through interactive video conferencing to secondary school students;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205.5(2)(b): a pathway for a secondary school student to earn college credits that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205.5(2)(b)(i): apply toward earning an Associate of Science or Associate of Arts degree; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205.5(2)(b)(ii): satisfy scholarship requirements or other objectives that best meet the needs of an individual student; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-205.5(2)(c): advisory support to secondary school students who participate in the program and the secondary school students' school counselors to ensure that students' concurrent enrollment courses align with the students' academic and career goals.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-302(2): Title 63G, Chapter 2, Government Records Access and Management Act that portion of a technology transfer record or sponsored research record to which access is restricted for competitive or proprietary purposes, as a condition of actual or potential participation in a sponsored research or technology transfer agreement; provided, however, that upon receipt of a written request for a reasonably identifiable record, the public institution of higher education shall disclose:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-302(2)(a): prior to a memorandum of intent to contract or an agreement in principle between the parties:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-302(2)(a)(i): the names of the parties, or, if the disclosure of names would cause competitive harm, a general description of the type of parties negotiating the technology transfer or sponsored research agreement; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-302(2)(a)(ii): a general description of the nature of the technology transfer or sponsored research under consideration, excluding proprietary or competitive information; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-302(2)(b): Title 63G, Chapter 2, Government Records Access and Management Act after a memorandum of intent to contract or an agreement in principle between the parties:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-302(2)(b)(i): the names of the parties involved in the technology transfer or sponsored research;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-302(2)(b)(ii): a general description of the nature of the technology transfer or sponsored research to be conducted, excluding proprietary or competitive information; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-302(2)(b)(iii): Title 63G, Chapter 2, Government Records Access and Management Act records of the technology transfer or sponsored research to be conducted, excluding those portions of records to which access is limited under this part or

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-401 Definitions.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
An institution of higher education shall require an officer or employee of the institution or a cooperating employer, who will be given significant unsupervised access to a minor student in connection with the student's activities as an intern, to submit to a criminal background check on the same basis as a volunteer under Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-405 Recognition of participation in internship program.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
A cooperating employer may be given appropriate recognition by an institution of higher education, including the posting of the employer's name and a short description of the employer's business in an appropriate location on the institution's property, or publication of that information in official publications of the institution.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-601(3): 76-10-101; 32B-1-102; 17-50-331 "Prohibited endorsement provision" means a provision that requires or permits the use of a student athlete's name, image, or likeness to promote:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-601(3)(a): 76-10-101 a tobacco product or e-cigarettes, as those terms are defined in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-601(3)(e): 17-50-331 a sexually oriented business, as that term is defined in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-601(5)(a): between a student athlete and a third party that is not an institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-601(5)(b): in which the student athlete and third party agree that the student athlete's name, image, or likeness may be used to promote a business, product, service, or individual in exchange for the student athlete receiving financial compensation or other benefits.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-602 Use of a student athlete's name, image, or likeness in intercollegiate athletics programs -- Contracts -- Exceptions -- Prohibitions.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-602(1): A student athlete may not enter into a student athlete agreement that contains a prohibited endorsement provision.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-602(2): Before a student athlete or prospective student athlete enters into a student athlete agreement that exceeds $600 in value, the student athlete or proposed student athlete shall provide the student athlete agreement to the student athlete's or proposed student athlete's institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-602(3): An institution that receives a student athlete agreement under Subsection (2) shall provide the student athlete or prospective student athlete with a written acknowledgment regarding whether the student athlete agreement conflicts with the institution's policies or the provisions in this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-602(4): A student athlete agreement or any communication, or other material related to a student athlete agreement, including those created before May 1, 2024, is not subject to Title 63G, Chapter 2, Government Records Access Management Act.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-16-602(5): An institution may not use funds appropriated by the Legislature for any purpose related to a student athlete's or prospective student athlete's student athlete agreement that the student athlete or prospective student athlete submits to the institution.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 17 - University of Utah
*****************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101 Legislative findings on public broadcasting and telecommunications for education.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The Legislature finds and determines the following:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101(1): The University of Utah's Dolores Dore' Eccles Broadcast Center is the statewide public broadcasting and telecommunications facility for education in Utah.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101(2): The center shall provide services to citizens of the state in cooperation with higher and public education, state and local government, and private industry.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101(3): Distribution services provided through the center shall include KUED - TV, KUER - FM, and KUEN - TV.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101(4): KUED - TV and KUER - FM are licensed to the University of Utah.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101(5): The Utah Education and Telehealth Network's broadcast entity, KUEN - TV, is licensed to the Utah Board of Higher Education and, together with UETN, is operated on behalf of the state's systems of public and higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101(6): (3) All the entities referred to in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101(7): This section neither regulates nor restricts a privately owned company in the distribution or dissemination of educational programs.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101.5 Definitions.
-----------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101.5(1): "Board" means the Utah Education and Telehealth Network Board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101.5(2): 53B-17-107 "Education Advisory Council" means the Utah Education Network Advisory Council created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101.5(3): "Digital resource" means a digital or online library resource, including a database.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101.5(4): "Digital resource provider" means an entity that offers a digital resource to customers for license or sale.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101.5(5): "Obscene or pornographic material" means material that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101.5(5)(a): an average person, applying contemporary community standards, finds that, taken as a whole, appeals to prurient interest in sex;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101.5(5)(b): is patently offensive in the description or depiction of nudity, sexual conduct, sexual excitement, sadomasochistic abuse, or excretion; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101.5(5)(c): taken as a whole does not have serious literary, artistic, political, or scientific value.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101.5(6): "Telehealth" means the electronic transfer, exchange, or management of related data for diagnosis, treatment, and consultation, and educational, public health, or other related purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101.5(7): 53B-17-106 "Telehealth Advisory Council" means the Utah Telehealth Advisory Council created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-101.5(8): 53B-17-105 "Utah Education and Telehealth Network," or "UETN," means a consortium and partnership between public and higher education, the Utah Department of Health, and health care providers, that is created in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105 Utah Education and Telehealth Network.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(1): There is created the Utah Education and Telehealth Network, or UETN.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2): UETN shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(a): coordinate and support the telecommunications needs of public and higher education, public libraries, and entities affiliated with the state systems of public and higher education as approved by the Utah Education and Telehealth Network Board, including the statewide development and implementation of a network for education, which utilizes satellite, microwave, fiber-optic, broadcast, and other transmission media;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(b): coordinate the various telecommunications technology initiatives of public and higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(c): provide high-quality, cost-effective Internet access and appropriate interface equipment for schools and school systems;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(d): procure, install, and maintain telecommunication services and equipment on behalf of public and higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(e): develop or implement other programs or services for the delivery of distance learning and telehealth services as directed by law;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(f): apply for state and federal funding on behalf of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(f)(i): public and higher education; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(f)(ii): telehealth services;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(g): in consultation with health care providers from a variety of health care systems, explore and encourage the development of telehealth services as a means of reducing health care costs and increasing health care quality and access, with emphasis on assisting rural health care providers and special populations; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(h): in consultation with the Utah Department of Health, advise the governor and the Legislature on:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(h)(i): the role of telehealth in the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(h)(ii): the policy issues related to telehealth;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(h)(iii): the changing telehealth needs and resources in the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(2)(h)(iv): state budgetary matters related to telehealth.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(3): (2); 54-8b-2 In performing the duties under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(3)(a): provide services to schools, school districts, and the public and higher education systems through an open and competitive bidding process;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(3)(b): work with the private sector to deliver high-quality, cost-effective services;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(3)(c): 54-8b-2 avoid duplicating facilities, equipment, or services of private providers or public telecommunications service, as defined under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(3)(d): utilize statewide economic development criteria in the design and implementation of the educational telecommunications infrastructure; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(3)(e): assure that public service entities, such as educators, public service providers, and public broadcasters, are provided access to the telecommunications infrastructure developed in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(4): The University of Utah shall provide administrative support for UETN.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(a): The Utah Education and Telehealth Network Board, which is the governing board for UETN, is created.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(b): The Utah Education and Telehealth Network Board shall have 13 members as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(b)(i): five members representing the state system of higher education, of which at least one member represents technical colleges, appointed by the commissioner of higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(b)(ii): four members representing the state system of public education appointed by the State Board of Education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(b)(iii): one member representing the state library appointed by the state librarian;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(b)(iv): two members representing hospitals as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(b)(iv)(A): the members may not be employed by the same hospital system;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(b)(iv)(B): one member shall represent a rural hospital;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(b)(iv)(C): one member shall represent an urban hospital; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(b)(iv)(D): the chief administrator or the administrator's designee for each hospital licensed in this state shall select the two hospital representatives; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(b)(v): one member representing the office of the governor, appointed by the governor.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(c): When a vacancy occurs in the membership for any reason, the replacement shall be appointed for the unexpired term.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(d): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(d)(i): The board shall elect a chair.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(5)(d)(ii): The chair shall set the agenda for the board meetings.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(6): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107; 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 A member of the board may not receive compensation or benefits for the member's service, but may receive per diem and travel expenses in accordance with:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(7): The board:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(7)(b): may terminate the executive director's employment or assignment;

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-105(12): If the network operated by the Division of Technology Services is not available, UETN may provide network connections to the central administration of counties and municipalities for the sole purpose of transferring data to a secure facility for backup and disaster recovery.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-106 Utah Telehealth Advisory Council.
------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-106(1): 53B-17-107 There is created the Utah Telehealth Advisory Council, which may, at the discretion of the board, and after July 1, 2015, be combined with the Utah Education Advisory Council created in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-106(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-106(3)(a): The Telehealth Advisory Council shall annually elect a chairperson from its membership.  The chair shall set the agendas for the meetings of the advisory council and shall report to the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-106(3)(b): The Telehealth Advisory Council shall hold meetings at least once every three months.  Meetings may be held from time to time on the call of the chair or a majority of the board members.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-106(4): 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107; 63A-3-106; 63A-3-107 A member may not receive compensation or benefits for the member's service, but, at the executive director's discretion, may receive per diem and travel expenses in accordance with:
