Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-106(6)(a): advise and make recommendations on telehealth service issues to the board and other state entities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-106(6)(b): advise and make recommendations on telehealth-related patient privacy to the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-106(6)(c): promote collaborative efforts to establish technical compatibility, uniform policies, and privacy features to meet legal, financial, commercial, and other societal requirements;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-106(6)(d): identify, address, and seek to resolve the legal, ethical, regulatory, financial, medical, and technological issues that may serve as barriers to telehealth service;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-106(6)(e): explore and encourage the development of telehealth as a means of reducing health care costs and increasing health care quality and access, with emphasis on assisting rural health care providers and special populations with access to or development of electronic medical records; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-106(6)(f): seek public input on telehealth issues.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-109 Digital resource standards.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-109(1): A digital resource purchased or licensed by UETN and offered to students in public schools must have safety policies and technology protection measures that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-109(1)(a): prohibit and prevent a public school student using the resource from sending, receiving, viewing, or downloading obscene or pornographic material; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-109(1)(b): filter or block access to obscene or pornographic material.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-109(2): (1); (1); (1); (2)(a)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-109(2)(a): (1); (1) Regardless of any contract provision to the contrary, if UETN discovers a digital resource does not meet the requirements described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-109(2)(a)(i): shall notify the digital resource provider; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-109(2)(a)(ii): (1) may withhold future payments pending the digital resource provider's compliance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-109(2)(b): (1); (2)(a)(i) A digital resource provider is in breach of contract if the digital resource provider fails to verify compliance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-109(2)(c): Beginning June 1, 2021, a contract UETN enters into for a digital resource shall contain provisions that comply with this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-109(3): Before November 30 of each year, UETN shall submit a report to the Education Interim Committee detailing all instances of a digital resource provider's failure to comply with the provisions of this section.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-201 Proceeds from federal land grants for a Miners' Hospital for Disabled Miners -- Reporting requirements.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-201(1): There is appropriated to the University of Utah all funds, assets, and revenues which have been, or will be, derived from the sale or other disposition of those lands conveyed to the state of Utah by those federal grants for a Miners' Hospital for Disabled Miners contained in Section 12 of the Enabling Act and in Chapter 280, Public Laws of the Seventieth Congress, 2nd Session (Act of February 20, 1929) which funds, assets, and revenues now are, or in the future will be, in the custody and control of the School and Institutional Trust Lands Board of Trustees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-201(2): (1) The University of Utah shall report annually to the Natural Resources, Agriculture, and Environmental Quality Appropriations Subcommittee and the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee the following information regarding the administration and operation of the Miners' Hospital for Disabled Miners described in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-201(2)(a)(ii): total number of patients served; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-201(2)(a)(iii): the types of service or care given to patients; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-201(2)(b): how the University of Utah plans to administer and operate the Miners' Hospital for Disabled Miners in the future.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-202 Use of funds -- Rehabilitation building.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
The funds, assets, and revenues shall be used for the construction, equipment, furnishings, and operation, or either or any of the same, on the campus of the university of a rehabilitation building, either as a separate structure or as an integrated unit in the University of Utah Medical Center.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-401 College of Mines and Earth Sciences -- Beneficiary of land grants -- Courses of study.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-401(1): There is established a College of Mines and Earth Sciences at the University of Utah.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-401(2): The college is the beneficiary of all land grants and appropriations made or to be made by the United States to the state for the establishment and maintenance of a school of mines.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-401(3): The college may offer courses in and related to mining, metallurgical and electrical engineering, and other branches of engineering that pertain to mining.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-402 Utah Engineering Experiment Station.
---------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-402(1): There is established a Utah Engineering Experiment Station in conjunction with the College of Mines and Earth Sciences.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-402(2): The station is controlled and managed by the University of Utah.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-403 Functions of the station.
----------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-403(1): The station has the following functions:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-403(1)(a): to conduct experiments and investigations on matters that have the potential to benefit the state's industrial interests or would be for the public good; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-403(1)(b): to inform the public of the results of the experiments and investigations conducted by the station.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-403(2): The station is not to conduct experiments or investigations on those matters that more properly relate to the functions of Utah State University's experiment station.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-403(3): The University of Utah makes an annual report on the engineering experiment station to the governor at a time designated by the governor.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-501 Research park authorized.
----------------------------------------------------------
The Legislature determines that it is in the public interest of the state of Utah, its citizens, and commerce to develop a research park in Salt Lake County upon property conveyed to the University of Utah under patent from the United States of America dated October 18, 1968.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-502 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in SectionsUtah Code Annotated § 53B-17-502(1): "Patent" means the patent covering the land acquired by the University of Utah from the United States of America dated October 18, 1968.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-502(2): "Research park" means research and development facilities, research institutes, testing laboratories, related business and government installations, and similar facilities, together with land, including all necessary appurtenances, rights, and franchises acquired and developed by the University of Utah which are suitable or necessary to promote the social welfare of the state of Utah through the advancement of education, science, research, economic development, and related purposes.  The acquisition and provision of any one or more of the following facilities may be included as part of the development of land for the research park: water, sewage, drainage, street, road, sidewalk, curb, gutter, street lighting, electrical distribution, and docking, but only to the extent that the facilities are incidental to the use of the land as a research park.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-503 Administration through nonprofit corporations or foundations -- Control -- Authority of corporations or foundations -- Personnel considered employees of university.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-503(1): The University of Utah may establish, develop, and administer through nonprofit corporations or foundations controlled by the president and the board a research park upon the land acquired by the university under the patent.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-503(2): The nonprofit corporations or foundations may receive and administer legislative appropriations, government grants, contracts, and private gifts to carry out their public purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-503(3): All salaried employees, agents, officers, faculty, and staff of the nonprofit corporation or foundation are for the purpose of employee benefits, employees, agents, officers, faculty, and staff of the University of Utah.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-504 Powers of university as related to research park.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The University of Utah has the following powers:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-504(1): to establish, acquire, develop, maintain, and operate a research park, including the acquisition of all necessary or suitable buildings, facilities, and improvements, and to acquire, purchase, construct, reconstruct, improve, remodel, add to, extend, maintain, equip, and furnish the research park or any building or facility, including research and service facilities and areas intended for the common use of the research park tenants;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-504(2): to form nonprofit corporations or foundations to aid and assist the University of Utah to attain its charitable, scientific, literary, and educational objectives, including the acquisition, construction, financing, operation, and management of a research park;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-504(3): to lease to the nonprofit corporation or foundation all or part of the land and facilities included in the research park upon terms and conditions established by the University of Utah, and to enter into any other contract or agreement with the nonprofit corporation or foundation as necessary for the construction, financing, operation, and management of the research park;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-504(4): to lease, either directly or through a nonprofit corporation or foundation, to any person, firm, partnership, or corporation engaged in business for a profit any part or all of the land, buildings, or facilities of the research park under guidelines established by the university;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-504(5): to allow a lessee to acquire or construct necessary or suitable buildings, facilities, and improvements upon the leased property. Any improvements acquired or constructed upon the premises during the term of the lease reverts to and becomes the property of the university at the termination of the lease, its renewal, or extension; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-504(6): to finance all or part of the cost of the research park including the purchase, construction, reconstruction, improvement, remodeling, addition to, extension, maintenance, equipment, and furnishing as permitted by law for the financing of self-liquidating projects by institutions of higher education.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-505 City to provide services and facilities to research park -- Fees and charges -- Disallowance of special improvement district or special taxes.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-505(1): The Salt Lake City Council shall provide police and fire protection and furnish, install, and maintain customary municipal services and facilities for street lighting, traffic control, sidewalks, curb, gutter, drainage, sewage disposal, and water supply to all areas of the research park established upon lands conveyed to the University of Utah under the patent.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-505(2): The services and facilities are to be furnished and provided as needed and determined by the board subject to connection fees, use charges, and other service fees customarily assessed against similar persons, companies, or properties within the territorial limits of Salt Lake City.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-505(3): No special improvement district may be created or special taxes imposed with respect to the services and facilities provided under this section.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-506 Agreements with Department of Transportation regarding research park roads.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The Department of Transportation may enter into agreements with the University of Utah between regular sessions of the Legislature designating all or part of the roads within or adjacent to the research park as part of the state highway system.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-601 Utah Museum of Natural History -- Traveling exhibits and Outreach Programs.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-601(1): There is established at the University of Utah the Utah Museum of Natural History, where tangible objects reflecting the past, present, and continuing development of our natural history may be collected and displayed for educational and cultural purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-601(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-601(2)(a): The museum shall make available to people throughout the state, through traveling exhibits and outreach programs, archeological and paleontological objects retrieved from the state of Utah.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-601(2)(b): The museum shall provide professional expertise and assistance in the proper care of the archeological and paleontological collections from state lands as they are housed throughout the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-601(3): (2) The museum shall submit an annual request to the Legislature to fund the ongoing costs of the programs authorized under Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-602 Acceptance of gifts.
-----------------------------------------------------
The University of Utah is authorized to receive gifts, contributions, and donations of all kinds, including tangible objects and specimens for the development of or display in the museum.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603 Curation and deposit of specimens.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(1): 9-8a-302; (3)(c); (3)(c); 53C-1-103 For purposes of this section:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(1)(b)(iii): (3)(c) for the purposes described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(1)(b)(iv): an appropriate state park.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(1)(c): "Museum" means the Utah Museum of Natural History.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(1)(d): "Paleontology museum" means a museum owned or established by a city of the first or second class, that:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(1)(d)(iii): is an approved repository, as that term is defined in 43 C.F.R. Sec. 49.5, or has a detailed plan to become an approved repository.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(1)(e): (3)(c) "Repository" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(1)(e)(i): a facility designated by the museum through memoranda of agreement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(1)(e)(ii): (3)(c) for the purposes described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(1)(e)(iii): a place of reburial.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(1)(f): 53C-1-103 "School and institutional trust lands" are those properties defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(2): The museum shall make rules to ensure the adequate curation of all collections from lands owned or controlled by the state or its subdivisions.  The rules shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(2)(a): conform to, but not be limited by, federal curation policy;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(2)(b): recognize that collections recovered from school and institutional trust lands are owned by the respective trust, and shall be made available for exhibition as the beneficiaries of the respective trust may request, subject to museum curation policy and the curation facility's budgetary priorities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(2)(c): recognize that any collections obtained in exchange for collections found on school and institutional trust lands shall be owned by the respective trust; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(2)(d): recognize that if, at its discretion, the curation facility makes and sells reproductions derived from collections found on school or institutional trust lands, any money obtained from these sales shall be given to the respective trust, but the curation facility may retain money sufficient to recover the direct costs of preparation for sale and a reasonable fee for handling the sale.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(3): (3)(c)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(3)(a): (3)(c) Subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(3)(b): In these memoranda, the museum may delegate some or all of its authority to curate.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(3)(c): A city that has a paleontology museum may retain, curate, and manage paleontological specimens, paleontological collections, and paleontological resources recovered on lands owned or controlled by the city.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(4)(c)(iii): the proximity of the curation facility or repository to the point of origin of the collection;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(4)(c)(iv): the preference of the owner of the land on which the collection was found;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(4)(c)(v): the nature of the collection and the repository's or curation facility's ability and desire to curate the collection in question, and ability to maximize the scientific, educational, and cultural benefits for the people of the state and the school and institutional trusts;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(4)(c)(vi): selection of a second curation facility or repository, if the original repository or curation facility becomes unable to curate the collections under its care; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(4)(c)(vii): establishment of an arbitration process for the resolution of disputes over the location of a curation facility or repository, which shall include an ultimate arbitration authority consisting of the landowner, the state archaeologist or paleontologist, and a representative from the governor's office.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(4)(d): The repository or curation facility may charge a curation fee commensurate with the costs of maintaining those collections, except that a fee may not be charged to the respective trust for collections found on school or institutional trust lands.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(5): The repository or curation facility shall make specimens available through loans to museums and research institutions in and out of the state when, in the opinion of the repository or curation facility:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-603(5)(b): arrangements are made for safe custodianship of the specimens.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701 Utah Museum of Fine Arts.
----------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(1): There is established at the University of Utah the Utah Museum of Fine Arts as:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(1)(a): a state general and multicultural art museum; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(1)(b): a state institution charged with the broad responsibility of collecting and exhibiting, for the education and enrichment of its citizens, art and related objects from around the world from prehistoric times to the present.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(2): (1) The museum shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(2)(a): (1) serve as a repository in Utah of the objects referred to in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(2)(b): collect and display tangible art objects that reflect the past, present, and continuing development of the visual arts in America and throughout the rest of the world;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(2)(c): provide professional expertise and assistance in the proper care of the tangible art objects displayed at the museum; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(2)(d): engage visitors to the museum in discovering meaningful connections with the artistic expressions of the world's cultures by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(2)(d)(i): acting as a responsible steward of the material legacy of the visual arts located at the Utah Museum of Fine Arts for the people of Utah;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(2)(d)(ii): serving as a teaching, learning, and research resource for the University of Utah, the state's greater educational community, and the general public;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(2)(d)(iii): promoting an open dialogue with visitors and the community about the role of visual arts in our society;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(2)(d)(iv): fostering and celebrating the diverse artistic expressions and accomplishments of the people of Utah and around the world;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(2)(d)(v): cultivating community partnerships and collaborations to ensure that the visual arts reach a broad spectrum of the general public; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-701(2)(d)(vi): offering a wide range of experiences that will enable visitors to the museum to explore the variety of ways the arts can inform and enhance the human experience.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-702 Acceptance of gifts.
-----------------------------------------------------
The University of Utah may receive gifts, contributions, and donations of all kinds, including tangible objects for the development of or display in the museum.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001 Reading clinics -- Purpose.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001(1): The Legislature recognizes the critical importance of identifying, assessing, and assisting students with reading difficulties at an early age in order for them to have successful and productive school and life experiences.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001(2): In order to help accomplish this, there is established a reading clinic, hereafter referred to as the "clinic," based at the University of Utah, College of Education, to assist educators and parents of students statewide in:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001(2)(a): assessing elementary school students who do not demonstrate satisfactory progress in reading;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001(2)(b): providing instructional intervention to enable the students to overcome reading difficulties; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001(2)(c): becoming better prepared to help all students become successful readers by providing them with professional development programs in reading that are based on best practices and the most current, scientific research available through nationally and internationally recognized reading researchers and instructional specialists.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001(3)(a): The clinic shall focus primarily on students in grades 1 through 3 since research shows the need for students to become successful readers by the end of grade 3.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001(3)(b): The clinic shall make assessment and instructional intervention services available to public education students of all ages.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001(4): The clinic shall provide these services at a base site in Salt Lake County and through remote access interactive technology to reach educators, parents, and students throughout the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001(5): The clinic shall provide:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001(5)(a): instruction to teachers in the use of technology and blended learning in providing individualized reading instruction and reading remediation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001(5)(b): access to students for reading remediation and instruction services through distance learning technology if a student is unable to regularly access a reading clinic location.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1001(6): The clinic shall integrate both the usage of and instruction on the use of technology-based reading assessment tools as part of the clinic's services.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1101 Definitions.
----------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1101(1): "Researcher" means an individual who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1101(1)(a): on May 8, 2018, is employed, alone or as part of a research team, by the university;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1101(1)(b): before May 8, 2018, received funding from USTAR for some or all of the researcher's startup costs or salary;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1101(1)(c): was recruited to become a member of the university's faculty; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1101(1)(d): after May 8, 2018, receives some or all of the researcher's start up costs or salary from a legislative appropriation to the university for that purpose.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1101(2): "University" means the University of Utah.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1101(3): "USTAR" means the Utah Science Technology and Research Initiative, which was repealed in 2020.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202 SafeUT Crisis Line established.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
The Huntsman Mental Health Institute shall:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202(1): establish a SafeUT Crisis Line to provide:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202(1)(a): a means for an individual to anonymously report:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202(1)(a)(i): unsafe, violent, or criminal activities, or the threat of such activities at or near a public school;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202(1)(a)(ii): incidents of bullying, cyber-bullying, harassment, or hazing; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202(1)(a)(iii): incidents of physical or sexual abuse committed by a school employee or school volunteer; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202(1)(b): crisis intervention, including suicide prevention, to individuals experiencing emotional distress or psychiatric crisis;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202(2): provide the services described in Subsection (1) 24 hours a day, seven days a week;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202(3): when necessary, or as required by law, promptly forward a report received under Subsection (1)(a) to appropriate:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202(3)(a): school officials; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202(3)(b): law enforcement officials;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202(4): 53-10-302 in accordance with Subsection (5), report the uses of the SafeUT Crisis Line described in Subsection (1) to the State Bureau of Investigation's systems described in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202(5): coordinate with the state security chief to determine the appropriate circumstances necessitating a report described in Subsection (4); and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1202(6): 53-22-104.1; 53-22-102; 53G-8-802 subject to legislative appropriations and in consultation with the School Security Task Force described in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203 SafeUT and School Safety Commission established -- Members.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(1): There is created the SafeUT and School Safety Commission composed of the following members:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(1)(a): one member who represents the Office of the Attorney General, whom the attorney general appoints;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(1)(b): one member who represents the Utah public education system, whom the State Board of Education appoints;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(1)(c): a designee of the Utah Board of Higher Education, whom the commissioner selects under direction of the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(1)(d): one member who represents the Department of Health and Human Services, whom the executive director of the Department of Health and Human Services appoints;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(1)(e): one member of the House of Representatives, whom the speaker of the House of Representatives appoints;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(1)(f): one member of the Senate, whom the president of the Senate appoints;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(1)(g): one member who represents the Huntsman Mental Health Institute, whom the chair of the commission appoints;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(1)(h): one member who represents law enforcement who has extensive experience in emergency response, whom the chair of the commission appoints;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(1)(i): one member who represents the Department of Health and Human Services who has experience in youth services or treatment services, whom the executive director of the Department of Health and Human Services appoints; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(1)(j): two members of the public, whom the chair of the commission appoints.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(2)(a): Except as provided in Subsection (2)(b), members of the commission shall be appointed to four-year terms.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(2)(b): The length of the terms of the members shall be staggered so that approximately half of the committee is appointed every two years.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(2)(c): When a vacancy occurs in the membership of the commission, the replacement shall be appointed for the unexpired term.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(3)(a): The attorney general's designee shall serve as chair of the commission.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(3)(b): The chair shall set the agenda for commission meetings.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(4): Attendance of a simple majority of the members constitutes a quorum for the transaction of official commission business.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(5): Formal action by the commission requires a majority vote of a quorum.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(6): 36-2-2
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(6)(a): Except as provided in Subsection (6)(b), a member may not receive compensation, benefits, per diem, or travel expenses for the member's service.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(6)(b): 36-2-2 Compensation and expenses of a member who is a legislator are governed by Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1203(7): The Office of the Attorney General shall provide staff support to the commission.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302 Huntsman Mental Health Institute -- Behavioral health curriculum.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(1): The Huntsman Mental Health Institute shall coordinate with the State Board of Education to develop a youth curriculum to increase awareness about behavioral health challenges facing youth in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(2): (1) The curriculum described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(2)(a): the connection and importance of mental health to overall health;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(2)(b): tools for maintaining mental health wellness, including evidence-based practices used to overcome behavioral health challenges;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(2)(c): signs and symptoms of common behavioral health challenges and ways to respond to the signs and symptoms;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(2)(d): the prevalence of behavioral health challenges across all populations;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(2)(e): common behavioral health conditions and evidence-based treatments for common behavioral health conditions; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(2)(f): how to seek assistance or find support for a behavioral health challenge in a school and the community.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(3): The Huntsman Mental Health Institute shall annually:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(3)(a): update the curriculum in coordination with the State Board of Education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(3)(b): publish the curriculum on the Huntsman Mental Health Institute's website in a conspicuous location; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(3)(c): distribute the curriculum as a resource to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(3)(c)(i): parents and guardians of elementary and secondary school students;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(3)(c)(ii): elementary and secondary schools; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(3)(c)(iii): other organizations that serve youth in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1302(4): (3)(a) The Huntsman Mental Health Institute shall consider feedback provided to the Huntsman Mental Health Institute about the curriculum when annually updating the curriculum under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402 Center creation -- Duties.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(1): There is created the Center for Medical Cannabis Research within the University of Utah.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2): 26B-4-222 The center:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(a): shall seek state, federal, and private funds to award grants for medical cannabis research;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(b): shall facilitate and support funding for research related to the health effects, including the potential risks or side effects, of the use of cannabis products;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(c): shall facilitate and support funding for research related to the efficacy and potential health effects of various cannabis delivery methods, including vaporizing, ingesting, topical application, and combustion;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(d): shall support researchers in applying for and securing federal and private research grant funding for expanding medical cannabis research;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(e): shall review current and future cannabis research literature, clinical studies, and clinical trials;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(f): shall educate medical providers, lawmakers, and the public about medical cannabis research advances;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(g): shall, if requested, consult with researchers and eligible institutions seeking to conduct medical cannabis research regarding legal implications of the research under state and federal law;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(h): shall monitor, to the extent that appropriate and sufficient data are available, patient outcomes in any state with a medicinal cannabis program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(i): may coordinate, share knowledge, and share best practices with a state:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(i)(i): that has a medical cannabis program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(i)(ii): is conducting cannabis research;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(j): may award or facilitate funding for grants to an eligible institution for medical cannabis research, including research regarding the growing of a medical-grade cannabis plant that is used for a cannabis product;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(k): shall support a licensed cannabis cultivation facility to provide medical-grade cannabis products for research;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(l): shall make, for research conducted by the center, the research outcomes publicly available;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(m): shall maintain a catalog of all published scientific reports based on projects funded or managed by the center;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(n): shall ensure that an individual who agrees to use a cannabis product as part of a research project conducted by the center or a grantee has:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(n)(i): a valid medical cannabis patient card from the state; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(n)(ii): if included in the research project as a resident of another state, the equivalent of a medical cannabis patient card under the laws of another state, district, territory, commonwealth, or insular possession of the United States;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(o): shall obtain an academic research cannabis license;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(p): may apply for, or assist an eligible institution to apply for, a federal cannabis cultivation registration to locate a cannabis cultivation site in Utah; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(q): 26B-4-222 for the report described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(q)(i): all research projects that are funded by a grant awarded by the center, including which institution received the grant;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(q)(ii): all research projects conducted by the center; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(2)(q)(iii): the adequacy of funding for the center's duties.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(3): 26-61-102 For research funded, conducted, or facilitated by the center, the center shall ensure the research:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(3)(a): includes appropriate research development, testing, and evaluation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(3)(b): 26-61-102 if the research involves human subjects, is reviewed, approved, and overseen by an institutional review board as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-17-1402(4): The University of Utah shall provide staff for the center.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 18 - Utah State University
********************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-101 Agricultural experiment station.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-101(1): There is established an agricultural experiment station in connection with Utah State University.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-101(2): The station conducts research as provided by state and federal laws governing the establishment and maintenance of agricultural experiment stations.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-102 Purchases of land -- Equipment -- Personnel.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah State University is in charge of the experiment station, and shall purchase or lease suitable lands, erect necessary buildings, provide needed equipment, and appoint officers and assistants to conduct and issue reports on the research conducted at the station.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-103 Cooperative agreements.
--------------------------------------------------------
The university may enter into cooperative agreements with governmental entities, organizations, corporations, institutions, and individuals to carry out the provisions governing agricultural experiment stations.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-104 Substations.
---------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-104(1): 53B-18-101 The university may establish and maintain substations to assist in conducting the research provided for in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-104(2): The university may discontinue the existence of a substation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-104(3): If a substation is created by legislative enactment, the university is under no obligation to maintain the substation beyond that time for which special appropriations are made by the Legislature.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-105 Climate center.
------------------------------------------------
Utah State University shall establish and maintain a climate center to gather and analyze climatological data for the benefit of all state agencies.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-201 Agricultural extension service.
----------------------------------------------------------------
There is established by Utah State University an agricultural extension service as provided in the federal Smith-Lever and Capper-Ketchum Acts and other federal laws.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-202 Cooperative contracts for expenses.
--------------------------------------------------------------------
The university may enter into cooperative contracts with the United States Department of Agriculture, county or city officers, private and public organizations, corporations, and individuals, to share the expense of establishing and maintaining an agricultural extension service.  The county legislative body of each county may provide sufficient funds to insure that the agricultural extension service functions properly in its county.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-203 Federal aid for experiment station.
--------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-203(1): 53B-18-204 The governor may apply to the Secretary of the Treasury to obtain any appropriation made by Congress relating to the federal laws referred to in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-203(2): (1) The university shall execute and file with the Secretary of the Treasury an agreement relating to the expenditure of funds received under the laws referred to in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-203(3): (1) The university shall comply with all conditions expressed in the laws referred to in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-204 Acceptance of federal grants.
--------------------------------------------------------------
The state of Utah reaffirms its acceptance of the grants of money and property authorized by the following Acts of Congress:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-204(1): the Morrill Act, approved July 2, 1862;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-204(2): an Act of Congress passed March 2, 1887, entitled, "An act to establish agricultural experiment stations in connection with the colleges established in the several states under the provisions of an act approved July 2, 1862, and all acts supplementary to that act";
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-204(3): an Act of Congress entitled, "An act to provide an increased annual appropriation for agricultural experiment stations and regulating the expenditure thereof," approved March 16, 1906;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-204(4): the Purnell Act, approved February 24, 1925;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-204(5): "the Smith-Lever Act to aid in the development of the extension work in connection with the agricultural colleges," approved May 8, 1914;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-204(6): "the Capper-Ketchum Act, providing for further support of agricultural extension work as conducted by the agricultural colleges," approved May 22, 1928.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-205 State guarantee of federal funds.
------------------------------------------------------------------
The state guarantees all money received under Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-206 Treasurer to receive appropriations.
---------------------------------------------------------------------
The treasurer of Utah State University is the officer who receives money appropriated by the Secretary of the Treasury under Sections

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-301 Regional campuses -- Administration -- Location.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah State University shall operate and administer regional campuses located at or near Roosevelt and Moab.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-302 Courses offered at regional campuses.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
A regional campus described in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-401 Control and supervision.
---------------------------------------------------------
Utah State University has general control and supervision of the state power plant in Logan Canyon.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-501 Nonprofit corporations or foundations -- Purpose.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-501(1): In addition to any other powers which it now has, Utah State University may form nonprofit corporations or foundations controlled by the president of the university and the board to aid and assist the university in attaining its charitable, scientific, literary, research, and educational objectives.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-501(2): The nonprofit corporations or foundations may receive and administer legislative appropriations, government grants, contracts, and private gifts to carry out their public purposes.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-601 Program creation -- Location.
--------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-601(1): There is created the Strengthening At-Risk Youth and Their Families Program to be administered through the Utah State University Extension Family Life and 4-H Programs.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-601(2): The program shall be implemented throughout the state through Utah State University Extension county offices.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602 Program requirements -- Referrals -- Evaluation.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(1): The program shall provide services to youth who have demonstrated behavioral and learning problems at school or have been referred to juvenile court for delinquent behavior.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(2): Youths and their families in need of services may be identified and referred to the program through:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(2)(a): school officials;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(2)(b): juvenile court officers;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(2)(c): community social service agencies; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(2)(d): parents.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(3): The program shall actively seek and screen adult volunteers to work with high risk youth and their families.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(4): The program shall provide training and support to the volunteers to prepare them for the wide variety of social, cultural, and other environmental factors they will encounter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(5): The volunteers shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(5)(a): enroll and involve youth in 4-H and other community service and activity programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(5)(b): provide academic tutoring, with an emphasis on reading skills, when necessary;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(5)(c): seek out opportunities for participation in structured recreational activities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(5)(d): facilitate the families' development of a positive family environment including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(5)(d)(i): setting clear expectations and limits in the home;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(5)(d)(ii): fostering communication skills between family members;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(5)(d)(iii): encouraging the families' involvement in the school and community; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(5)(d)(iv): assisting in the development of time management skills.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(6): The program shall provide for an annual assessment and evaluation of the entire program including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(6)(a): assessments conducted on youths and their families before entering the program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(6)(b): documentation of ongoing changes observed in the youths while participating in the program, including behavioral and academic changes;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(6)(c): assessments conducted on youths and their families upon exiting the program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(6)(d): overall assessment of the program in the various communities, to include:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(6)(d)(i): acceptance and support within the community;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(6)(d)(ii): availability of sufficient programs and activities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-602(6)(d)(iii): availability of qualified adults to serve as volunteers.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-701 Recreation and Tourism Program.
----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-701(1): There is appropriated for fiscal year 1998-99, $150,000 from the General Fund to Utah State University for base budget funding to conduct a program of teaching, research, and extension on outdoor recreation and tourism.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-701(2): The university shall establish the program in the Institute of Outdoor Recreation and Tourism in the College of Natural Resources.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-701(3): The extension and research program shall focus on at least three areas:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-701(3)(a): tourism and outdoor recreation use;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-701(3)(b): the social and economic tradeoffs of tourism and outdoor recreation for local communities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-701(3)(c): the relationship between outdoor recreation and tourism and public land management practices and policies.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-701(4): The purpose of the program is to provide:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-701(4)(a): better data for the Legislature and state agencies in their decision-making processes on issues relating to tourism and outdoor recreation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-701(4)(b): a base of information and expertise to assist community officials as they attempt to balance the economic, social, and environmental tradeoffs in tourism development; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-701(4)(c): an interdisciplinary approach of research and study on outdoor recreation and tourism, a complex sector of the state's economy.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-701(5): The program shall include an office at the university for coordinating interdepartmental research and extension efforts with different agencies and institutions of higher education.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801 Establishment of the center -- Purpose -- Duties and responsibilities.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(1): There is hereby established the Center for the School of the Future at Utah State University, hereafter referred to as "the center."
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(2)(a): The purpose of the center is to promote best practices in the state's public education system and encourage cooperative and research development relationships between public and higher education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(2)(b): For purposes of this section "best practices" means the best process or system that effectively achieves an educational objective.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(3): The center has the following duties and responsibilities:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(3)(a): to direct its efforts to those education issues judged to be of greatest importance by the State Board of Education, school districts, and their patrons, subject to the availability of funds to sustain its efforts;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(3)(b): to coordinate and collaborate with education stakeholders, such as institutions of higher education, the State Board of Education, school districts, parent-teacher organizations, and other public and private educational interests in identifying or developing and then implementing best practices throughout the state's public education system;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(3)(c): to contribute to the creation and maintenance of a public education system that continually and systematically improves itself by building upon the most effective education policies, programs, and practices and rejecting those that are less effective;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(3)(d): to identify problems and challenges in providing educational and related services to all students in the public schools, including special education students and students at risk;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(3)(e): to identify current public and private resources at both the state and national level that are available to resolve problems or overcome challenges within the public education system and seek additional resources as necessary; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(3)(f): to support the implementation of best practices in the public education system through professional development programs and dissemination of information.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(4): The center in collaboration with the State Board of Education shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(4)(a): clarify the problems and challenges identified under this section, identify desired outcomes, and agree upon measures of outcomes;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(4)(b): prioritize the problems and challenges;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(4)(c): identify readily accessible resources to solve problems and challenges, including best practices that could be implemented with little or no adaptation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(4)(d): determine whether new programs or procedures should be developed, and estimate the extent of effort required for that development;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(4)(e): determine which existing programs should be eliminated; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-801(4)(f): assist in implementing solutions, monitoring accomplishments, disseminating results, and facilitating the extension of successful efforts to new settings.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901 Distance Education Doctorate Program.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(1): The Legislature finds that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(1)(a): many Utah public education administrators are nearing the end of their careers and will retire early in the 21st Century;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(1)(b): Utah public schools have many mid-career faculty that could become the next wave of administrators if they were prepared with a doctorate in education degree that emphasized curriculum and instruction;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(1)(c): each of Utah's community colleges have several faculty that need a terminal degree and further knowledge in curriculum development and state-of-the-art instructional methodology, and these individuals, being mid-career, find it difficult to relocate to a college campus for a traditional program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(1)(d): the state and its students will be better served if faculty and administrators are more knowledgeable about the development of curriculum and the latest instructional methodology based on documented research.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(2): Therefore, Utah State University shall establish a Distance Education Doctorate Program to accommodate public education administrators and community college faculty and administration.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(3): Title 53B, Chapter 17, Part 1, Educational Telecommunications The program shall include the following components:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(3)(a): Title 53B, Chapter 17, Part 1, Educational Telecommunications the offering of courses for a doctorate degree in education over the system established under
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(3)(b): structuring of the program to make it identical to a regular campus program in rigor and course work; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(3)(c): providing a support system from at least the following five departments at the university:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(3)(c)(i): Elementary Education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(3)(c)(ii): Secondary Education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(3)(c)(iii): Business Information Systems and Education;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(3)(c)(iv): Industrial Technology; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(3)(c)(v): Agricultural Systems Technology and Education.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(4): Title 53B, Chapter 17, Part 1, Educational Telecommunications The university shall augment the program with off-campus summer courses, with those courses eventually being offered over the system established under
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-901(5): The Legislature shall provide an annual appropriation to fund the program established under this part.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1001 Definitions.
----------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1001(1): "Alliance" means the Utah Heritage Highway 89 Alliance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1001(2): "Center" means the Mormon Pioneer Heritage Center.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1001(3): "Counties" means the counties of Sanpete, Sevier, Piute, Wayne, Garfield, and Kane.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002 Establishment of the center -- Purpose -- Duties and responsibilities.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(1): There is established the Mormon Pioneer Heritage Center in connection with Utah State University.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(2): The purpose of the center is to coordinate interdepartmental research and extension efforts in recreation, heritage tourism, and agricultural extension service and to enter into cooperative contracts with the United States Departments of Agriculture and the Interior, state, county, and city officers, public and private organizations, and individuals to enhance Mormon pioneer heritage.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3): The center has the following duties and responsibilities:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3)(a): to support United States Congressional findings that the landscape, architecture, traditions, products, and events in the counties convey the heritage of pioneer settlements and their role in agricultural development;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3)(b): to coordinate with extension agents in the counties to assist in the enhancement of heritage businesses and the creation of heritage products;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3)(c): to foster a close working relationship with all levels of government, the private sector, residents, business interests, and local communities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3)(d): to support United States Congressional findings that the historical, cultural, and natural heritage legacies of Mormon colonization and settlement are nationally significant;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3)(e): to encourage research and studies relative to the variety of heritage resources along the 250-mile Highway 89 corridor from Fairview to Kanab, Utah, and Highways 12 and 24, the All American Road, to the extent those resources demonstrate:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3)(e)(i): the colonization of the western United States; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3)(e)(ii): the expansion of the United States as a major world power;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3)(f): to demonstrate that the great relocation to the western United States was facilitated by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3)(f)(i): the 1,400 mile trek from Illinois to the Great Salt Lake by the Mormon Pioneers; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3)(f)(ii): the subsequent colonization effort in Nevada, Utah, the southeast corner of Idaho, the southwest corner of Wyoming, large areas of southeastern Oregon, much of southern California, and areas along the eastern border of California; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3)(g): to assist in interpretive efforts that demonstrate how the Boulder Loop, Capitol Reef National Park, Zion National Park, Bryce Canyon National Park, and the Highway 89 area convey the compelling story of how early settlers:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3)(g)(i): interacted with Native Americans; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(3)(g)(ii): established towns and cities in a harsh, yet spectacular, natural environment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(4): The center, in collaboration with the United States Department of the Interior, the National Park Service, the United States Department of Agriculture, the United States Forest Service, the Department of Cultural and Community Engagement, the Utah Historical Society, and the alliance and its intergovernmental local partners, shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(4)(a): assist in empowering communities in the counties to conserve, preserve, and enhance the heritage of the communities while strengthening future economic opportunities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(4)(b): help conserve, interpret, and develop the historical, cultural, natural, and recreational resources within the counties; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(4)(c): expand, foster, and develop heritage businesses and products relating to the cultural heritage of the counties.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1002(5): The center, in collaboration with the United States Department of the Interior, the National Park Service, and with funding from the alliance, shall develop a heritage management plan.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1101 Higher Education Engineering Partnership.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1101(1): Utah State University and Weber State University shall enter into a partnership agreement to jointly deliver a bachelor's degree in electrical engineering to meet the demand for electrical engineers in the state, including the demand at Hill Air force Base.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1101(2): The partnership agreement may provide for:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1101(2)(a): a satellite location for the Utah State University electrical engineering program on a Weber State University campus, including the Davis campus; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1101(2)(b): a curriculum using courses from:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1101(2)(b)(i): Weber State University's electrical engineering technology and general education programs; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1101(2)(b)(ii): Utah State University's electrical engineering bachelor's degree program and other related programs.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1301 Veterinary education program -- Partnership agreement.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1301(2): (2)(a) The partnership agreement may provide that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1301(2)(a): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1301(2)(a)(i): initially, up to 20 Utah resident students and 10 nonresident students may be accepted each year into a four-year program leading to a doctorate in veterinary medicine; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1301(2)(a)(ii): if resources become available to expand the doctoral program in veterinary medicine, additional Utah resident students and nonresident students may be accepted into the program; and

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1401 Uintah Basin Air Quality Research Project -- Report.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1401(1): There is created the Uintah Basin Air Quality Research Project to study ozone formation in the Uintah Basin.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1401(2): (2)(a) The Utah State University Bingham Entrepreneurship and Energy Research Center shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1401(2)(a): conduct the Uintah Basin Air Quality Research Project by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1401(2)(a)(i): developing and improving computer models to simulate ozone formation and determine its cause;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1401(2)(a)(ii): measuring pollutants in the ambient air to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1401(2)(a)(ii)(A): track how emissions are changing over time; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1401(2)(a)(ii)(B): verify the accuracy of computer models; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1401(2)(a)(iii): characterizing pollutant emissions from various sources; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1401(2)(b): (2)(a) annually report to the Natural Resources, Agriculture, and Environment Interim Committee on the results of the research described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501 Remote online opportunities program -- Report to Legislature.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(1): Title 11, Chapter 13, Interlocal Cooperation Act As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(1)(a): Title 11, Chapter 13, Interlocal Cooperation Act "Association of governments" means an association of political subdivisions established pursuant to an interlocal agreement under
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(1)(b): "Program" means the program administered by Utah State University in accordance with this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(1)(c): "Remote online opportunity" means employment, including freelance employment, or the operation of an online business for which an individual:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(1)(c)(i): can complete duties primarily online; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(1)(c)(ii): is not required to work from a specific geographic location.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(2): (4)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(2)(a): Subject to legislative appropriations, Utah State University, through a county extension office, shall administer a program that helps individuals who live in rural areas access remote online opportunities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(2)(b): (4) In administering the program, Utah State University shall consider input from a county located in a geographic area selected for the program under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(3): Utah State University shall, as part of the program:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(3)(a): provide training modules to adults and high school students;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(3)(b): coordinate with rural high schools and postsecondary institutions;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(3)(c): develop marketing materials;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(3)(d): develop relationships with information technology companies that offer remote online opportunities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(3)(e): partner with websites that list freelance remote online opportunities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(3)(f): provide scholarships for individuals who live in rural areas to access online skill-based training for remote online opportunities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(3)(g): provide one-on-one coaching for an individual who pursues a remote online opportunity; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(3)(h): conduct other activities related to remote online opportunities as determined by Utah State University.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(4)(a): Utah State University shall administer the program:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(4)(a)(i): in at least one geographic area in the state initially; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(4)(a)(ii): in additional geographic areas if resources allow.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(4)(b): In determining where to initially administer the program, Utah State University shall consider whether counties in a geographic area:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(4)(b)(i): are primarily rural or have remote rural areas;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(4)(b)(ii): face high unemployment rates;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(4)(b)(iii): have access to high speed Internet;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(4)(b)(iv): have a large percentage of high school graduates leave the geographic area after graduating from high school; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(4)(b)(v): are members of an association of governments that supports helping individuals who live in rural areas access remote online opportunities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(5): On or before November 1, 2020, and on or before November 1 every third year thereafter, Utah State University shall report to the Economic Development and Workforce Services Interim Committee on:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(5)(a): the number of individuals who receive training through the program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(5)(b): the number and percentage of individuals who participate in the program and access a remote online opportunity; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1501(5)(c): whether there is a reduction in the unemployment rate in a geographic area included in the program.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1601 Definitions.
----------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1601(1): "Researcher" means an individual who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1601(1)(a): on May 8, 2018, is employed, alone or as part of a research team, by the university;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1601(1)(b): before May 8, 2018, received funding from USTAR for some or all of the researcher's startup costs or salary;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1601(1)(c): was recruited to become a member of the university's faculty; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1601(1)(d): after May 8, 2018, receives some or all of the researcher's start up costs or salary from a legislative appropriation to the university for that purpose.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1601(2): "University" means Utah State University.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1601(3): "USTAR" means the Utah Science Technology and Research Initiative, which was repealed in 2020.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602 Researcher reporting requirements.
--------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(1): On or before September 1 each year, the university shall submit a written report to the governor, the Legislature, and the Business, Economic Development, and Labor Appropriations Subcommittee.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2): (1) A report under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(a): the amount and sources of funding expended on a researcher's research program, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(a)(i): university funds and other state funds;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(a)(ii): legislative appropriations;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(a)(iii): federal funds;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(a)(iv): philanthropic or nonprofit funds; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(a)(v): industry funds;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(b): a copy of each:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(b)(i): technology disclosure that a researcher files with the university;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(b)(ii): license agreement that the university enters into with respect to a technology developed by a researcher, including any current, expired, or breached license; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(b)(iii): patent filed by the university based on technology developed by a researcher;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(c): publications in which a researcher participated, including a citation for each peer reviewed publication;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(d): the number of jobs maintained by a researcher's research program and average wages paid to those holding those jobs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(e): expenses paid by legislative appropriations for each researcher, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(e)(i): salary and benefits for a researcher or staff;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(e)(ii): operational expenses;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(e)(iii): capital equipment expenses; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(e)(iv): travel; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1602(2)(f): compensation, including salary and benefits, that a researcher received from a publicly funded source other than legislative appropriations under this part.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702 Creation of Food Security Council -- Members.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(1): There is created at Utah State University the Food Security Council.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2): The council is composed of the following 15 members:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(a): the executive director of the Department of Health and Human Services or the executive director's designee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(b): the executive director of the Department of Workforce Services or the executive director's designee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(c): the state superintendent or the state superintendent's designee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(d): the commissioner or the commissioner's designee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(e): the commissioner of the Department of Agriculture and Food or the commissioner's designee; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(f): the following members appointed by the chair of the council:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(f)(i): one member who represents the Utah State University Extension Service;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(f)(ii): one member who represents the Utah State University Expanded Food and Nutrition Education Program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(f)(iii): one member who represents the Utah Women, Infants, and Children Program administered under 42 U.S.C. Sec. 1786;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(f)(iv): one member who represents the Utah SNAP-Ed program;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(f)(v): one member who represents a food assistance organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(f)(vi): one member who represents an advocacy group that addresses federal nutrition programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(f)(vii): one member who represents an organization that promotes healthy eating and active lifestyles in the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(f)(viii): one member who represents an organization that provides refugee resettlement services in the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(f)(ix): one member who represents the Utah Farm Bureau Federation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(2)(f)(x): one member who represents a tribal government in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(3): (2)(d); (2)(d)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(3)(a): (2)(d) A member described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(3)(b): (2)(d) If a vacancy occurs for a member described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(3)(c): A member may serve more than one term.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(4): A member may not receive compensation or benefits for the member's service.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(5): The council shall elect a chair from the council's members, who shall serve a two-year term.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(6)(a): A majority of the members of the council constitutes a quorum of the council.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(6)(b): The action by a majority of the members of a quorum constitutes the action of the council.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1702(7): The Utah State University Hunger Solutions Institute shall provide staff support to the council.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1703(1): (2) The council shall:

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1802 Research enter -- Designation -- Duties.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1802(1): The ASPIRE Engineering Research Center at Utah State University is designated as the lead research center to coordinate and lead the initiative described in this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1802(2): The research center shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1802(2)(a): direct and carry out the mission of the initiative;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1802(2)(b): appoint a project director to oversee the initiative; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1802(2)(c): provide administrative and staff support to the steering committee and industry advisory board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1802(3): The project director shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1802(3)(a): oversee the operations of the initiative; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1802(3)(b): propose to the steering committee the expenditure of funds appropriated by the Legislature to carry out the duties under this part.

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-18-1803(2)(b): the executive director of the Department of Environmental Quality, or the executive director's designee;
