Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204 Funding request for capital development project -- Legislative approval -- Board prioritization, approval, and review.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(1): In accordance with this section, an institution is required to receive legislative approval in an appropriations act for a dedicated project or a nondedicated project.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(2): An institution shall submit to the board a proposal for a funding request for each dedicated project or nondedicated project for which the institution seeks legislative approval.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3): The board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(a): review each proposal submitted under Subsection (2) to ensure the proposal:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(a)(i): is cost effective and an efficient use of resources;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(a)(ii): is consistent with the institution's mission and master plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(a)(iii): fulfills a critical institutional facility need;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(b): based on the results of the board's review under Subsection (3)(a), create:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(b)(i): a list of approved dedicated projects; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(b)(ii): a list of approved nondedicated projects, prioritized in accordance with Subsection (5); and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(c): submit the lists described in Subsection (3)(b) to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(c)(i): the governor;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(c)(ii): the Infrastructure and General Government Appropriations Subcommittee;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(c)(iii): the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(c)(iv): the Division of Facilities Construction and Management for a:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(c)(iv)(A): recommendation, for the list described in Subsection (3)(b)(i); or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(3)(c)(iv)(B): recommendation and prioritization, for the list described in Subsection (3)(b)(ii).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(4): 63A-5b-403; 63A-5b-403 A dedicated project:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(4)(a): 63A-5b-403 is subject to the recommendation of the Division of Facilities Construction and Management as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(4)(b): 63A-5b-403 is not subject to the prioritization of the Division of Facilities Construction and Management as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(5)(a): Subject to Subsection (6), the board shall prioritize institution requests for funding for nondedicated projects based on:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(5)(a)(i): capital facility need;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(5)(a)(ii): utilization of facilities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(5)(a)(iii): maintenance and condition of facilities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(5)(a)(iv): any other factor determined by the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(5)(b): On or before August 1, 2019, the board shall establish how the board will prioritize institution requests for funding for nondedicated projects, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(5)(b)(i): how the board will measure each factor described in Subsection (5)(a); and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(5)(b)(ii): procedures for prioritizing requests.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(6)(a): Subject to Subsection (6)(b), and in accordance with Subsection (5), the board may annually prioritize:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(6)(a)(i): up to three nondedicated projects if the ongoing appropriation to the fund is less than $50,000,000;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(6)(a)(ii): up to two nondedicated projects if the ongoing appropriation to the fund is at least $50,000,000 but less than $100,000,000; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(6)(a)(iii): one nondedicated project if the ongoing appropriation to the fund is at least $100,000,000.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(6)(b): For each calendar year beginning on or after January 1, 2020, the dollar amounts described in Subsection (6)(a) shall be adjusted by an amount equal to the percentage difference between:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(6)(b)(i): the Consumer Price Index for the 2019 calendar year; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(6)(b)(ii): the Consumer Price Index for the previous calendar year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(7): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(7)(a): An institution may request operations and maintenance funds for a capital development project approved under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(7)(b): An institution shall make the request described in Subsection (7)(a) at the same time the institution submits the proposal described in Subsection (2).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(7)(c): The Legislature shall consider an institution's request described in Subsection (7)(a).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-22-204(8): After an institution completes a capital development project described in this section, the board shall review the capital development project, including the costs and design of the capital development project.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 23 - Instructional Materials for Students with a Disability Act
*********************************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-101 Title.
---------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Instructional Materials for Students with a Disability Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
For purposes of this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(1): 53B-23-103; 53B-23-106
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(1)(a): 53B-23-103; 53B-23-106 "Instructional material or materials" means textbooks and other materials written and published primarily for use by students in postsecondary instruction that are required or essential to a student's success in a course of study in which a student with a disability is enrolled.  The determination of which materials are "required or essential to student success" shall be made by the instructor of the course in consultation with the official making the request pursuant to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(1)(b): "Instructional material or materials" does not include nontextual mathematics and science materials until the time software becomes commercially available that permits the conversion of existing electronic files of the materials into a format that is compatible with braille translation software or alternative media for students with disabilities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(2): "Printed instructional material or materials" means instructional material or materials in book or other printed form.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(3): "Nonprinted instructional materials" means instructional materials in formats other than print, and includes instructional materials that require the availability of electronic equipment in order to be used as a learning resource, including software programs, video disks, and video and audio tapes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(4): 53B-2-101 "State institution of higher education" means an institution listed in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(5): "Specialized format" means braille, audio, or digital text that is exclusively for use by blind or other persons with disabilities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(6)(a): "Structural integrity" means all of the printed instructional material, including the text of the material, sidebars, the table of contents, chapter headings and subheadings, footnotes, indexes, glossaries, and bibliographies.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-102(6)(b): "Structural integrity" need not include nontextual elements such as pictures, illustrations, graphs, or charts.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103 Instructional materials to be provided in electronic format.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1): (1)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1)(a): On or after January 1, 2009, any person that publishes or manufactures printed instructional material for students attending a state institution of higher education shall provide to the institution for use by students attending the institution any printed instructional material in an electronic format mutually agreed upon by the publisher or manufacturer and the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1)(b): Computer files or electronic versions of the printed instructional material shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1)(b)(i): maintain the structural integrity of the printed instructional material;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1)(b)(ii): be compatible with commonly used braille translation and speech synthesis software; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1)(b)(iii): include corrections and revisions as may be necessary.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(1)(c): (1)(a) If good faith efforts fail to produce an agreement pursuant to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(2): The computer files or electronic versions of the printed instructional material shall be provided to the institution at no additional cost and in a timely manner, upon receipt of a written request that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(2)(a): certifies that the institution has purchased the printed instructional material for use by a student with a disability or that a student with a disability attending or registered to attend that institution has purchased the printed instructional material;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(2)(b): certifies that the student has a disability that prevents the student from using standard instructional materials;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(2)(c): certifies that the printed instructional material is for use by the student in connection with a course in which the student is registered or enrolled at the institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(2)(d): is signed by the coordinator of services for students with disabilities at the institution or by the official responsible for monitoring compliance with the Americans with Disabilities Act of 1990, 42 U.S.C. 12101 et seq. at the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(3): (2)(a); (2)(d) A publisher or manufacturer providing instructional materials in an electronic format to an institution may require that, in addition to the requirements specified in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(3)(a): the student will use the electronic copy of the printed instructional material in specialized format solely for the student's own educational purposes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(3)(b): the student will not copy or duplicate the printed instructional material for use by others.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(4): If an institution permits a student to directly use the electronic version of an instructional material, the disk or file shall be copy-protected or the institution shall take other reasonable precautions to ensure that the student does not copy or distribute electronic versions of instructional materials in violation of the Copyright Revisions Act of 1976, 17 U.S.C. Sec. 101 et seq.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(5): (1); (2) A person that publishes or manufactures nonprinted instructional materials for students attending a state institution of higher education shall provide computer files or other electronic versions of the nonprinted instructional materials for use by students attending the institution subject to the same requirements specified in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-103(6): Nothing in this chapter shall be construed to prohibit an institution from assisting a student with a disability by using the electronic version of printed instructional material provided pursuant to this section solely to transcribe or arrange for the transcription of the printed instructional materials into braille.  If a transcription is made, the institution shall have the right to share the braille copy of the printed instructional material with other students with disabilities.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-104 Centers for processing requests for electronic versions of instructional materials.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-104(1): The board may establish one or more centers to process requests for electronic versions of instructional materials pursuant to this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-104(2): The institutions designated as within the jurisdiction of a center shall submit requests for instructional material to the center, which shall transmit the request to the publisher or manufacturer.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-104(3): If there is more than one center, each center shall make every effort to coordinate requests.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-104(4): The publisher or manufacturer of instructional material shall be required to honor and respond to only those requests submitted through a designated center.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-104(5): If a publisher or manufacturer has responded to a request for instructional materials by a center, all subsequent requests for those instructional materials shall be satisfied by the center to which the request is made.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-105 Infringement of copyright laws not authorized.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Nothing in this chapter shall be considered to authorize any use of instructional materials that would constitute an infringement of copyright under the Copyright Revision Act of 1976, as amended, 17 U.S.C. Sec. 101 et seq.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-106 Institution to make policy.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-106(1): 53B-1-102 As used in this section, "institution" means an institution listed in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-106(2): 53B-23-103; 53B-23-102; 53B-23-103 An institution shall make policy consistent with this section for the implementation and administration of the institution, including policy addressing:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-106(2)(a): the designation of materials considered "required or essential to student success";
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-106(2)(b): 53B-23-103; 53B-23-102 the determination of the availability of technology for the conversion of nonprinted materials pursuant to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-23-106(2)(c): 53B-23-103 the procedures and standards relating to distribution of files and materials pursuant to Section


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 25 - Internet Postsecondary Institution Privacy Act
*********************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-101 Title.
---------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Internet Postsecondary Institution Privacy Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-102 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-102(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-102(1)(a): "Personal Internet account" means an online account that is used by a student or prospective student exclusively for personal communications unrelated to any purpose of the postsecondary institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-102(1)(b): "Personal Internet account" does not include an account created, maintained, used, or accessed by a student or prospective student for education related communications or for an educational purpose of the postsecondary institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-102(2): "Postsecondary institution" means an institution that provides educational services offered primarily to persons who have completed or terminated their secondary or high school education or who are beyond the age of compulsory school attendance.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-201 Prohibited activities.
-------------------------------------------------------
A postsecondary institution may not do any of the following:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-201(1): request a student or prospective student to disclose a username and password, or a password that allows access to the student's or prospective student's personal Internet account; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-201(2): (1) expel, discipline, fail to admit, or otherwise penalize a student or prospective student for failure to disclose information specified in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-202 Permitted activities.
------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-202(1): This chapter does not prohibit a postsecondary institution from requesting or requiring a student to disclose a username or password to gain access to or operate the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-202(1)(a): an electronic communications device supplied by or paid for in whole or in part by the postsecondary institution; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-202(1)(b): an account or service provided by the postsecondary institution that is either obtained by virtue of the student's admission to the postsecondary institution or used by the student for educational purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-202(2): 53B-25-201(1) This chapter does not prohibit or restrict a postsecondary institution from viewing, accessing, or using information about a student or prospective student that can be obtained without the information described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-203 Duties not created.
----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-203(1): This chapter does not create a duty for a postsecondary institution to search or monitor the activity of a personal Internet account.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-203(2): A postsecondary institution is not liable under this chapter for failure to request or require that a student or prospective student grant access to, allow observation of, or disclose information that allows access to or observation of the student's or prospective student's personal Internet account.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-301 Private right of action.
---------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-301(1): A person aggrieved by a violation of this chapter may bring a civil cause of action against a postsecondary institution in a court of competent jurisdiction.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-25-301(2): (1) In an action brought under Subsection


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 27 - Campus Individual Rights Act
***************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-101 Title.
---------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-101(1): This chapter is known as the "Campus Individual Rights Act."
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-101(2): This part is known as "General Provisions."


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-102 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter, "institution" means an institution of higher education listed in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-201 Title.
---------------------------------------
This part is known as the "Campus Free Expression Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-202 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part, "expressive activity" includes:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-202(1): peacefully assembling, protesting, or speaking;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-202(2): distributing literature;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-202(3): carrying a sign; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-202(4): circulating a petition.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203 Expressive activities at an institution.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(1): An outdoor area of an institution's campus is a traditional public forum.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(2): An institution may maintain and enforce reasonable time, place, or manner restrictions on an expressive activity in an outdoor area of the institution's campus, if the restrictions:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(2)(a): are narrowly tailored to serve a significant institutional interest;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(2)(b): are based on published, content-neutral, and viewpoint-neutral criteria; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(2)(c): leave open ample alternative channels for communication.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(3): (2) Subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(3)(a): a member of the institution's community or the public from spontaneously and contemporaneously assembling in an outdoor area of the institution's campus; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(3)(b): a person from freely engaging in noncommercial expressive activity in an outdoor area of the institution's campus if the person's conduct is lawful.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-203(4): This part does not apply to expressive activity in an area on an institution's campus other than an outdoor area.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204 Cause of action.
-------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(1): The following persons may bring an action in a state court of competent jurisdiction to enjoin a violation of this part or to recover compensatory damages, reasonable court costs, or reasonable attorney fees:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(1)(a): the attorney general; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(1)(b): a person claiming that the person's expressive rights, as described in this part, were violated.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2): In an action brought under this part, if the court finds a violation of this part, the court:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(a): shall enjoin the violation;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(b): shall, if a person whose expressive rights were violated brought the action, award the person:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(b)(i): at least $500 for an initial violation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(b)(ii): if the person notifies the institution of the violation, $50 for each day the violation continues after the notification; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(c): may award a prevailing plaintiff:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(c)(i): compensatory damages;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(c)(ii): reasonable court costs; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(2)(c)(iii): reasonable attorney fees.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-204(3): Title 63G, Chapter 7, Governmental Immunity Act of Utah Notwithstanding


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-205 Statute of limitations.
--------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-205(1): (3) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-205(2): Each day that a violation continues after an initial violation, and each day that an institution's policy in violation of this part remains in effect, shall constitute a continuing violation of this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-205(3): (2); (1) For a continuing violation described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-301 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-301(1): "Civil liberty" means a civil liberty enumerated in the United States Constitution or the Utah Constitution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-301(2): 63G-3-601 "Initiate rulemaking proceedings" means the same as that term is defined in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-302 Policies requiring rulemaking -- Policy review.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-302(1): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act An institution may not make or amend a policy that directly affects a student's civil liberty, unless the policy is made a rule in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-302(2): (2)(a) Each institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-302(2)(a): before November 30, 2018, review the institution's policies as of May 11, 2018, and identify any policy that directly affects a student's civil liberty; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-302(2)(b): (2)(a) before August 1, 2019, for each policy identified under Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303 Complaint process -- Reporting.
----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(1): Before August 1, 2019, the board shall make rules in accordance with Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act, establishing a procedure whereby a student enrolled in an institution may submit a complaint to the board alleging a policy of the institution directly affects one or more of the student's civil liberties.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(a): When a student submits a complaint in accordance with the rules adopted under Subsection (1), the board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(a)(i): examine the complaint and, within 30 days after the day on which the board receives the complaint, determine whether the complaint is made in good faith; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(a)(ii): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(a)(ii)(A): if the board determines that the complaint is made in good faith, direct the institution against which the complaint is made to initiate rulemaking proceedings for the challenged policy; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(a)(ii)(B): if the board determines that the complaint is made in bad faith, dismiss the complaint.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(b): Before November 30 of each year, the board shall submit a report to the Rules Review and General Oversight Committee detailing:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(b)(i): the number of complaints the board received during the preceding year;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(b)(ii): the number of complaints the board found to be made in good faith during the preceding year; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(2)(b)(iii): each policy that is the subject of a good-faith complaint that the board received during the preceding year.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-303(3): If the board directs an institution to initiate rulemaking proceedings for a challenged policy in accordance with this section, the institution shall initiate rulemaking proceedings for the policy within 60 days after the day on which the board directs the institution.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(1): "Discriminatory harassment" means student-on-student speech that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(1)(a): is unwelcome;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(1)(b): discriminates on the basis of a classification protected under federal or state law; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(1)(c): is so severe, pervasive, and objectively offensive, and that so undermines and distracts from a student's educational experience, that the student is effectively denied access to an institution's resource or opportunity.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(2): "Student" means an individual enrolled at an institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(3)(a): "Student-on-student speech" means verbal, written, or other communication that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(3)(a)(i): communicated by a student; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(3)(a)(ii): directed at another student.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-401(3)(b): "Student-on-student speech" does not include an act of physical contact between a student and another student.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402 Institution duties.
----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(1): An institution is in violation of this part if the institution:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(1)(a): gains actual knowledge of discriminatory harassment in the institution's program or activity; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(1)(b): acts with deliberate indifference to the discriminatory harassment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(2)(a): An institution may not sanction or discipline, as discriminatory harassment, student-on-student speech that does not constitute discriminatory harassment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(2)(b): An institution is not liable under this part for failing to sanction or discipline a student who communicates student-on-student speech that is not discriminatory harassment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(3): Nothing in this part prevents an institution from sanctioning or disciplining student-on-student speech that is otherwise not protected under the First Amendment to the United States Constitution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(4): Nothing in this part prevents an institution from responding to student-on-student speech that is not discriminatory harassment by taking nonpunitive actions designed to promote a welcoming, inclusive environment.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-402(5): Nothing in this part prevents an institution from maintaining policies prohibiting stalking or other criminal activity.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-403 Cause of action.
-------------------------------------------------
The attorney general may bring an action to enjoin a violation of this part, in a state court of competent jurisdiction, against an institution or an institution's agent acting in the agent's official capacity.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-404 Statute of limitations.
--------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-404(1): (3)(b) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-404(2): 53B-27-402(2)(a); 53B-27-402(2)(a) For an action alleging a violation of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-404(3): 53B-27-402(1); (3)(a); (1)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-404(3)(a): 53B-27-402(1) For an action alleging a violation of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-404(3)(b): (3)(a); (1) For an action described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405 Student religious accommodations.
------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(1): An institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(1)(a): reasonably accommodate a student's absence from an examination or other academic requirement under the circumstances described in Subsection (2) for reasons of:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(1)(a)(i): the student's faith or conscience; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(1)(a)(ii): the student's participation in an organized activity conducted under the auspices of the student's religious tradition or religious organization; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(1)(b): ensure that an accommodation described in Subsection (1)(a) does not adversely impact the student's academic opportunities.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(2): An institution shall make an accommodation described in Subsection (1) if:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(2)(a): the time at which an examination or academic requirement is scheduled to occur creates an undue hardship for a student due to the student's sincerely held religious belief; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(2)(b): the student provides a written notice to the instructor of the course for which the student seeks the accommodation regarding the date of the examination or academic requirement for which the student seeks the accommodation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(3): An institution shall establish policies related to the accommodation described in Subsection (1) that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(3)(a): require the institution to provide the accommodation with respect to when the student participates in examinations and other academic requirements;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(3)(b): allow an instructor who receives a notice described in Subsection (2)(b) to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(3)(b)(i): schedule an alternative examination time before or after the regularly scheduled examination; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(3)(b)(ii): make accommodations for other academic requirements related to the accommodation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(3)(c): require an instructor who receives a notice described in Subsection (2)(b) to keep confidential a student's request for the accommodation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(4)(a): The commissioner shall annually:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(4)(a)(i): create a list of the dates of religious holidays for the following two years; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(4)(a)(ii): distribute the list described in Subsection (4)(a) to an institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(4)(b): The creation and distribution of the list described in Subsection (4)(a) does not prohibit a student from seeking, or an institution from granting, an accommodation for a date of a religious holiday that is not included on that list.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(5): An institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(5)(a): designate a point of contact for information about an accommodation described in Subsection (1);
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(5)(b): establish a process by which a student may submit a grievance with regards to implementation of this section; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(5)(c): publish the following information on the institution's website and update the information annually:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(5)(c)(i): the institution's religious accommodation policies described in Subsection (3);
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(5)(c)(ii): the point of contact described in Subsection (5)(a);
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(5)(c)(iii): the list described in Subsection (4);
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(5)(c)(iv): a description of the general procedure to request an accommodation described in Subsection (1); and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-405(5)(c)(v): the grievance process described in Subsection (5)(b).


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501 Free expression policies.
----------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(1): As used in this section, "free expression policy" means an institution's policy, regulation, or other expectation related to student expression.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(2): An institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(2)(a): publish the institution's free expression policies:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(2)(a)(i): in the institution's student handbook; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(2)(a)(ii): on the institution's website;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(2)(b): include information about the institution's free expression policies in an orientation program for students enrolled in the institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(2)(c): develop a program, procedures, and materials to ensure that an individual who has responsibility for the discipline or education of a student at the institution understands the institution's free expression policies.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(3): (2)(c) An individual described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(3)(a): administrator;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(3)(b): campus police officer;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(3)(c): residence life official; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(3)(d): faculty member.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-501(4): An institution shall ensure that a free expression policy is consistent with the provisions of this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-601 Application.
---------------------------------------------
The provisions of this part do not:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-601(1): govern campus law enforcement departments or law enforcement personnel; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-601(2): otherwise replace or amend criminal procedures that govern law enforcement activities.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(1): "Academic dishonesty" means an act of dishonesty relating to a student's academic work or performance.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(2): "Accused student" means an individual enrolled in an institution who has allegedly violated a policy or rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(3): "Accused student organization" means a student organization, recognized by an institution, that has allegedly violated a policy or rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(4): "Alleged victim" means an individual whose rights are allegedly infringed or who is otherwise allegedly harmed by an accused student's or a student organization's violation of a policy or rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(5): "Evidence" means information that is inculpatory or exculpatory as the information relates to an accusation against an accused student or accused student organization, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(5)(a): a complainant statement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(5)(b): a third-party witness statement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(5)(c): electronically stored information;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(5)(d): a written communication;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(5)(e): a post to social media; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(5)(f): demonstrative evidence.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(6): "Full participation" means the opportunity in a student or student organization disciplinary proceeding to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(6)(a): make opening and closing statements;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(6)(b): examine and cross-examine a witness;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(6)(c): introduce relevant evidence; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(6)(d): provide support, guidance, or advice to an accused student, accused student organization, or alleged victim.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(7): "Legal representation" means an attorney, who is licensed to practice law in this state and whom:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(7)(a): an accused student selects to assist the student in the student's disciplinary proceeding;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(7)(b): an alleged victim selects to assist the alleged victim at a proceeding that pertains to the alleged victim; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(7)(c): an accused student organization selects to assist the student organization at a student organization disciplinary proceeding.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(8): "Nonattorney advocate" means an individual, who is not licensed to practice law and whom:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(8)(a): an accused student selects to assist the student in the student's disciplinary proceeding;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(8)(b): an alleged victim selects to assist the alleged victim at a proceeding that pertains to the alleged victim; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(8)(c): an accused student organization selects to assist the student organization at a student organization disciplinary proceeding.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(9): "Policy or rule" means a policy or rule, or a relevant section of a policy or rule, of an institution that, if violated, may result in:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(9)(a): for a student, a suspension of 10 calendar days or more or expulsion from the institution; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(9)(b): for a student organization, the suspension or the removal of institutional recognition of the student organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(10): "Proceeding" means an adjudicatory hearing, including an appeal, in which evidence is presented to a hearing officer or a hearing panel, and that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(10)(a): required by a policy or rule; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(10)(b): held to determine whether a policy or rule has been violated.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(11): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(11)(a): "Student disciplinary proceeding" means a proceeding initiated by an institution to determine whether an accused student has violated a policy or rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(11)(b): "Student disciplinary proceeding" does not include a proceeding that solely involves a student's academic dishonesty.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(12): "Student organization" means a club or other organization:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(12)(a): that meets during noninstructional time;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(12)(b): that is recognized by the institution at which the organization meets; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(12)(c): with a majority of members who are current students at the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(13): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(13)(a): "Student organization disciplinary proceeding" means a proceeding initiated by an institution to determine whether an accused student organization has violated a rule or policy.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-602(13)(b): "Student organization disciplinary proceeding" does not include a proceeding that solely involves a student's academic dishonesty.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603 Student disciplinary proceedings -- Legal representation.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(1): An institution may not prohibit:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(1)(a): an accused student from being represented, at the accused student's expense, by legal representation or a nonattorney advocate at a student disciplinary proceeding that pertains to the accused student; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(1)(b): an accused student's legal representation or nonattorney advocate from full participation in a student disciplinary proceeding that pertains to the accused student.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(2): An institution may not prohibit:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(2)(a): an alleged victim from being represented, at the alleged victim's expense, by legal representation or a nonattorney advocate at a student disciplinary proceeding that pertains to the alleged victim; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(2)(b): the alleged victim's legal representation or nonattorney advocate from full participation in a student disciplinary proceeding that pertains to the alleged victim.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(3)(a): An institution shall provide an accused student described in Subsection (1) or an alleged victim described in Subsection (2) written notice of the accused student's or alleged victim's rights under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(3)(b): The institution shall ensure that the notice provided to an accused student under Subsection (3)(a) notifies the accused student that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(3)(b)(i): the accused student is entitled to a student disciplinary proceeding to contest the charges against the accused student;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(3)(b)(ii): the accused student is entitled to a presumption of innocence; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(3)(b)(iii): the presumption of innocence remains until:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(3)(b)(iii)(A): the accused student acknowledges responsibility for the alleged violation; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(3)(b)(iii)(B): the institution has established every element of the alleged violation at a student disciplinary proceeding.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-603(3)(c): Unless exigent circumstances reasonably justify proceeding without providing notice under Subsection (3)(a), an institution shall establish policies and procedures to ensure that the institution provides written notice of the accused student's or alleged victim's rights as soon as practicable but no later than seven days before a student disciplinary proceeding that pertains to the accused student or alleged victim.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604 Student organization disciplinary proceedings -- Legal representation.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(1): An institution may not prohibit:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(1)(a): an accused student organization from being represented, at the accused student organization's expense, by legal representation or a nonattorney advocate at a student organization disciplinary proceeding that pertains to the accused student organization; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(1)(b): an accused student organization's legal representation or nonattorney advocate from full participation in a student organization disciplinary proceeding that pertains to the accused student organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(2): An institution may not prohibit:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(2)(a): an alleged victim from being represented, at the alleged victim's expense, by legal representation or a nonattorney advocate at a student organization disciplinary proceeding that pertains to the alleged victim; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(2)(b): the alleged victim's legal representation or nonattorney advocate from full participation in a student organization disciplinary proceeding that pertains to the alleged victim.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(3)(a): An institution shall provide an accused student organization described in Subsection (1) or an alleged victim described in Subsection (2) written notice of the accused student organization's or alleged victim's rights under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(3)(b): The institution shall ensure that the notice provided to an accused student organization under Subsection (3)(a) notifies the accused student organization that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(3)(b)(i): the accused student organization is entitled to a student organization disciplinary proceeding to contest the charges against the accused student organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(3)(b)(ii): the accused student organization is entitled to a presumption of innocence; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(3)(b)(iii): the presumption of innocence remains until:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(3)(b)(iii)(A): the accused student organization acknowledges responsibility for the alleged violation; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(3)(b)(iii)(B): the institution has established every element of the alleged violation at a student organization disciplinary proceeding.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-604(3)(c): Unless exigent circumstances reasonably justify proceeding without providing notice under Subsection (3)(a), an institution shall establish policies and procedures to ensure that the institution provides written notice of the accused student organization's or alleged victim's rights as soon as practicable but no later than seven days before a student organization disciplinary proceeding that pertains to the accused student organization or alleged victim.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-605 Exchange of evidence.
------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-605(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-605(1)(a): An institution shall ensure that an accused student, an alleged victim, or an accused student organization has access to all material evidence that is in the institution's possession, including both inculpatory and exculpatory evidence, unless the material is subject to a legal privilege, no later than one week before the day on which a proceeding begins.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-605(1)(b): Evidence that is an accused student's or an alleged victim's personal medical record, mental health record, therapy note, or journal may not be used as evidence in a proceeding unless the accused student or alleged victim consents to the use of the evidence in the proceeding.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-605(1)(c): Any evidence presented in a proceeding under this part is confidential and may not be:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-605(1)(c)(i): used as evidence in a subsequent proceeding; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-605(1)(c)(ii): used or disclosed to a third-party for any other purpose other than for the proceeding.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-605(2): Nothing in this part:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-605(2)(a): provides for formal or informal discovery beyond the exchange of evidence described in Subsection (1); or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-605(2)(b): incorporates or binds an institution to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-605(2)(b)(i): the Utah Rules of Civil Procedure or the Utah Rules of Evidence; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-605(2)(b)(ii): the Federal Rules of Civil Procedure or the Federal Rules of Evidence.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-606 Conflict of interest.
------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-606(1): An institution shall conduct a student disciplinary proceeding or student organization disciplinary proceeding in an impartial manner free from conflicts of interests.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-606(2): Except as provided in Subsection (3), in order to avoid conflicts of interest created by a comingling of roles, an institution shall prohibit an individual employed by or otherwise representing an institution from acting as an adjudicator, hearing officer, or appellate hearing officer in a student disciplinary proceeding or student organization disciplinary proceeding if the individual has also served in one of the following roles in the same matter:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-606(2)(a): an advocate or counselor for an alleged victim, accused student, or accused student organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-606(2)(b): an investigator;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-606(2)(c): an institutional prosecutor; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-606(2)(d): an advisor to a person described in Subsection (2)(a), (b), or (c).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-606(3): If an individual employed by the institution or otherwise representing the institution serves as an investigator and an institutional prosecutor for the alleged violation of a policy or rule, the institution shall advise an accused student, accused student organization, or alleged victim before the investigation proceeding.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-606(4): An individual may not serve as an investigator or institutional prosecutor and an advocate for an accused student, accused student organization, or alleged victim in the same matter.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-606(5): In a proceeding conducted under this part, an institution shall allow an accused student, accused student organization, or an alleged victim to raise objections to issues that could potentially compromise the impartiality of the proceedings, including any potential conflicts of interest in violation of this section.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-607 Application -- Institution policies.
---------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-607(1): This part does not prohibit an institution from temporarily suspending an accused student or accused student organization pending the completion of a student or student organization disciplinary proceeding.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-607(2): An institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-607(2)(a): enact policies to govern proceedings in which a student has a right to an active legal representation or a nonattorney advocate in accordance with this part;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-607(2)(b): train adjudicators, hearing officers, and appellate hearing officers on relevant evidence and nonrelevant, nonprobative evidence; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-607(2)(c): enact policies and procedures to notify a student of the student's right to bring a cause of action in violation of this part to the attorney general's office.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-607(3): An institution may adopt a policy requiring a legal representation or nonattorney advocate of an accused student, alleged victim, or accused student organization to submit questions for an opposing party to the hearing officer.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-608 Cause of action.
-------------------------------------------------
The attorney general may bring an action to enjoin a violation of this part, in a state court of competent jurisdiction, against an institution or an institution's agent acting in the agent's official capacity.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-609 Statute of limitations.
--------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-609(1): The attorney general may not bring an action under this part later than one year after the day on which the cause of action accrues.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-27-609(2): The cause of action accrues on the day on which the student or student organization receives final notice, from the institution, of sanction or discipline that violates an institution's rule or policy.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 28 - Student Rights and Responsibilities
**********************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-101 Title.
---------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "Student Rights and Responsibilities."

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-102 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter, "institution" means a public or private postsecondary institution that is located in Utah, including an institution of higher education listed in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(1): "Certified advocate" means an individual who:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(1)(a): is employed by or volunteers at a qualified institutional victim services provider;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(1)(b): has completed at least 40 hours of training in counseling and assisting victims of sexual harassment, sexual assault, rape, dating violence, domestic violence, or stalking; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(1)(c): acts under the supervision of the director or director's designee of a qualified institutional victim services provider.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2): (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(a): "Confidential communication" means information that is communicated by a victim, in the course of the victim seeking an institutional advocacy service, to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(a)(i): a certified advocate;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(a)(ii): a qualified institutional victim services provider;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(a)(iii): a person reasonably necessary for the transmission of the information;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(a)(iv): an individual who is present at the time the information is transmitted for the purpose of furthering the victim's interests; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(a)(v): another individual, in the context of group counseling at a qualified institutional victim services provider.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(2)(b): (2)(a) "Confidential communication" includes a record that is created or maintained as a result of the communication described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3): "Institutional advocacy service" means a safety planning, counseling, psychological, support, advocacy, medical, or legal service that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a): addresses issues involving:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a)(i): sexual harassment;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a)(ii): sexual assault;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a)(iii): rape;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a)(iv): domestic violence;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a)(v): dating violence; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(a)(vi): stalking; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(3)(b): is provided by a qualified institutional victim services provider.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(a): "Qualified institutional victim services provider" means an organization that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(a)(i): is affiliated with an institution;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(a)(ii): employs or provides volunteer opportunities for certified advocates;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(a)(iii): provides an institutional advocacy service to victims or families of victims; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(a)(iv): is designated by the affiliated institution as a qualified institutional victim services provider.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(b): "Qualified institutional victim services provider" may include an institution's:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(b)(i): sexual assault center;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(b)(ii): victim advocacy center;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(b)(iii): women's center;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(b)(iv): health center; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(4)(b)(v): counseling service center.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(5): "Record" means a book, letter, document, paper, map, plan, photograph, film, card, tape, recording, electronic data, or other documentary material regardless of physical form or characteristics.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-201(6): "Victim" means an individual who seeks an institutional advocacy service.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(1): "Alleged perpetrator" means an individual whom a victim alleges committed an act of sexual violence against the victim.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(2): "Code of conduct" means an institution's student code of conduct, student code of ethics, honor code, or other policy under which the institution may sanction a student.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(3): "Covered allegation" means an allegation made to an institution that an individual committed an act of sexual violence.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(4): "Law enforcement agency" means an off-campus law enforcement agency of the unit of local government with jurisdiction to respond to a covered allegation.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5): "Sexual violence" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(a): sexual abuse as described in 18 U.S.C. Sec. 2242;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(b): aggravated sexual abuse as described in 18 U.S.C. Sec. 2241;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(c): assault resulting in substantial bodily injury as described in 18 U.S.C. Sec. 113(a)(7);
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(d): sexual assault;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(e): dating violence;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(f): domestic violence; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(5)(g): stalking.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(6): "Student" means an individual enrolled in an institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-301(7): "Victim" means a student who alleges that the student was a victim of sexual violence.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-302 Code of conduct violation -- Report of sexual violence.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
An institution may not sanction a student for a code of conduct violation related to the use of drugs or alcohol if:Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-302(1): the student is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-302(1)(a): a victim of an act of sexual violence; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-302(1)(b): a witness to an act of sexual violence;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-302(2): (1) the student reports to the institution, in good faith, a covered allegation related to the act of sexual violence described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-302(3): (2) the institution learns of the student's code of conduct violation due to the student's report described in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304 Criminal retaliation against a victim or a witness.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304(1)(a): 76-1-101.5 "Bodily injury" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304(1)(b): "Damage" means physical damage to an individual's property.

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304(2)(a): upon a victim of or a witness to an act of sexual violence alleged in a covered allegation; and

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-304(3)(a)(ii)(A): report of the covered allegation; or

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401 Campus safety plans and training -- Institution duties -- Governing board duties.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(1): 53B-1-102 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(1)(a): "Covered offense" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(1)(a)(i): sexual assault;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(1)(a)(ii): domestic violence;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(1)(a)(iii): dating violence; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(1)(a)(iv): stalking.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(1)(b): 53B-1-102 "Institution" means an institution of higher education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(1)(c): "Student organization" means a club, group, sports team, fraternity or sorority, or other organization:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(1)(c)(i): of which the majority of members is composed of students enrolled in an institution; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(1)(c)(ii): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(1)(c)(ii)(A): that is officially recognized by the institution; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(1)(c)(ii)(B): seeks to be officially recognized by the institution.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(2): An institution shall develop a campus safety plan that addresses:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(2)(a): where an individual can locate the institution's policies and publications related to a covered offense;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(2)(b): institution and community resources for a victim of a covered offense;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(2)(c): the rights of a victim of a covered offense, including the measures the institution takes to ensure, unless otherwise provided by law, victim confidentiality throughout all steps in the reporting and response to a covered offense;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(2)(d): how the institution informs the campus community of a crime that presents a threat to the campus community;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(2)(e): availability, locations, and methods for requesting assistance of security personnel on the institution's campus;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(2)(f): guidance on how a student may contact law enforcement for incidents that occur off campus;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(2)(g): institution efforts related to increasing campus safety, including efforts related to the institution's increased response in providing services to victims of a covered offense, that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(2)(g)(i): the institution made in the preceding 18 months; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(2)(g)(ii): the institution expects to make in the upcoming 24 months;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(2)(h): coordination and communication between institution resources and organizations, including campus law enforcement;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(2)(i): institution coordination with local law enforcement or community resources, including coordination related to a student's safety at an off-campus location; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(2)(j): how the institution requires a student organization to provide the campus safety training as described in Subsection (5).
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(3): An institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(3)(a): prominently post the institution's campus safety plan on the institution's website and each of the institution's campuses; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(3)(b): annually update the institution's campus safety plan.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(4): An institution shall develop a campus safety training curriculum that addresses:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(4)(a): awareness and prevention of covered offenses, including information on institution and community resources for a victim of a covered offense;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(4)(b): bystander intervention; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(4)(c): sexual consent.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(5): An institution shall require a student organization, in order for the student organization to receive or maintain official recognition by the institution, to annually provide campus safety training, using the curriculum described in Subsection (4), to the student organization's members.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-401(6): 53B-28-403 An institution shall report annually to the Education Interim Committee and the Law Enforcement and Criminal Justice Interim Committee, at or before the committees' November meetings, on crime statistics aggregated by housing facility as described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403 Student housing crime reporting.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1): 53B-2-101; (1)(d)(i); 53B-28-401 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(a): "Campus law enforcement" means an institution's police department.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(b): "Crime statistics" means the number of each of the crimes in 34 C.F.R. Sec. 668.46(c)(1) that are reported to a local police agency or campus law enforcement, listed by type of crime.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(c): 53B-2-101 "Institution" means an institution of higher education described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(d): (1)(d)(i)
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(d)(i): "Institution noncampus housing facility" means a building or property that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(d)(i)(A): is used for housing students;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(d)(i)(B): is not part of the institution's campus; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(d)(i)(C): the institution owns, manages, controls, or leases;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(d)(ii): (1)(d)(i) "Institution noncampus housing facility" includes real property that is adjacent to, and is used in direct support of, the building or property described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(e): "Local law enforcement agency" means a state or local law enforcement agency other than campus law enforcement.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(f): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(f)(i): "On-campus housing facility" means a building or property that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(f)(i)(A): used for housing students; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(f)(i)(B): part of the institution's campus.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(f)(ii): "On-campus housing facility" includes real property that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(f)(ii)(A): adjacent to the on-campus housing facility; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(f)(ii)(B): used in direct support of the on-campus housing facility.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(g): "Student housing" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(g)(i): an institution noncampus housing facility;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(g)(ii): an on-campus housing facility; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(g)(iii): a student organization noncampus housing facility.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(h): 53B-28-401 "Student organization" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(i): "Student organization noncampus housing facility" means a building or property that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(i)(i): is used for housing students;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(i)(ii): is not part of the institution's campus; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(i)(iii): 
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(i)(iii)(A): a student organization owns, manages, controls, or leases; or
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(1)(i)(iii)(B): is real property that is adjacent to the student organization noncampus housing facility and is used in direct support of the noncampus housing facility.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(2): (2)(a); 53B-28-401(6) An institution shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(2)(a): create a report of crime statistics aggregated by:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(2)(a)(i): on-campus housing facility, identified and listed individually using the institution's system for inventorying institution facilities;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(2)(a)(ii): institution noncampus housing facility, identified and listed individually using the institution's system for inventorying institution facilities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(2)(a)(iii): student organization noncampus housing facilities, identified and listed individually using the institution's system for identifying student organization noncampus housing facilities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(2)(b): (2)(a); 53B-28-401(6) include the report described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-28-403(3): Upon request from an institution, a local law enforcement agency shall provide to the institution crime statistics for each student housing facility over which the local law enforcement agency has jurisdiction.
