Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202 Council duties -- Reporting.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1): The council shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(a): coordinate, facilitate, and support higher education delivered in the state's correctional facilities, including the county jails under contract with the Department of Corrections to house inmates, to prepare incarcerated individuals for integration and productive employment upon release;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b): explore and provide recommendations to the board and the Department of Corrections for the efficient and effective delivery of higher education programs to incarcerated individuals, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(i): evidence-based practices and technologies;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(ii): methods of maximizing and facilitating incarcerated individuals' access to educational programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(iii): methods of supporting and facilitating timely completion of courses, certificates, and degrees;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(iv): methods of emphasizing educational programs that:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(iv)(A): align with current and future workforce demands of the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(iv)(B): lead to occupations that are accessible to released incarcerated individuals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(iv)(C): provide sustainable wages following release; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(iv)(D): maximize accessibility and timely completion during incarceration;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(v): use of cross-institutional application of coursework toward certificates and degrees;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(vi): use of coursework that encourages personal and civic development; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(b)(vii): methods of leveraging innovative course delivery, including technology resources;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(c): explore methods and make recommendations for the collection and analysis of critical data regarding:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(c)(i): enrollment and completion of postsecondary education courses, certificate programs, credentials, and degree programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(c)(ii): federal and state student aid awarded to incarcerated individuals;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(c)(iii): costs of postsecondary education in prison, including any recommendations for continued improvement; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(c)(iv): outcomes of formerly incarcerated individuals who participated in postsecondary programming during incarceration if the individual is under the supervision of the Department of Corrections, including recidivism, employment, and post-release postsecondary education engagement; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(1)(d): recommend requests for legislative appropriations to the board to support the purposes and objectives of the council.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(2): The council shall annually report regarding the council's plans and programs, the number of enrollees served, and the number of enrollees receiving degrees and certificates to:
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(2)(a): the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(2)(b): before the committee's November interim committee meeting, the Education Interim Committee; and
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-202(2)(c): at least 30 days before the beginning of the annual legislative session, the Higher Education Appropriations Subcommittee.


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-301 Higher education student advisors.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-301(1): A degree-granting institution of higher education providing education to inmates in a correctional facility shall provide relevant academic and career advising services that are substantially similar to services provided to a student who is not a confined or incarcerated individual.
Utah Code Annotated § 53B-35-301(2): Each participating institution of higher education described in Subsection (1) shall report annually to the council regarding the guidance and support provided.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 53B - Chapter 36 - Southern Utah University
***********************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 53B-36-101 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------


Utah Code Annotated § 53B-36-201 Helen Foster Snow Cultural Center.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Subject to legislative appropriations, Southern Utah University shall establish the Helen Foster Snow Cultural Center to provide language support and cultural opportunities to students studying the Mandarin Chinese language.
